## Meow Mobile

### Product Offering

#### Meow Mobile Plan - 3 months for $15/month
*Article ID: 46627089482779 | Updated: 2026-02-13*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46627089482779-Meow-Mobile-Plan-3-months-for-15-month*

The pricing structure has changed from the previous $50/month + taxes model. The new structure reduces the effective monthly base rate after the initial 3-month period.

All plan benefits remain unchanged:

- Unlimited talk
- Unlimited text
- Unlimited data
- 24/7 vet care access
## **How the Offer Works**### **1. Initial Purchase ‚Äì Covers First 3 Months**At checkout, customers make one upfront payment that covers the first 3 full months of service (Months 1‚Äì3).

This is not a monthly charge. It is a single charge covering the entire 3-month period.

### **Cost Breakdown for Months 1‚Äì3**
- Base Plan: $45.00 (covers all 3 months)
- Vet Service Fee: Waived for the first 3 months
- Recovery Fee: $6.00 ($2 √ó 3 months)
- Taxes: Vary depending on jurisdiction
**Total at Checkout:**
$51.00 + applicable taxes

This equals $15/month (before taxes) for the first 3 months.

There are no additional charges during Months 1‚Äì3, as they are fully covered by the upfront payment.

### **System Indicator**In the billing payload, the system reflects:

- recurringChargePeriodLength: 3This confirms that the initial charge covers a 3-month billing period.

The upfront charge includes:

- Data
- Voice
- SMS
- Included/zero-rated fees for the full 3-month period
## **Automatic Transition After 3 Months**Starting in Month 4, billing automatically transitions to a standard monthly cycle.

### **Month 4 and Beyond ‚Äì Monthly Charges**
- Base Plan: $30.00
- Vet Service Fee: $2.00
- Recovery Fee: $2.00
- Taxes: Vary by jurisdiction
**Total Monthly Charge from Month 4:**
$34.00 + applicable taxes

This replaces the previous $50/month + taxes pricing model.

Standard recurring billing applies from this point forward.

## **Customer Billing Timeline**### **Month 0 ‚Äì Purchase Date**
- Customer pays one upfront charge covering 3 full months.
- The plan activates immediately.
- The ‚ÄúNext Billing Date‚Äù should display purchase date + 3 months.
### **Months 1‚Äì3**
- No additional charges are applied.
- Service remains active.
- These months are fully covered by the initial upfront payment.
- Notifications should reflect that billing resumes after the 3-month period.
### **Month 4 and Onward**
- Monthly billing resumes.
- Customer is charged:
$30 base plan
- $2 Vet Service Fee
- $2 Recovery Feeapplicable taxes

- Standard monthly billing cycle continues.
## **Known Issue ‚Äì Next Billing Date Display**There is a known display/notification issue affecting some accounts.

In certain cases, the ‚ÄúNext Billing Date‚Äù may incorrectly show the following month after purchase.

Important clarification:

- This is only a visual or notification bug.
- The system billing logic is correct.
- Customers are not charged early.
- The actual charge occurs after the full 3-month period.
If customers raise concerns about the displayed date, reassure them that their billing is accurate and aligned with the 3-month prepaid structure.

## **Summary for Support Reference**
- First 3 months are paid upfront in a single charge.
- Total upfront: $51.00 + taxes.
- No charges during Months 1‚Äì3.
- Month 4 billing resumes at $34.00 + taxes per month.
- Benefits remain unchanged.
- Any early ‚ÄúNext Billing Date‚Äù shown is a display issue only.

#### Super Secret Club
*Article ID: 44556507620507 | Updated: 2025-12-18*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44556507620507-Super-Secret-Club*

# **[Hairy Meow.png]Meow Mobile Super Secret Club**## **Overview**The **Meow Mobile Super Secret Club** is a private group of approximately 100 early supporters who have been granted **lifetime free Meow Mobile mobile service**.

This program exists to:

- Reward early trust in Meow Mobile
- Gather high-quality, real-world feedback
- Build a direct, human relationship between our team and our earliest users
Members of the Super Secret Club are part of a special early cohort and are not enrolled through any public promotion.

## **What members receive**Members of the Meow Mobile Super Secret Club receive:

- **Lifetime free Meow Mobile mobile service**
- **$0 cost ‚Äî including all taxes, fees, and surcharges**
- Access to the Meow Mobile plan **as it exists today**

- Certain additional benefits and features that are **currently included at no cost**

- A direct feedback channel with the Meow Mobile team
- Early visibility into updates and changes when applicable
As long as the member‚Äôs line remains active and in good standing, **they will never be billed** for the included mobile service.

## **What ‚Äúlifetime free‚Äù means (important)**
- ‚ÄúLifetime‚Äù means for as long as the **original recipient** keeps their Meow Mobile service continuously active
- The benefit is **personal, one-time, and non-transferable**

- If a member cancels, ports out, suspends service (outside of Meow Mobile-approved temporary suspensions), or otherwise leaves Meow Mobile, the lifetime benefit ends permanently and cannot be reinstated
- The offer has no cash value and cannot be exchanged, refunded, or resold
## **What is included at no cost**The lifetime free benefit covers:

- The **Meow Mobile mobile service subscription as it exists today**

- All required **taxes, fees, and surcharges**, fully covered by Meow Mobile
Members will pay **absolutely nothing** for the included mobile service.

## **Ancillary and third-party services (important)**Some features included with Meow Mobile today (for example, veterinary telehealth) are provided by third-party partners.

- These services are **currently included at no cost** for members of the Meow Mobile Super Secret Club
- Unlike the mobile service itself, **we do not guarantee these services will remain the same or be included forever**

- Partners, features, or benefits may change over time as we improve the experience or operate the business responsibly
- We may replace existing services or introduce new benefits that enhance or augment the overall experience
- Any changes to ancillary or third-party services **do not affect the lifetime free mobile service subscription**

The lifetime guarantee applies **only** to the Meow Mobile mobile service.

## **What is *****not***** included (now and in the future)**The lifetime free benefit does **not** include:

- International usage or roaming
- Premium features, add-ons, or optional third-party services
- Future products that increase or extend high-speed data usage
In the future, Meow Mobile may offer optional products that allow users to:

- Increase high-speed data after exceeding current thresholds
More than **50GB of personal data**, or
- More than **10GB of hotspot usage**

If introduced, these products **will not be included** as part of the lifetime free benefit.

## **Important clarification (current state)**At this time:

- Meow Mobile does **not** support international usage or roaming
- No paid add-ons or data extension products are available
As a result, **there is currently no way for Super Secret Club members to incur additional charges**.

Any future optional products would:

- Be clearly communicated
- Require explicit user opt-in
- Never affect the lifetime free mobile service itself
## **Community space**Members of the Meow Mobile Super Secret Club are invited to a **private Facebook Group** created exclusively for this cohort.

The group is used for:

- Sharing feedback and experiences
- Flagging issues or questions
- Receiving updates from the Meow Mobile team
- Light community interaction with other early members
This space is for feedback and collaboration and is **not a formal customer support channel**, though the team actively monitors and responds.

## **How the Meow Mobile team uses the group**
- The team regularly reviews posts and comments
- Feedback is shared internally with product, operations, and network teams
- Responses are written by real team members, not automated systems
- Internal coordination may happen in Slack, but replies are always made directly to members in the Facebook Group
## **Expectations for members**Members are expected to:

- Provide honest and respectful feedback
- Understand that Meow Mobile is early and evolving
- Avoid sharing sensitive personal information publicly
- Use the community constructively
Fraud, abuse, or misuse of service may result in removal from the Super Secret Club and forfeiture of the lifetime benefit.

## **Expectations to set clearly (for team & AI)**
- There are **no guaranteed response times**

- Feedback does **not guarantee product changes**

- The Super Secret Club does **not override** Meow Mobile‚Äôs Terms & Conditions
- Network coverage, speeds, and performance may vary by location and device
## **Common questions & answers****Q: Will I ever be charged anything?**
A: No. Your Meow Mobile mobile service, including all taxes and fees, is fully covered as long as your service remains active and eligible.

**Q: Is veterinary telehealth included for life?**
A: Veterinary telehealth is currently included at no cost, but it is not guaranteed to remain the same or included forever. The lifetime guarantee applies only to the mobile service.

**Q: Are international or roaming charges included?**
A: No. International and roaming are not currently supported. If launched in the future, they will not be included.

**Q: Are future high-speed data add-ons included?**
A: No. If optional data extension products are introduced later, they will not be included.

**Q: Can I leave and rejoin later?**
A: No. If you leave Meow Mobile, the lifetime benefit ends permanently.

## **AI-safe short summary**The Meow Mobile Super Secret Club is a private group of early members who receive lifetime free Meow Mobile mobile service with all taxes and fees covered. Some additional features are currently included at no cost but may change over time. The lifetime guarantee applies only to the mobile service itself.

#### Offers & Services
*Article ID: 42175975142427 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42175975142427-Offers-Services*

Meow Mobile is a prepaid, eSIM-only mobile service designed for pet parents! For $50/month, you get unlimited talk, text, and data, plus 24/7 access to licensed vets through the Airvet app. It's simple, contract-free, and works on most unlocked, eSIM-compatible phones.¬†

The fair use limit is 50GB of high-speed data per billing cycle. After you hit 50GB, your data stays unlimited but slows to 128 kbps. That slower speed lasts until your next plan renewal date.¬†

Unlike regular mobile providers, Meow Mobile is built for cat parents. Unlimited talk, text, and data plus round‚Äëthe‚Äëclock vet care through Airvet. The perfect blend of staying connected and caring for your kitty ‚Äî all in one plan.

### TELCO

#### TELCO Abbreviations
*Article ID: 44516740266395 | Updated: 2025-12-18*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516740266395-TELCO-Abbreviations*

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Core Identifiers (VERY IMPORTANT)**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**IMEI **(International Mobile Equipment Identity)
Unique ID of the phone/device
- Used to check compatibility, blacklist stolen phones

- 
**IMEI2**Second IMEI for dual-SIM phones

- 
**ICCID **(Integrated Circuit Card ID)
Unique ID of the SIM or eSIM
- Used to activate and manage SIM profiles

- 
**EID **(eSIM Identifier)
Unique ID of the eSIM chip inside the phone
- Required for eSIM activation

- 
**MSISDN**Your phone number (the number people dial)

- 
**IMSI **(International Mobile Subscriber Identity)
Internal network ID tied to the subscriber
- Used by the carrier for authentication

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Network & Technology Basics**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Carrier / MNO** (Mobile Network Operator)Owns the network (AT&T, Verizon, T-Mobile)

- 
**MVNO **(Mobile Virtual Network Operator)Uses another carrier‚Äôs network (ex: Meow Mobile)

- 
**Core Network**Backend system handling calls, data, SMS, billing

- 
**Radio Access Network (RAN)**Towers that connect phones to the network

- 
**LTE (4G)**Long Term Evolution, standard 4G network

- 
**5G**Faster data, lower latency network

- 
**NSA 5G**5G using 4G core (most common)

- 
**SA 5G**Pure 5G core (newer, faster)

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Coverage & Signal Terms**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Signal Bars**Visual indicator of network strength

- 
**Roaming**Using another network outside home coverage

- 
**Domestic Roaming**Using a partner US network

- 
**International Roaming**Using networks outside the US

- 
**No Service**Device cannot connect to any tower

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **SIM & eSIM Concepts**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**eSIM**
Digital SIM built into phone
- Activated via QR code or manual entry

- 
**eSIM Profile**Downloaded carrier configuration

- 
**QR Code Activation**Scans to install eSIM profile

- 
**Manual Activation**Enter SM-DP+ address + activation code

- 
**Dual SIM**Two active lines (SIM + eSIM or eSIM + eSIM)

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Number Management**

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Port-In**Moving number from old carrier to new carrier

- 
**Port-Out**Moving number away from current carrier

- 
**Account Number**Needed for porting (from old carrier)

- 
**Port-Out PIN**Security PIN required to transfer number

- 
**LNP (Local Number Portability)**System that allows number transfers

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Voice, SMS & Data**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Unlimited Data**No fixed data cap (may slow after threshold)

- 
**Data Throttling**Reduced speed after high usage

- 
**Deprioritization**Lower priority during congestion

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Device Compatibility**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Unlocked Device**Can be used on any carrier

- 
**Locked Device**Restricted to one carrier

- 
**Band Compatibility**Phone must support carrier‚Äôs LTE/5G bands

- 
**Whitelist**Approved device list for network

- 
**Blacklist**Blocked devices (lost, stolen, unpaid)

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Billing & Plans**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Prepaid**Pay before usage (most MVNOs)

- 
**Postpaid**Pay after usage

- 
**Autopay**Automatic monthly payment

- 
**Billing Cycle**Monthly plan period

- 
**Renewal Date**Date plan resets

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Support & Ops Terms**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Provisioning**Setting up services on the network

- 
**Activation**Turning the line live

- 
**Suspension**Temporarily disabling service

- 
**Termination**Permanent cancellation

- 
**Line**One phone number/service

- 
**Account**Customer profile holding one or more lines

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Network Issues**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**Outage**Network not working in an area

- 
**Intermittent Service**On-and-off connectivity

- 
**APN (Access Point Name) - ‚Äúereseller‚Äù**Network settings for data

- 
**Reset Network Settings**Fixes many data/call issues

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Security & Compliance**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**2FA**Two-factor authentication for account access

- 
**SIM Swap**Moving number to another SIM (fraud risk)

- 
**CPNI - Customer Proprietary Network Information¬†**Customer data protection rules (US)

‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

## **Regulatory (US-Specific)**‚Äî--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

- 
**FCC**Regulates US telecom

- 
**911 / E911**Emergency calling & location services

- 
**KYC**Identity verification (limited for prepaid)

### Chat Flow

#### Chat Flow
*Article ID: 44612761830939 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44612761830939-Chat-Flow*

**Chat Flow**

**Greeting/Open-****(within 10 seconds)**

Hello Cxx! Thank you so much for contacting Meow-Mobile! I hope you are doing well today. I'm your Cat Squad member, Santosh, ready to pounce into action for you today.¬†

¬†

**Verify the concern- ****(Identify the concern within 1 minute, or verify it with the customer within 2 minutes.)**

As I understand from the above bot chat that ( concern), am I correct?

**(If not mentioned concern above during the conversation with Bot)**

I‚Äôm sorry, I couldn‚Äôt fully understand your concern. Could you please share a few more details so I can assist you better? üêæ
¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† ¬† OR

Could you please share your concern so that I can assist you with it today?

¬†

**Apology - ****(Within 2 minutes)**

I sincerely apologize for that (concern). But no worries, since you‚Äôve reached me on chat, I‚Äôll make sure this issue is resolved.

¬†

**Hold**** (Hold 2 minutes)**

Let me place you on a brief hold while I check the details for you. I hope that sounds good to you.

**UNHOLD**

I really appreciate your patience and the time you‚Äôve taken to wait.

¬†

**RESOLUTION ****(3 Minutes)**

**Example-¬† **I understand how important it is for you to stay connected, [Customer Name] üòä I‚Äôm truly sorry that your network isn‚Äôt working, but no worries, we‚Äôll get this sorted.

Please take a moment to follow these steps:¬† go to Settings ‚Üí Mobile Service ‚Üí Mobile Data Options ‚Üí Mobile Data Network üì± and check whether eReseller is selected.

There‚Äôs no rush at all, once you‚Äôve checked, just let me know. If anything looks different or you need help along the way, I‚Äôm right here to assist you üëç

¬†

**FURTHER ASSISTANT- ****(1 minute)**

Is there anything else apart from this, I would love to assist you today?

**CLOSING -**** (1 Minute)**

*It‚Äôs been my pleasure to assist you today. I‚Äôll go ahead and end the chat now. Thank you for chatting with me ‚Äî my name is Santosh. üò∫ If you need any help in the future, please remember that you can visit the Help Center on the Meow-Mobile App, or reach out to us via email or chat for any frequently asked questions or concerns. Have a great day, and keep your pets safe! üêæüê±*

### Customer Onboarding

#### Workflow
*Article ID: 42174785773339 | Updated: 2025-12-16*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42174785773339-Workflow*

**User Type**
**Workflow**

New User
Create Account ‚Üí Purchase Subscription ‚Üí Transfer Number (Optional) ‚Üí Activate eSIM ‚Üí Activate 24x7 vet care ‚Üí Home

FDT User*
Purchase Subscription ‚Üí Transfer Number (Optional) ‚Üí Activate eSIM ‚Üí Activate 24x7 vet care ‚Üí Home

*FDT User already has an account created
¬†

¬†

[Entire Customer Journey¬†](https://excalidraw.com/?name=Customer%20Journey#room=2cef0e28773f6579082f,XqwB2HGmJ5YfGxoMYBuPYw) ( Please do not make any changes in the specified link)

¬†

- **Create Account**
User can create an account or sign-in using Apple or Google sign-in only. No manual email based login is supported.

[InitialSignupimage.jpg]

¬†

- **Purchase Subscription**
Post account creation (new user) or sign-in (FDT user, when enabled for purchase post launch), will see the following screens to make a purchase

- We‚Äôll only have one plan auto applied for the user, i.e. the user doesn‚Äôt need to select the planPlan: Unlimited data, talk & text with 24x7 Vetcare at $X per month

- Zipcode is needed for internal purposes (e.g. tax calculation), hence we request user to enter it while also checking their network coverage at the provided location
- User can pay via 3 payment methods
iOS ‚Üí Apple Pay (default), Card and PayPal
- Android ‚Üí Google Pay (default), Card and PayPal

- Post purchase, user has to complete 3 steps before being taken to the home screen ‚Üí (1) Transfer Number (Port-in) ‚Üí Optional step; (2) Install & activate eSIM; (3) Activate non-telco benefit (24x7 Vetcare)

¬†

Note:

- There is no KYC to onboard user.
- User is by default onboarded on a new number. User has an option to transfer their number at the next step.
- User doesn‚Äôt have an option to select their new number (AT&T limitation).
- Payment is collected (i.e. customer‚Äôs account is debited) instantly when order is placed.
- User is by default enabled for auto-pay (30-day subscription renewal cycle).

[AccountSetup.jpg]

¬†

- **Transfer Number (Port-in)**
User is by default onboarded on a new number, and has an option to transfer their existing number at this step. User can also skip this step if needed.
¬†

Note:

- User needs a PIN from their existing carrier to initiate a transfer number (port-in) process.
- Transfer Number (Port-in) is near realtime, and could take up to few mins to complete ‚Üí According to our partner, it can take between 2-5 mins for most customers.

[PortingOverview.jpg]

¬†

- **Activate eSIM**
User will be able to install & activate eSIM with one click from the app.

[esimActivation.jpg]

¬†

- **Activate 24x7 Vetcare**
This is still WIP ‚Üí [delbert.ty@rockstar-automations.com](mailto:delbert.ty@rockstar-automations.com) can provide context once the journey & integration approach is finalized

[AirvetSetup.jpg]

### Customer Post-Onboarding

#### Workflow
*Article ID: 42174836986907 | Updated: 2025-12-02*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42174836986907-Workflow*

[Customer Journey](https://excalidraw.com/?name=Customer%20Journey#room=2cef0e28773f6579082f,XqwB2HGmJ5YfGxoMYBuPYw) (Please don't make any changes in the specified link)¬†

¬†

- **Home ‚Üí Cat Wellness**Since our core value proposition is anchored on non-telco benefit (cat wellness), the user has an option to search for anything related to cat wellness and more ‚Üí The search will fetch & synthesize relevant content from Reddit & display to the user. The user will have an option to ‚ÄúSave‚Äù or ‚ÄúShare‚Äù the result or talk to a vetcare if they have more queries. The user will also have a separate option to directly talk to the vet via video call or chat whenever needed

¬†

Note:

- This search will be the entry point for customer service chatbot as well ‚Üí Based on user query, we would redirect the user to search result or customer service chatbot.

¬†

- **Profile**Since the telco plan is Unlimited (data, talk & text), the core focus of customer journey is on non-telco benefit and experience.¬†

¬†

Note:

- [Deprioritised and will be available post launch] ‚Üí The user will be shown the ‚ÄúX‚Äù GB left banner (when data remaining is less than 5GB) and allowed to purchase additional high speed data.
- Manage Telco Plan ‚Üí User can manage key telco related actions in self-serve mode, rest will be managed via chatbot.
Manage Payments ‚Üí Change payment method.
- Payment History ‚Üí All purchases are shown here. Since we‚Äôre offering prepaid service, no bill is provided. Instead an invoice will be available to download for each payment made on our platform.
- Update Address ‚Üí In case the user decides to update their address later.
- Transfer Number (Port-out) ‚Üí User can view the PIN needed to transfer their number out from Meow Mobile to any other carrier.
- Terminate Account ‚Üí User can request to terminate their account.

### Customer Profile

#### How to Check Customer's Account if They Cannot Access it?
*Article ID: 42223257266203 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42223257266203-How-to-Check-Customer-s-Account-if-They-Cannot-Access-it*

Updated:

### Situation:Customers usually ask this question when:

- They‚Äôre unable to log in to their Meow Wireless account or app.

- Their registered email or Apple Private Relay email isn‚Äôt working.

- They‚Äôre not receiving the password reset link or access email.

- Their phone is lost, damaged, or they switched to a new device.

- They need help verifying their identity to recover access.

This may also occur after reinstalling the app, switching devices, or changing login credentials linked to Apple ID or another service.

### Task:The agent‚Äôs goal is to:

- Confirm the customer‚Äôs identity securely.

- Identify whether the login issue is related to credentials, device, or Apple Private Relay.

- Guide the customer through the correct recovery process.

- Escalate cases requiring identity verification or manual login reset.

### Steps for Agents:#### Check the account in ConnectX:
- Go to ConnectX ‚Üí Customer360.

- Search using the customer‚Äôs email address or phone number.

- 
Verify:

Account status (Active / Locked / Suspended)

- Last login attempt

- Linked email type (Private Relay or regular email)

- Any recent password reset or access recovery activity

#### Ask clarifying and verification questions:
- ‚ÄúCan you confirm the email you used to sign up with Meow Wireless?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you using an Apple Private Relay email (it usually looks like @privaterelay.appleid.com)?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúDid you try accessing your account through the Meow Wireless app or the website?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúIs your phone currently available, or do you need access from another device?‚Äù

These questions help identify whether the customer can log in through the app or needs identity verification via email.

### Action:#### If customer can still access their email (non-Private Relay):Example Response:

Thanks for confirming! In this case, we would suggest you to access meow mobile over the app and then simply log into your account using the registered email address that you used initially to get Meow mobile services. Make sure to check your inbox and spam folder for the reset link.
¬†

#### If customer is using an Apple Private Relay email:Example Response:
‚ÄúIf your account is linked to an Apple Private Relay email (usually ending in @privaterelay.appleid.com), we recommend logging in through the Meow Wireless app for quicker access. The app provides a secure and direct connection to your Apple-linked account.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm account linkage to Apple ID in ConnectX ‚Üí Account Details.

- Advise user to access through the app.

- Tag the ticket accordingly.

#### üî¥ If customer lost access to their device or app:Example Response:

We would suggest you to access meow mobile over the app on a new device and then simply log into your account using the registered email address that you used initially to get Meow mobile services. Make sure to check your inbox and spam folder for the reset link.

¬†

### Result:
- Customer successfully regains access to their Meow Wireless account.

- Apple Private Relay and app-based login issues are handled seamlessly.

- All verification and access recovery steps are documented in ConnectX.

- The customer feels reassured that their data and account are secure.

### Additional Notes:
- Always confirm the customer‚Äôs identity before making changes.

- Never send direct reset links ‚Äî direct users to official channels (email or app).

- If the customer fails identity verification, escalate to Account Security (Viru).

- Document all actions, including timestamps and verification results, in internal notes.

#### How to Update Customer Information in ConnectX?
*Article ID: 42223005974171 | Updated: 2025-11-10*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42223005974171-How-to-Update-Customer-Information-in-ConnectX*

Updated:

### Situation:Customers usually ask this question when:

- They notice incorrect details on their Meow Wireless account (e.g., name, email, phone number, or cat information).

- They recently changed their contact details and want to update them.

- Their account profile shows outdated information in the Meow Wireless app or portal.

- They are unable to edit some fields directly in the app and need agent assistance.

This may also come up when the customer is trying to ensure their shipping, billing, or pet information is accurate before activation or billing.

### Task:The agent‚Äôs goal is to:

- Verify the customer‚Äôs identity and confirm account ownership.

- Review and confirm which information needs updating.

- Update editable details in ConnectX or guide the customer on how to update it in-app.

- Escalate if the requested field cannot be edited manually (e.g., verified email, linked number).

### Steps for Agents:#### Access the customer record in ConnectX:
- Go to ConnectX ‚Üí Customer360.

- Search for the customer using their email address or phone number.

- Open their Profile tab to view current personal and pet details.

#### Verify ownership and identity:Before making any updates, confirm the customer‚Äôs identity by asking for:

- Registered email or phone number,

- Order ID or waitlist reference number (if applicable),

- Or confirm details such as last transaction or recent activity.

#### Review editable sections:Within the Customer360 view, check:

- Contact Information ‚Üí Name, Email, Phone number

- Address or billing information ‚Üí Home/shipping address (if applicable)

Editable fields will display an ‚ÄúEdit‚Äù or ‚ÄúUpdate‚Äù icon.

#### Ask clarifying questions to ensure accuracy:To confirm what needs to be updated and where:

- ‚ÄúWhich details would you like to update ‚Äî your name, contact number, or cat information?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúCan you confirm the correct spelling or updated details you‚Äôd like us to use?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúDid you already try updating your information through the app or portal?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you updating this for your main profile or your cat‚Äôs information?‚Äù

These questions help confirm whether the issue is an app limitation or a data mismatch.

#### Update or guide accordingly:
- If editable in ConnectX: Update the field and click Save Changes.

- If not editable: Advise the customer to update directly in the Meow Wireless app.

### Action:#### If agent can update directly:Example Response:
‚ÄúI‚Äôve updated your contact information in our system as requested. Please allow a few minutes for the changes to reflect in your Meow Wireless app. If you don‚Äôt see the update after refreshing, you can try logging out and back in.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm the updated field and timestamp in ConnectX.

- Tag the ticket appropriately.

- Note changes in the ticket for reference.

#### If customer needs to update via the app:Example Response:
‚ÄúYou can update your personal details directly through your Meow Wireless app by going to Profile ‚Üí Account Information ‚Üí Edit. Once saved, the changes sync automatically with your Meow Wireless account.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Guide customer through steps visually if needed.

- Tag the ticket accordingly.

- Set to ‚ÄúSolved‚Äù after confirmation from the customer.

#### If field is locked or requires backend update:Example Response:
‚ÄúSome details, like verified email or linked phone number, can only be updated internally for security reasons. I‚Äôll escalate your request to our Account Management Team for verification and update. This process usually takes **2‚Äì3 business days**.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Escalate to Viru with updated details and verification info.

- Include transaction or identity proof if required.

- Tag the ticket accordingly.

### Result:
- The customer‚Äôs information is verified and accurately updated.

- Sensitive updates (like verified email or phone) are handled securely through escalation.

- Data consistency is maintained across ConnectX and the Meow Wireless platform.

- Customer confidence in data accuracy and privacy is reinforced.

### Additional Notes:
- Never change account details without confirming ownership.

- If multiple fields need updating, confirm each one clearly before saving.

- Sensitive updates (email/phone) always require escalation.

- Log every change in the ticket comments for audit purposes.

- Encourage customers to regularly review their profile to keep information current.

#### How to Check Services Included with the Plan?
*Article ID: 42171816385563 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42171816385563-How-to-Check-Services-Included-with-the-Plan*

Updated:¬†

### Situation:Customers usually ask this question when they‚Äôre reviewing their plan details in the Meow Mobile app or right after activating their eSIM. Some may be confused about whether vet care is part of their mobile plan or requires a separate subscription. Others might assume the eSIM covers only mobile data and calls, not realizing that Meow Mobile integrates pet wellness services as part of its unique offering.

### Task:Before answering, the agent should verify a few key details and ensure clarity on the customer‚Äôs plan type.

- 
Verify customer details in the ConnectX panel in Zendesk first. If information is not available, proceed to ConnectX Admin:

Navigate to ConnectX > Customer360 > Enter email or contact number.

- Confirm the plan name or type under the **Products** tab.

- Check for any linked vet care package or service entitlements under their account.

- 
Ask probing questions to understand their concern:

‚ÄúHave you already activated your eSIM?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you asking about the mobile plan, the vet care services, or both?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúHave you tried booking a wellness check through the Meow Mobile app?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúWhich plan did you select when signing up?"

These questions help determine if the customer‚Äôs confusion is about plan inclusions, app usage, or vet service activation.

### Action:#### If the plan details are confirmed in ConnectX:Acknowledge the question and explain what‚Äôs included based on their plan type.

- Mobile Service (eSIM):
Includes data, calls, and SMS according to their selected plan tier.

- Vet Care Perks:
Provides access to cat wellness checks (worth $50) and discounted veterinary services through Meow Mobile‚Äôs partnered clinics.

Example Response:
‚ÄúYour Meow Mobile plan gives you the best of both worlds ‚Äî reliable mobile service through your eSIM and wellness perks for your cat! You‚Äôll get access to $50 worth of cat wellness checks and ongoing discounts through our partnered clinics. You can view these details or book an appointment directly in the Meow Mobile app.‚Äù

Advise the customer to keep their app updated and linked to their registered account to access all included services.

#### If plan details or vet care entitlement aren‚Äôt showing yet in ConnectX:Apologize and reassure the customer that their plan details or benefits may take time to fully sync.
Explain that activation and vet care linking may take up to 24‚Äì48 hours after eSIM activation or payment confirmation.

Example Response:
‚ÄúIt looks like your plan details are still syncing on our end, which can take up to **24‚Äì48 hours** after activation. Don‚Äôt worry because once everything updates, you‚Äôll see both your mobile plan and cat care benefits reflected in your Meow Mobile app. If it‚Äôs still missing after that, we‚Äôll get our system team to check the link between your eSIM plan and vet care perks.‚Äù

### Result:
- The customer clearly understands that their plan includes both eSIM mobile service and vet care perks.

- They know where to view these benefits (in the Meow Mobile app).

- If their plan information hasn‚Äôt synced yet, they‚Äôve been advised of the **24‚Äì48 hour processing time** and next steps.

### Additional Notes:
- Always check ConnectX > Customer360 > Plan Details first before escalating.

- 
If the vet care service is missing in both ConnectX and the Meow Mobile app after **48 hours**:

Tag the ticket accordingly.

- Escalate to the L1 for backend review.

- Remind customers that app updates may be required for the latest plan features to display.

## Airvet

### Airvet

#### States Where Airvet Veterinarians Can Prescribe
*Article ID: 45569798195355 | Updated: 2026-01-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/45569798195355-States-Where-Airvet-Veterinarians-Can-Prescribe*

[airvet2.png]## **Overview**Airvet veterinarians can prescribe medications **only in states where it is legally permitted** and **when medically appropriate**. Prescription availability is governed by state veterinary regulations and clinical judgment.

## **States Where Prescriptions May Be Available**Airvet prescription services are currently available in the following states:

- Alabama
- Arizona
- California
- Florida
- Indiana
- Louisiana
- Maine
- Massachusetts
- Mississippi
- Missouri
- New Jersey
- New York
- Ohio
- Pennsylvania
- Rhode Island
- South Carolina
- Texas
- Vermont
- Virginia
## **Important Notes**
- A prescription is **never guaranteed**, even in eligible states.
- The veterinarian determines whether prescribing is **legally allowed and medically appropriate**.
- Some conditions may still require **in-person veterinary care**.
## **Sample Script:**Absolutely! Airvet prescription services may be available if you‚Äôre located in one of the following states:
Alabama, Arizona, California, Florida, Indiana, Louisiana, Maine, Massachusetts, Mississippi, Missouri, New Jersey, New York, Ohio, Pennsylvania, Rhode Island, South Carolina, Texas, Vermont, and Virginia.

That said, we always want to be transparent. A prescription isn‚Äôt guaranteed, even in these states. During your visit, the veterinarian will carefully review your pet‚Äôs needs and determine what‚Äôs both medically appropriate and legally allowed.

If a prescription isn‚Äôt the right option, the vet will still guide you with expert advice and next steps to help support your pet‚Äôs health. üêæ

#### Airvet Account Setup & Pet Registration
*Article ID: 44455580058395 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455580058395-Airvet-Account-Setup-Pet-Registration*

**Airvet Account Setup & Pet Registration**

**Use this procedure when guiding a customer through the initial app setup to ensure they successfully link their Meow Mobile benefit and register their pet.**

### **Step 1: Download & Activation via Meow Mobile App**
- 
**Download Airvet:**
Download the **Airvet** app from the Apple App Store (iOS) or Google Play Store (Android).
- 
*Note:* Do not create an account directly in the Airvet app yet.

- 
**Initiate from Meow Mobile:**
Open the **Meow Mobile App** on the device.
- Navigate to the **"Benefits"** or **"Plan Details"** tab.
- Tap the button labeled **"Activate Airvet"** or **"Launch Airvet"**.

- 
**Automatic Redirection:**
The device will automatically switch over to the Airvet app.
- Because the user clicked through the Meow Mobile app, the free subscription benefit will be automatically applied to the registration flow.

### **Step 2: Owner Profile Setup**
- 
**Sign Up:** Once redirected to Airvet, tap **"Sign Up"**.
- 
**Personal Details:**

**Full Name:** Enter the primary account holder's First and Last Name.
- 
**Email Address:** Enter a valid email address (used for visit summaries and login).
- 
**Password:** Create a secure password (minimum 8 characters).

- 
**Notifications:**
Select **"Allow Notifications"** when prompted.
- 
*Context:* Explain that this is essential so they do not miss callbacks from the vet during a triage session.

### **Step 3: Pet Profile Registration**
- 
**Add a Pet:** Tap **"Add Pet"** or the **"+"** icon on the home screen.
- 
**Basic Details:**

**Name:** Enter the pet's name.
- 
**Species:** Select Dog, Cat, or Other.
- 
**Breed:** Search for the breed (e.g., "Golden Retriever" or "Domestic Shorthair"). If mixed, select "Mix" or the dominant breed.
- 
**Gender:** Select Male or Female.

- 
**Physical Stats:**

**Age/DOB:** Enter the Date of Birth (or approximate age if unknown).
- 
**Weight:** Enter the approximate weight (lbs or kg).
- 
**Spayed/Neutered:** Select "Yes" or "No".

- 
**Medical Context (Optional but Recommended):**

**Photo:** Upload a clear photo of the pet (helps vets visualize the animal during triage).
- 
**Medications:** List any current daily medications.
- 
**Known Conditions:** Add any chronic issues (e.g., "Diabetic," "Hip Dysplasia").

### **Step 4: Primary Vet Information**
- 
**Clinic Details:**
Search for the customer's regular, physical vet clinic in the search bar.
- Select the correct clinic from the results.

- 
**Authorization:**
Toggle **"Share records with my vet"** to **ON**.
- 
*Context:* This allows Airvet to email a copy of the consultation summary to the customer's regular doctor for their permanent file.

### **Step 5: Final Confirmation**
- 
**Dashboard Verification:**
Ensure the user lands on the Airvet Home Screen.
- Verify that no payment banner appears (the account should show as "Active" or "Sponsored by Meow Mobile").

- 
**Ready State:**The **"Talk to a Vet"** button should be visible and active (colored blue, not greyed out).

---

### Airvet - Escalation / Redirect

#### How to Handle Airvet Escalations / Redirect?
*Article ID: 42368272851483 | Updated: 2025-11-10*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42368272851483-How-to-Handle-Airvet-Escalations-Redirect*

Updated:

### Situation:Customers usually reach out with these inquiries when:

- They‚Äôre having issues inside the Airvet app (ex. unable to log in, video call not working, or missing appointment history).

- They need account actions or data updates (ex. delete or change personal info).

- They have billing or subscription questions specific to Airvet.

- They‚Äôre seeking veterinary advice or medical records from past consultations.

These requests cannot be handled by Meow Wireless support because they require direct access to Airvet‚Äôs internal systems or veterinary team.

Common examples:

- ‚ÄúCan you help me access my Airvet account?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúI need to delete or update my Airvet profile.‚Äù

- ‚ÄúMy Airvet membership was charged incorrectly.‚Äù

- ‚ÄúI want a copy of my pet‚Äôs consultation records.‚Äù

- ‚ÄúI need to speak with a vet through Airvet.‚Äù

### Task:The agent‚Äôs goal is to:

- Identify when an inquiry involves Airvet-specific systems or veterinary support.

- Gently inform the customer that Airvet manages those functions directly.

- Guide the customer to contact Airvet Support for secure and accurate assistance.

- Reassure them that Airvet and Meow Wireless are trusted partners working together.

### Steps for Agents:#### 1. Identify if the issue belongs to AirvetCheck if the question involves:

- Airvet app access, features, or consultations.

- Medical or veterinary-related requests.

- Subscription or billing related to Airvet‚Äôs service.

- Account management or privacy (ex. delete, update, or retrieve personal data).

If yes, the case must be redirected to Airvet instead of handled internally.

#### 2. Ask clarifying questions (to confirm scope)To ensure it‚Äôs an Airvet-related issue, you may ask:

- ‚ÄúAre you currently using the Airvet app or the Meow Wireless app?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúCan you tell me what happens when you try to access your Airvet account?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúWas this charge for your Airvet membership or for Meow Wireless‚Äôs waitlist?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúIs your concern about your pet‚Äôs medical consultation or app login?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúWhich app are you currently trying to use ‚Äî Meow Wireless or Airvet?‚Äù

These questions help confirm if the user needs Airvet‚Äôs direct help.

#### 3. Advise the customer to contact Airvet directlyOnce confirmed, guide the customer in a clear and reassuring way.

Example Response:

‚ÄúThank you for reaching out! Since this involves your Airvet account and features within their app, the best way to get this resolved quickly is to contact Airvet‚Äôs dedicated Support Team.

Please email them directly at support@airvet.com using the same email address you used to sign up.

They‚Äôll be able to securely verify your account and help with this request right away.‚Äù

If it‚Äôs a technical or medical concern:

‚ÄúThat sounds like something Airvet‚Äôs support team can best help you with, as they handle all app access, billing, and vet consultations directly. You can reach them at support@airvet.com.‚Äù

### Action:Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm that the user understands they should contact Airvet.

- Provide the correct contact email or app path.

- Add an internal note (ex. ‚ÄúCustomer redirected to Airvet Support‚Äù).

- Tag the ticket accordingly.

- Close the interaction with a helpful and polite tone.

### Result:
- Customers are properly guided to Airvet for faster, expert assistance.

- Meow Wireless support avoids handling protected or system-specific data.

- Communication remains clear, helpful, and consistent.

- The partnership between Meow Wireless and Airvet is reinforced through a seamless redirection process.

### Additional Notes:Redirect to Airvet if:

- The inquiry involves app access, login, consultations, billing, or account deletion.

- The customer needs veterinary or medical-related help.

- Any data or action involves Airvet‚Äôs internal system or vet team.

Do not attempt to:

- Troubleshoot Airvet app errors beyond general suggestions (update, reinstall, retry).

- Access or modify Airvet user accounts.

- Promise refunds or changes within the Airvet platform.

## Port-in and Port-out

### Port-out Procedure

#### Carrier-wise number port out ability check
*Article ID: 44754208880795 | Updated: 2025-12-24*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44754208880795-Carrier-wise-number-port-out-ability-check*

### **AT&T¬†**
### **1. How to Check Your Contract Status**Most modern AT&T plans are "no-contract," but you may still have a **Service Commitment** (from an older plan) or an **Installment Plan** (paying off a phone).

- **Via myAT&T App/Web:**Log in to your Account Overview.
Go to My Wireless.
Select the device you want to check and click Manage device & features.
Scroll to the bottom. You will see a Service commitment end date if you are under a traditional contract.

- **Checking Device Balance:**Under the same Manage device section, look for Installment plan details. If you owe money on the phone itself, you must pay the remaining balance in full before the device can be "unlocked" for another carrier.

Via Short Code: Dial *225# from your AT&T phone. You will receive a text message with your current balance and basic account info, though it may not show full installment details.

Via Phone: Call AT&T Customer Service at 800-331-0500 or dial 611 from your mobile device and ask for your "contract or installment end date."

### ### **2. Your Ability to Port Out**Legally, per FCC rules, AT&T **cannot refuse** to port your number to another carrier, even if you owe a balance or are under contract. However, there are financial and technical catches:

- 
**Financial Impact:** If you port out while under contract, AT&T will charge an **Early Termination Fee (ETF)**. If you are on an installment plan, the **entire remaining balance** of the phone becomes due immediately on your final bill.
- 
**Device Locking:** Your phone will remain "locked" to AT&T's network until it is paid off in full. You can port your *number* to a new phone on another carrier anytime, but you can't use your *current AT&T phone* elsewhere until the balance is zero.
- 
**Account Status:** Your account must be **active** to port. **Do not cancel** your AT&T service yourself; the porting process with your new carrier will automatically cancel the AT&T line once it's finished.
### ### **3. What You Need to Port Your Number**To move your number, you will need three specific pieces of information to give to your new carrier:

- 
**Account Number:** Found at the top of your paper bill or under "Profile" in the app.
- 
**Transfer PIN:** You must request a **Number Transfer PIN** (this is different from your account passcode).

**Quick Way:** Dial **#PORT** (**#7678**) from your AT&T phone.
- 
**App Way:** Go to **Profile** > **Settings** > **Transfer phone number** > **Request a new PIN**.

- 
**Account ZIP Code:** The billing ZIP code associated with your AT&T account.### **Important Tip : **Before you start the port, check if you have **"Wireless Account Lock"** enabled in your security settings. If this is "On," it will block any transfer attempts until you toggle it

### ### **Verizon**### **1. How to Check Your Status**You can see if you are still paying for a device or have a legacy contract through these steps:

- 
**Via the My Verizon App:**
Tap the **Account** tab at the bottom.
- Go to **Devices** and select your specific phone line.
- Look for the **Device payment** section. If you see a remaining balance and a "Pay off device" option, you have an active installment plan.

- 
**Via the Verizon Website:**
Log in and go to **Account > My devices > Device Overview**.
- Select your device; the **Contract End Date** or **Device Payment Plan** details will be listed near the top left, next to the image of your phone.

- **Via Phone:** Call **800-922-0204** or dial **611** from your mobile device.
¬†

### **2. Can You Port Your Number Out?****Yes.** Under FCC rules, Verizon cannot refuse a port request, even if you owe money on your bill or a device. However, there is a common "blocker" specific to Verizon that you must handle first:

- 
**Number Lock (Port Protection):** Verizon has a security feature called **Number Lock** that is often enabled to prevent fraud. **If this is ON, your port will fail.****How to disable it:** In the My Verizon app or website, go to **Account > Account Settings > Security Settings** and toggle **Number Lock** to **Off** for the line you want to move.

- **Financial Impact:** As soon as you port your number, any remaining balance on your device payment plan will be accelerated and added to your **final bill** immediately.
¬†

### **3. Requirements for a Verizon Port**To move your number to a new carrier, you will need:

- 
**Account Number:** Found on your bill or under **Account Overview** online. It usually ends in -00001.

- 
**Number Transfer PIN:** Verizon does *not* use your account password for porting. You must generate a unique 6-digit PIN.

**The Shortcut:** Dial **#PORT**** (****#7678****)** from your Verizon phone. They will text you a link to generate the PIN.

- **Manual:** In the app/website, go to **Profile > Number Transfer PIN > Generate PIN**.

- **Active Line:** Your service must be active at the moment the new carrier requests the transfer.
**Pro-Tip:** Verizon devices are usually automatically unlocked 60 days after purchase, but only if they are not flagged for fraud. If you haven't hit that 60-day mark, your phone may remain locked to Verizon even after you port the number.

¬†

**T-Mobile**

### **1. How to Check Your T-Mobile Status**To see if you still owe money on a device or have a specific agreement:

- 
**Via the T-Life App (formerly T-Mobile App):**
Open the **Manage** tab.
- Select your plan or the specific line you want to check.
- Look for **"Installment plan details"** or **"Equipment"**. It will show you your remaining balance and how many payments are left.

¬†

- 
**Via the T-Mobile Website:**
1. Log in and go to your **Account Overview**.
2. Scroll to **"Lines and Devices"** and click on your device.¬†
3. Select **"View installment plan"** to see your remaining balance.

¬†
- 
**Via Short Code:** Dial **#BAL#**** (****#225#****)** on your keypad to see your current account balance. To check device-specific info, you usually need to use the app or website.
¬†

### **2. Can T-Mobile Block Your Port?****No.** Legally, T-Mobile cannot block you from porting your number to another carrier, even if you have a past-due balance or an unpaid device. However, there is **one specific setting** that might *technically* block the process until you turn it off:

- 
**Port Out Protection:** T-Mobile offers a security feature called "Port Out Protection" (sometimes called "Takeover Protection"). If this is enabled on your line, any porting request will be automatically rejected. You must disable this in the app or website under **Profile > Privacy and Notifications** before you can leave.
- 
**Financial Impact:** Just like with AT&T, once you port your number, any remaining device balance (EIP) becomes **due immediately** on your final bill.
¬†

### **3. Requirements to Port Out of T-Mobile**To successfully move your number, you will need three things:

- 
**Account Number:** Found at the top of your PDF bill or on your online dashboard.
- 
**Number Transfer PIN:** T-Mobile uses a specific "Temporary Port Out PIN" that is different from your account password.
**How to get it:** In the T-Life app or website, go to **Profile > Settings > Line Settings > Request a Transfer PIN**.

- 
**Account Status:** Keep your line active until the port is finished.
**Note on Device Unlocking:** If you still owe money on your phone, T-Mobile will keep the *device* locked to their network. Even after you port your number, you won't be able to use that phone with another carrier until the balance is paid and you request an unlock.
¬†

### **Cricket Wireless¬†**

**1. Verify "Contract" and Financial Status**Cricket Wireless does not use annual service contracts. However, users must verify two specific areas of obligation:

- Service Payments: Since Cricket is prepaid, you do not have "Early Termination Fees." You simply stop paying for the next month.
- 
Device Unlock Eligibility: If you purchased your phone from Cricket, it is likely locked to their network.
The Rule: The device must have been active on Cricket service for at least 6 months to be eligible for an unlock.
- How to Check: Open the myCricket App > Settings > Device Unlock. If eligible, you can request the unlock directly there.

## **2. Pre-Port Requirements (Mandatory)**A port request will be automatically rejected by Cricket if these two security features are not addressed:

### **A. Disable Account Lock**Cricket's "Account Lock" feature protects you from unauthorized transfers. It must be turned OFF before the new carrier requests your number.

- Open the myCricket App.
- Tap the Gear Icon (Settings) in the top right.
- Select Account Lock.
- Toggle the setting to OFF. (You will receive a one-time PIN via text to verify this change).
### **B. Obtain a Number Transfer PIN**You cannot use your standard 4-digit account PIN to port out. You must generate a unique, temporary Number Transfer PIN.

- 
Option 1 (Fastest): Dial *PORT (*7678) from your Cricket phone and follow the prompts.

- Option 2 (App): Go to Settings > Line Settings > Get my Number Transfer PIN.
- Validity: This PIN is valid for 5 days.
## 
**3. Execution Checklist for Porting****Gather the following data before contacting Meow Mobile:**

**Phone Number**
**Your 10-digit Cricket mobile number.**

**Account Number**
**Found in the myCricket App under "Account Summary" (9 digits).**

**Transfer PIN**

**Obtained via *****PORT**** or the App (not your login PIN).**

**Billing Zip Code**
**The Zip Code on file with your Cricket account.**

¬†

## **4. Finalizing the Transfer**
- Do Not Cancel: Ensure your Cricket account remains active. If you cancel your account manually before the transfer is finished, you will lose your number.
- Submit Request: Provide the data above to your new carrier.
- Automatic Cancellation: Once the new carrier successfully "pulls" the number, your Cricket service for that line will cancel automatically.

¬†

### **Mint Mobile**

**1. Identify "Contractual" Obligations**Since Mint Mobile is prepaid, your "contract" is simply the duration of the plan you purchased.

- **Step 1.1: **Log in to the Mint Mobile App.
- **Step 1.2: **View the "My Plan" section.
- 
**Step 1.3: **Note your Plan End Date.

¬†***Note:***** **You can port out at any time before this date, but Mint Mobile does not offer pro-rated refunds for unused months.

### **2. Verify Device "Lock" Status**Even if your number is ready to port, your phone might be restricted if you purchased it directly from Mint.

- **Step 2.1: **If you brought your own device (BYOP), it is already unlocked. Skip to Section 3.
- **Step 2.2: **If you bought your phone from Mint, check the Unlock Policy. Mint typically requires the device to have been active on their service for 12 months before they will unlock it for use with another carrier.
- **Step 2.3: **To request an unlock, contact Mint Support at (800) 683-7392.
### **3. Confirm Porting Eligibility**The FCC mandates that carriers cannot "hold your number hostage" due to unpaid balances or pending time on a plan.

- **Criteria A: **Your account must be active. Do not cancel your Mint service before the port is finished, or you will lose the number.
- **Criteria B: **Ensure you have no "Number Lock" enabled in the Account Settings > Security tab of the app.
### 
**US Mobile**

**1. Verify "Contract" and Device Status**
- There are no service contracts or early termination fees (ETFs). You pay for your plan upfront; if you port out before your 30-day cycle ends, you simply forfeit the remaining days.
- 
**Device Lock Status:**
BYOP (Bring Your Own Phone): If you brought your own device to US Mobile, it is already unlocked.
- Purchased from US Mobile: Most devices sold by US Mobile are unlocked. However, if you purchased a device under a specific promotional "lock" term, it generally unlocks automatically after 60 days of continuous service. You can check this in the App > Shop > My Orders.

## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**US Mobile does not display porting information in their app or dashboard for security reasons. You must contact their support team to have the information generated and the "port-out" manually authorized.

### **A. Disable Internal Security Locks**Before a port can be initiated, you must ensure your account is authorized for a move.

- **Step:** Contact US Mobile Support (via Live Chat or 611) and ask them to "Disable the Port-Out Lock" for your specific line. They will verify your identity before toggling this off.### **B. Retrieve Account Number and Port PIN****You cannot use your standard account password or login PIN to port out.**

- **Contact Method 1 (Fastest):** Use the 24/7 Live Chat on the US Mobile website or in the app.
- 
**Contact Method 2:** Email help@usmobile.com or call (878) 205-0088.

¬†
- **Requirement:** State clearly:** *****"I need my Account Number and Port-Out PIN for the purpose of a number transfer."***** **They will send this sensitive data to your registered email address.
****

### 
**Xfinity Mobile**

**1. ****Verify Contract vs. Device Balance**Xfinity Mobile plans are month-to-month with no long-term service contracts. Your primary obligation is likely your device.

- 
**Check Device Status:**
1. Log in to the Xfinity App or[ online portal](https://www.google.com/search?q=https://www.xfinity.com/mobile/my-account/devices).
2. Select the Services tab, then tap Mobile lines and data usage.¬†
3. Select the specific device line.¬†
4. Look for "Payment Details". If you have a remaining balance, porting the number out will cause that balance to be accelerated, meaning the full remaining cost of the phone will appear on your next bill.

- Service Billing: Xfinity does not pro-rate "By the Gig" plans. If you port out in the middle of a cycle, you are charged for the full gigabytes used up to that point.
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Xfinity Mobile uses two distinct security layers that will cause a port to fail if not addressed.

### **A. Disable Number Lock**Xfinity has a fraud-prevention feature called Number Lock. It is often enabled by default.

- Open the Xfinity App and sign in.
- Tap the Services tab > Mobile lines and data usage.
- Tap the line you wish to transfer.
- Scroll to the Line management section and tap Number Lock.
- Toggle the switch to OFF. (You will receive a confirmation email once this is done).
### **B. Generate a Security (Transfer) PIN**You must generate a unique PIN specifically for porting. Do not use your account login password.

- Via App: 1. Navigate to the line you want to transfer (same as Step A). 2. Tap Transfer or cancel this line. 3. Select Get started and follow the prompts. 4. Xfinity will send a 6-digit PIN to that line via text.
- Validity: This PIN is valid for 24 hours. If you do not initiate the port within a day, you must generate a new one.
### 
**Visible**

**1. Verify Financial Status and Device Locking**Visible is a strictly prepaid service. Your only "contractual" obligations are related to the hardware or the current month's payment.

- **Service Payments: **You pay for your service 30 days in advance. If you port out in the middle of a month, you will not receive a pro-rated refund for the remaining days.
- 
**Device Unlock Status:**
If you brought your own phone to Visible, it is already unlocked.
- If you purchased a phone from Visible, it is automatically unlocked 60 days after activation. You do not need to submit a request; it happens over-the-air once the 60-day requirement is met and the device is paid in full.

- **Device Balances:** If you financed your phone through Visible's partner (Affirm), your loan agreement is separate from your phone service. Porting your number does not cancel your loan; you must continue making payments to Affirm as scheduled.
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Visible has a high-security "Number Lock" feature that will cause a port-out request to be immediately rejected by their system if not toggled off.

### **A. Disable Line Lock (Number Lock)**
- 
Open the Visible App or log in to your[ account online](https://www.visible.com/sign-in).

- Navigate to the Account section (on the app) or the Profile tab (on desktop).
- Look for Privacy & Security and select Manage Number Security.
- Locate Line Lock and ensure it is toggled to OFF (Unlocked).
- You may be asked to enter a security code sent to your email or phone to confirm this change.
### **B. Retrieve Your Port-Out PIN**Visible generates a unique 6-digit PIN for transfers. Do not use your account password or your SIM PIN.

- In the same Account/Profile section used above, find the Port-Out PIN button.
- Select Request via email.
- Visible will send an email containing your Account Number and your 6-digit Port-Out PIN.
- Validity: This PIN is valid for 7 days. If you do not port within a week, you must request a new one.
### 
**Google Fi**

**1. Verify Contract and Financial Status**Google Fi does not use annual service contracts. However, users must check for "Equipment" or "Promotion" obligations that could lead to a large final bill.

- 
**Check for Device Financing:¬†**
1. Log in to the Google Fi App or[ ](https://fi.google.com)[fi.google.com](http://fi.google.com).
2. Go to the Billing tab and select Manage device payments.¬†
3. If you have a remaining balance, the full amount will be charged to your Google Payments account once the port is successful.

¬†
- 
**Check Promotional Status:¬†**
1. If you received a discount on a phone (e.g., "$500 off via 24 monthly credits"), porting out before the 24 months are up will void the remaining credits.
2. You will be billed for the "un-rebated" portion of the device's original price.

## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Google Fi does not show your Account Number or Transfer PIN on your main dashboard. You must go through a specific "cancellation flow" to reveal this information. This will not cancel your service immediately.

### **Retrieve Account Number and Transfer PIN**
- Open the Google Fi App or website.
- On the Account tab, select Manage plan.
- Scroll to the bottom and select Leave Google Fi.
- Follow the on-screen prompts (Google will ask why you are leaving).
- Select Transfer your number to another carrier.
- Once you confirm, a "Cancellation pending" banner will appear. Under this banner, select Get Transfer Info.
- Crucial Note: Your Account Number and PIN are case-sensitive. Write them down exactly as they appear.
- Validity: The Transfer PIN is valid for 14 days.

¬†

### 
**Straight Talk**

**1. Verify "Contract" and Device Status**Straight Talk does not use annual service contracts. Your primary obligations are related to your pre-paid service period and your hardware.

- 
**Service Status**: Check your Service End Date by texting the word USAGE or DUE to 611611.*Note:* You can port out at any time, but Straight Talk does not offer refunds for unused days remaining in your 30-day cycle.

- 
**Device Unlock Status**: If you purchased your phone from Straight Talk, it is likely locked.
The Rule: Most Straight Talk phones are eligible for unlocking after 12 months of active service (some newer Apple/Samsung devices may unlock after 60 days).
- To check eligibility, call their Unlocking Department at (888) 442-5102.

## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Straight Talk has high security standards for porting. If your account details do not match their records exactly, the port will be rejected.

### **A. Disable Port Protection (Line Lock)**Some Straight Talk accounts have a "Line Lock" feature enabled to prevent unauthorized transfers.

- Open the My Account App or log in to the Straight Talk website.
- Go to Account Settings > Security.
- Ensure Line Lock is toggled OFF.
### **B. Retrieve Your Account Number**Straight Talk account numbers are not clearly labeled on your bill.

- 
If you bought your phone from Straight Talk: Your Account Number is usually the IMEI or MEID of that original phone. You can find this by dialing *#06# on your keypad.

- If you brought your own phone (BYOP): Your Account Number is typically the last 15 digits of your SIM card number (ICCID).
### **C. Obtain a Number Transfer PIN (NTP)**You cannot use your standard 4-digit security PIN to port out. You must generate a temporary 4-digit Number Transfer PIN.

- 
The Shortcut: Text the letters NTP to 611611 from your Straight Talk device.

- Response: You will receive a text message with a unique 4-digit PIN.
- Validity: This PIN is valid for 7 days.

¬†

### **Spectrum**

**1. Verify "Contract" vs. Device Payment Balance**Spectrum Mobile offers month-to-month service with no annual contracts. However, if you purchased a device from them, you are likely under a financial agreement.

- 
**Check Your Status:**

Log in to the **My Spectrum App** or the[ Spectrum.net portal](https://www.spectrum.net/).

- Navigate to the **Billing** tab.
- Select **Mobile** from your service list.
- Choose your device to see the **Remaining Balance**.

- **Financial Impact:** If you port your number while you still owe money on a phone, the **entire remaining balance becomes due immediately** on your final bill.
- **Internet Dependency:** Note that if you cancel your Spectrum Internet service but keep Spectrum Mobile, your mobile bill will increase by an "unbundled" service fee (typically $10+ per line).
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Spectrum Mobile protects numbers with a security lock. You must generate a specific PIN to bypass this before the new carrier can take the number.

### **A. Disable Port-Out Locks**If you have previously called Spectrum to "lock" your number for security, you must call **(833) 224-6603** to have the representative remove the manual port-protection lock.

### **B. Generate a Transfer PIN**You cannot use your account password or your 4-digit security code for porting. You must generate a unique 6-digit **Transfer PIN**.

- Sign in to the **My Spectrum App** or the online portal.
- Go to **Services** > **Mobile**.
- Select the specific line you want to move.
- Scroll down and select **Get Transfer PIN**.
- Follow the prompts to receive a passcode via text or email to verify your identity.
- Once verified, the **6-digit Transfer PIN** will be displayed.
- **Validity:** This PIN is valid for **72 hours** (3 days) only.

¬†

### 
******H2O Wireless**

**1. Verify Contract and Financial Status**H2O Wireless is a no-contract provider. You are not bound by an annual agreement or early termination fees (ETFs).

- **Service Obligation:** Since you pay in advance, you can leave at any time. However, H2O does not offer pro-rated refunds for any unused days or airtime remaining on your current 30-day cycle.
- 
**Check Plan Expiration:** Text the word bal to 327986787 from your handset to see your current balance and service end date.

- **Device Status:** If you purchased a phone through H2O's website via financing (like Affirm), your loan is independent of your service. Porting your number will not cancel your loan payments; you must continue paying Affirm as agreed.
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**H2O Wireless does not display porting credentials (Account Number and PIN) in your online account dashboard or mobile app. To protect against "SIM swapping" fraud, they require a manual verification process.

### **A. Prepare for Verification**H2O will require you to verify your identity by providing the 3 most recent outgoing calls you made from your phone. Have these numbers ready before you contact them.

### **B. Retrieve Account Number and Porting PIN**You must contact the H2O Porting Department directly to have your number "released" for transfer.

- **Call Support**: Dial 1-800-643-4926 or the Porting Hotline at 1-800-562-3229.
- **Request Info**: State that you need your Account Number and Porting PIN to transfer your service.
- **Identity Check**: Provide the 3 outgoing call numbers as requested.
- 
**Note the Info**: * Account Number: This is typically a unique 9-digit or 12-digit number (not your phone number).**PIN:** The default is often the last 4 digits of your phone number, but the representative will confirm if yours is different or needs to be set.

**¬†**

### 
**Consumer Cellular**

**1. Verify "Contract" and Financial Obligations**Consumer Cellular provides month-to-month service. However, your account may have financial ties related to your device or billing cycle.

- 
**Check Device Status:** 1. Log in to the My CC App or your[ online account](https://www.consumercellular.com/login). 2. Check your Equipment or Installment Plan status. 3. If you have an outstanding balance on an EasyPay installment plan, porting your number will cause the remaining balance to be due immediately on your final bill.

- **Billing Cycle**: Consumer Cellular bills in arrears (after the service is used). If you port out mid-cycle, they do not pro-rate your final month. You will be responsible for the full monthly service charge of your final billing period.
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Consumer Cellular does not display porting credentials in your online profile for security reasons. You must contact their customer service team to have your account "port-ready."

### **A. Disable Port Protection**Consumer Cellular uses internal security protocols to prevent unauthorized transfers. There is no toggle switch in the app; instead, the security is cleared when you request your credentials.

### **B. Retrieve Account Number and Transfer PIN**You must obtain a specific 9-digit account number and a unique Transfer PIN (sometimes called an Authorization ID or AID).

- **Contact Support:** Call (888) 345-5509 or dial 611 from your Consumer Cellular device.
- **Verify Identity**: The representative will verify your identity (usually via a code sent to your phone or your account's security question).
- **Request Info**: State clearly that you are moving to a new carrier and need your Account Number and Number Transfer PIN.
- 
**Note the Details**: * Account Number: This is usually a 9-digit number found on your invoice (not your phone number).Transfer PIN: This is a temporary 4-to-6 digit code provided by the agent.

- **Validity**: This PIN is typically valid for 30 days.

¬†

****

### **C Spire**

**1. Verify Contract and Financial Status**C Spire is a regional carrier that still utilizes traditional service contracts for some legacy plans and device promotions.

- **Check Your Status**: Log in to the My C Spire app or website. Navigate to Account > Plan Details. Look specifically for a "Contract End Date" or "Device Installment Balance."
- **Financial Obligations**: If you are under a legacy 2-year contract, porting out before the end date will trigger an Early Termination Fee (ETF). If you have a device payment plan, the remaining balance will be charged in full on your final bill.
- **Device Locking**: C Spire typically locks devices for 60 days after activation. If you are porting out after this period and the phone is paid off, it should be eligible for unlocking via their support line at (855) 277-4734.
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**C Spire does not have a "Number Lock" toggle in the app, but they require specific credentials that are often misunderstood.

- **Account Number**: This is a 10-digit number found on the top right of your paper bill or under "Account Summary" in the app.
- **Port-Out PIN**: Unlike larger carriers, C Spire does not always generate a temporary PIN. In most cases, your Account Security PIN (the 4-digit code you use to verify your identity with support) serves as your Transfer PIN. If you do not have one set, call 611 to establish it before attempting the port.
****

### 
**Dish (Project Genesis)¬†**

**1. Verify Contract Status**Project Genesis is a month-to-month, "early-access" 5G service. There are no service contracts.

- **Billing: **Service is prepaid. There are no refunds for unused days if you port out early.
- **Device Financing:** Most Project Genesis users bought their hardware outright or are on a specific trial. Check your original order email to confirm if you have any remaining device obligations.
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Because Project Genesis is a specialized network, the porting process is highly manual and handled through their specific support team.

- **Retrieving Info:** You cannot find your Porting PIN in the app. You must use the In-App Chat or call the Project Genesis support line directly.
- **The "Manual Release"**: Once you have the PIN and provide it to your new carrier, Dish often requires a manual "release" from their porting department. It is recommended to stay in the chat with a representative until the new carrier confirms they have received the number.

¬†

### **Boost Mobile¬†**

**1. Verify Status and "Contract"**Boost Mobile is strictly no-contract. However, since the acquisition by Dish, many users were moved to a new billing system.

- 
**Check Your System:** If you use the Boost One app, you are on the new system. If you use the older My Boost app, you are a legacy customer.

¬†
- **Device Payments:** If you are on "Boost Infinite," check for device financing. Like other carriers, the balance is due immediately upon port-out.
## 2. **Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**
- 
**Requesting the PIN:**

**New System**: In the Boost One app, go to Account Settings > Port Out Info. The app will generate a 6-digit PIN.

¬†
- 
**Legacy System**: You must call (833) 502-6678 to get your account number and PIN. Legacy account numbers are not listed in the app for security reasons.

¬†

- 
**Validity:** The Port-Out PIN is typically valid for 30 days.

### ### **Ultra Mobile**

**1. Verify Account Standing**Ultra Mobile is a prepaid service with no long-term contracts.

- Plan Duration: Ultra offers 1, 3, 6, and 12-month plans. Like Mint Mobile, if you port out before your multi-month plan ends, the remaining months are non-refundable.
- Account Status: Your account must be Active. If you are in a "Suspended" state for non-payment, the port will be rejected.
## **2. Mandatory Pre-Port Actions (Security)**Ultra Mobile requires a manual request for porting credentials to ensure the account owner is the one making the move.

- **Account Number:** Found in the Account Details section of the Ultra Mobile app or web portal.
- **Transfer PIN:** This is not your account password. You must call Ultra Mobile at (888) 777-0446 or use their Online Chat to speak with a representative.
- **Identity Verification:** They will ask for your Billing Zip Code and potentially the last 4 digits of the Credit Card on file to release the PIN.
