#### Port-Out Steps
*Article ID: 44557426677531 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44557426677531-Port-Out-Steps*

## **Port-Out (Transfer Number Away from Meow Mobile)**## **Step 1: Discovery (The "Why")**## Before providing the porting details, gently ask for the reason behind the request.- ## Script: "I‚Äôm sorry to hear you‚Äôre thinking of leaving us! To help us improve, may I ask what is making you switch? Is it related to the price, coverage, or a specific technical issue?"### **Step 2: Retention (The "Save")**## Match your response to their reason. Most churn is preventable.## **Scenario A:** "The Data/Service isn't working"## Action: Check the ticket history. Have we actually troubleshot the issue?## **Scenario B:** "I need a feature you don't have (e.g., International Roaming)"## Action: Check if we have an add-on or upcoming feature release.¬†

### **Step 3: The Process (Self-Service Guidance)**## If the customer declines the offer or insists on proceeding, provide the instructions clearly. Do not make it difficult. Customers can get their port out PIN generated right from the Meow Mobile application.¬†- 
## Instructions from the application:
Moreover, we can also generate the port out PIN from ConnectX on behalf of the customer if they are unable to do it on their own.**¬†**
## **On ConnectX: Go to Customer Details tab > Port out PIN > click on 3 dots > select generate**.¬†
## **Once generated the PIN will be valid for 5 days.****¬†**
##

### Port-in Introduction

#### Port-In Procedure
*Article ID: 44557504609947 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44557504609947-Port-In-Procedure*

## **Part 1: Port-In (Transfer Number to Meow Mobile)****L0 Action -**

### **Step 1 - Visual Audit**
- **Check Ticket History:** Review if the customer has attempted to port this number previously or if there are rejected requests.
- 
**Check Account Status in ConnectX:**
¬†Ensure account is ACTIVE¬†
- ¬†Ensure eSIM is INSTALLED¬†
- ¬†Check data balance not throttled¬†
- ¬†Check most recent usage
- ¬†Check subscription start date¬†
- ¬†Check if line was recently ported in¬†
- ¬†Fetch details of port-in (status, donor, number, timestamp)¬†

- **Verify Number Format:** Ensure the number to be ported is a valid 10-digit US number (International ports are not supported).
### **Step 2 - Probing & Data Collection**
- 
**Acknowledge and Advise (The Golden Rule):***Script:* "I can certainly help you move your number over! Please remember not to cancel your old service yet. The number must be active for the transfer to work."

- 
**Collect Mandatory Credentials:**
**Phone Number** to transfer.
- **Account Number** from the previous carrier.
- **Number Transfer PIN (NTP):** A temporary 6-digit PIN (different from their login password).
- **Billing Zip Code** associated with the old carrier account.

- **Confirm Eligibility:** "Is your previous number currently active and not suspended for fraud?"
### **Step 3 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Check : Account is ACTIVE, eSIM is INSTALLED, Check data balance not throttled, Check subscription start date

[Account Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600349458331-Check-Account-Status-ConnectX)

2
Fetch details of port-in (status, donor, number, timestamp)

[Port-in Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44601028819739-Port-in-Status-ConnectX)

3
Check for similar open tickets

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

### **Step 4 - Steps to be done by (L0)**
- 
**Check for Port-in status:**
*Open - OP - means in progress*
- *Confirmed - CF¬† - means confirmed by donor and now AT&T needs to issue final command to complete it.¬†*
- *Complete - CO - Port In is complete*
- *Denied - Rejected by Donor*
- *Cancelled - Can be cancelled by¬† any party depending upon reasons.*
- *Delayed - Not really relevant for wireless, usually used for wireline*
- *Error - ER - Not sure what will be received in which scenario. Amdocs said they have not seen it yet.*
- *Conflict - CT - One or more information fields are incorrect, correct them and resubmit the request.*

- 
***L0 Mandatory Actions & Checks if Port-in fails after customer submission.¬†***
*(L0 must perform these steps before escalation)*
***Capture RAT/Signal Screenshot** (Radio Access Technology proof).*
- ***Confirm eSIM is Detected and Provisioned.***
- ***Verify no ‚ÄúEmergency Calls Only‚Äù** status.*
- ***Test Inbound/Outbound Call and SMS Routing.***
- ***Check if APN Settings are correct.***

- 
**Post-Port Activation:**
Once the system shows **"Port Complete"**:
Instruct the customer to **Restart** their device.
- If calls fail, toggle **Airplane Mode** ON/OFF.
- Reset Network Settings if issues persist.

**Step 5 - Providing the ETR to customer**

- **Wireless to Wireless:** 10 minutes - 2 hours.
- **Assurance:** "We will notify you via email as soon as the transfer is complete.¬†
**Step 6 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk -**

- **Ensure all mandatory fields are filled.**
- **Set Priority:** High (if the customer has no service).
- 
**L1 Mandatory Requirements ***(L1 requires these details before touching the case)*
**Timestamp**
- **MSISDN** (Phone Number)
- **ICCID** (SIM Number)
- **Donor Operator** (Previous Carrier)
- **SIM Slot / Primary-SIM Status**

- **Status:** On-hold / Escalated.
- Also make sure to transfer the chat to L1 group and not a particular agent.

#### Carrier-wise port-in instructions
*Article ID: 44457968468763 | Updated: 2025-12-24*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44457968468763-Carrier-wise-port-in-instructions*

## **Carrier wise Port-In instructions**
¬†**1. T-Mobile**
- 
**Account Number:**
**App/Web:** Top right corner of the **Bill** or main **Dashboard**.

- 
**Transfer PIN (NTP):**

*Requirement:* Wi-Fi must be **OFF**.
- 
**App (T-Life / T-Mobile):** Go to **Manage** > **Settings** (Gear) > **Permissions & Controls** (or Profile) > **Line Settings** > **Request a Transfer PIN**.
- 
**Web:** **Account** > **Profile Settings** > **Line Settings** > **Request a Transfer PIN**.
- 
**Validity:** 7 Days.

### **2. AT&T**
- 
**AT&T Postpaid (Standard Monthly Bill)**
**Account Number:**

**On Bill:** Top right corner of the paper/PDF bill (9‚Äì12 digits).
- 
**App:** Log in > **Profile** > **Sign-in Info** > Scroll to **My Linked Accounts**.

- 
**Transfer PIN (NTP):**
*Do not use the login password.*
- 
**Dial:** Dial ***PORT** (*7678) from the device. Follow the prompts to receive the 6-digit PIN via text.
- 
**App:** Go to **More** > **Manage Profile** > **People & Permissions** > **Transfer Phone Number** > **Request a New PIN**.
- 
**Validity:** 4 Days.

- 
**AT&T Prepaid (GoPhone)**

**Account Number:**
Not visible on the SIM. You must call **611** or Chat Support.
- Ask the agent specifically for the **"12-digit Prepaid Account Number."**

- 
**Transfer PIN:**Use your **4-digit Security PIN** (the same one used to call customer service).

### **3. Verizon**
- 
**Account Number:**

**On Bill:** Top of the first page (usually ends in -00001).
- 
**App:** Go to **Account** > **Edit Profile & Settings** > **Account Overview**.

- 
**Transfer PIN (NTP):**

**Dial:** Dial **#PORT** (#7678) from the device.
- 
**App:** **Account** > **Edit Profile & Settings** > **Mobile** > **Number Transfer PIN** > **Generate PIN**.
- 
**Important:** Go to **Settings > Security** and ensure **"Number Lock"** is turned **OFF**.
- 
**Validity:** 7 Days.¬†

### **4. Cricket Wireless**
- 
**Account Number:**

**App/Web Only:** Log in > **Account Settings** > **Account Info**.
- (It is NOT on the SIM card).

- 
**Transfer PIN:**

**Dial:** Dial ***PORT** (*7678) from the device.
- 
**App:** **Account Settings** > **Line Settings** > Select Line > **Get my Number Transfer PIN**.
- 
**Validity:** 5 Days.

### **5. Mint Mobile**
- 
**Account Number:**Visible in the web dashboard or app, but often masked.

- 
**Transfer PIN:**

**Method 1 (App):** Go to **Account** > scroll down to **Line Settings** or **Account Info**. If not visible there, use Method 2.
- 
**Method 2 (Chat):** Use the "Fox Bot" chat on the website/app. Type **"Port Out"**. The bot will guide you to a secure link to reveal your Account Number and PIN.

### **6. US Mobile**
- 
**Account Number:**

**Web Dashboard:** Log in > Go to **Lines** > Click on the specific line you want to transfer.
- Click **"Port out this line"** (usually under "Line Settings" or "Connectivity").
- If you don't see it, use the **Chat** bubble. Their agents provide it instantly.

- 
**Transfer PIN:**
Found in the same section as the Account Number on the dashboard after clicking "Port out this line".
- It is often 1234 or randomly generated depending on the network (Warp 5G vs GSM).

### **7. Xfinity Mobile**
- 
**Account Number:**

**App:** Go to the **Account** tab > Scroll to **Account settings**.
- 
**Web:** Log in > **My Account** > The number is at the top left of the page.

- 
**Transfer PIN:**

**App:** Go to the **Devices** tab > Select the device/number > Scroll down to **Transfer or Cancel this Line** > **Learn More**.
- Select **Get a Transfer PIN**.
- 
*Note:* You may not be able to generate this if the device is not paid off.
- 
**Validity:** 5 Days.¬†

### **8. Visible**
-

- (You may need to toggle the "Masking" eye icon to see the full number).

- 
**Transfer PIN:**

**App:** Go to **Account** > **Port-Out PIN**.
- Tap **Request via Email**.
- The PIN is sent immediately to the email address on file.
- 
**Validity:** 7 Days.

### **9. Google Fi**- 
**Account Number & PIN:**
*Note: The Account Number is NOT the phone number.*
- 
**App/Web:** Open Google Fi > **Account** > **Manage Plan** > **Leave Google Fi**.
- Follow the guided steps (they will try to convince you to stay).
- At the final step, a screen will appear showing both your **Account Number** and **Transfer PIN**.
- 
**Validity:** 14 Days.

### **10. Straight Talk**
- 
**Account Number:**
It is usually the **IMEI** of the phone (dial *#06# to check).
- 
*Exception:* If the customer brought their own phone (BYOP), it is the **last 15 digits of the SIM card number**.

- 
**Transfer PIN:**

**Text:** Send the text message **NTP** to **611611**.
- They will reply with a 4-digit PIN.
- 
*Note:* Do not use the login password.

### **11. Spectrum Mobile**

- 
**Transfer PIN:**

- Scroll down to **Get Transfer PIN**.
- You will be asked to verify your identity (email/text code).
- 
**Validity:** 7 Days.¬†

### **12. H2O Wireless**

### Port-in troubleshooting

#### Port-in/eSIM Error Codes and Rejections
*Article ID: 44457984778651 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44457984778651-Port-in-eSIM-Error-Codes-and-Rejections*

**Port-in/eSIM Error Codes and Rejections**

This Standard Operating Procedure (SOP) outlines the L0 actions for various e-SIM installation and port-in rejection errors, based on the provided error code details.

### **1.¬† Probing and Empathy**
- Acknowledge the frustration and confirm the exact error code or message the customer is receiving.
- Gather details: Device Model and current Operating System (OS) version.
- Obtain an Alternate Contact Number if the current line is completely non-functional.
### **2. ¬†L0 Probing with the Customer**The following errors are typically resolved by guiding the customer through an action on their device:

- 
**ERROR_CARRIER_LOCKED**** (Device is locked by another carrier):**Action: Inform the customer that their device is locked by the previous carrier. They need to contact that carrier to unlock it or use another unlocked device before trying e-SIM again.

- 
**ERROR_EUICC_INSUFFICIENT_MEMORY**** (Insufficient memory for new profile):**
**Action:** Guide the subscriber to the Cellular/Mobile Data settings. Ask them to delete any unused or old e-SIM profiles to free up memory, and then retry the installation process

***Setting>>Mobile Service>>Cellular Plans" or "SIMs>>Delete e-SIM (or Remove Cellular Plan). Confirm the action when prompted.¬†***

- 
**ERROR_EUICC_MISSING**** (e-SIM not supported or module is defective):**
**Action: **Advise the subscriber that the device either does not support e-SIM or has a hardware issue. Ask them to try installing the e-SIM on a different, confirmed e-SIM-compatible device and then retry the installation.

- 
**ERROR_INCOMPATIBLE_CARRIER**** (LPA on device is incompatible):**
**Action: **Ask the subscriber to ensure their device Operating System (OS) is updated to the latest available version. Once updated, they should retry the installation/activation process.
¬†

- 
**ERROR_TIME_OUT**** (Operation timed out):**
**Action: **Advise the subscriber that the connection timed out. Ask them to wait for 5-10 minutes and then retry the installation process, ensuring they have a stable Wi-Fi connection.

### **3. ‚¨ÜÔ∏è Escalation to L1 (Backend/System Errors)****The following errors require intervention from L1/Technical Support, as they relate to profile generation, system configuration, or carrier certificates. L0 Action: escalate Ticket to L1 with all necessary details.**

- 
**EMBEDDED_SUBSCRIPTION_RESULT_ERROR**** (Missing carrier privilege certificate):**
**Action:** Raise the Zendesk Ticket to L1.

- 
**ERROR_ADDRESS_MISSING**** (Incorrect e-SIM activation string):**
**Action**: Raise the Zendesk Ticket to L1.

- 
**ERROR_DISALLOWED_BY_PPR**** (e-SIM profile policy rules preventing installation):**
**Action:** Raise the Zendesk Ticket to L1.

- 
**ERROR_NO_PROFILES_AVAILABLE**** (e-SIM profile not available on SMDP+):**
**Action: **Raise the Zendesk Ticket to L1

### **4. üìù Documentation and Hand-off**
- For all cases, meticulously document the specific error code, the customer's device model/OS, and the action taken (either L0 self-service or L1 escalation).
- Required details by L1:
Registered Mobile Number
- Device Make & Model
- OS Version
- Device IMEI (SIM Slot 1 & 2)
- Date & Time of Issue
- Location (State/City/Area)
- Error Messages / Screenshots"

## eSIM

### eSIM Activation & Set Up

#### How to Check if eSIM is Already Activated?
*Article ID: 44463392211739 | Updated: 2025-12-16*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44463392211739-How-to-Check-if-eSIM-is-Already-Activated*

Updated:

### Situation:Customers usually ask this question after signing up for Meow Wireless and receiving their eSIM activation email.
They may be:

- Unsure how to install or scan the QR code.

- Trying to activate on a device that‚Äôs not eSIM-compatible.

- Reporting that they didn‚Äôt receive their activation link or email.

Agents should be familiar with the basic steps of eSIM setup and the resources available in ConnectX for troubleshooting activation issues.

### Task:The agent‚Äôs goal is to guide the customer through eSIM activation, confirm whether their device supports eSIM, and ensure the activation completes successfully. If activation fails or the email hasn‚Äôt arrived, the agent should verify the account status in ConnectX.

### Steps for Agents:#### 1. Verify customer details in the ConnectX panel in Zendesk first. If information is not available, proceed to ConnectX Admin:
- Go to ConnectX > Customer360.

- Search by email or phone number.

- Check the Account Status and ensure that the eSIM has been issued **(status: ‚ÄúActivation Pending‚Äù or ‚ÄúActivated‚Äù)**.

- Confirm that the activation link or QR code was sent to the registered email.

#### 2. Ask clarifying questions:
- ‚ÄúHave you received your eSIM activation email from Meow Wireless?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you using an eSIM-compatible device?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúDid you already scan the QR code or try the activation link?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you seeing any specific error message during setup?‚Äù

These questions help identify if the issue is with email delivery, device compatibility, or activation failure.

### Action:If the customer received the activation email but hasn‚Äôt installed the eSIM yet:

Guide them through the standard activation steps.

Example Response:
‚ÄúThanks for confirming! You can activate your Meow Wireless eSIM by following these steps:

- Open the email from Meow Wireless containing your eSIM QR code.

- On your phone, go to Settings > Cellular/Mobile Network > Add eSIM.

- Scan the QR code or enter the activation details manually.

- Wait for your device to complete setup ‚Äî this usually takes just a few minutes.
Once installed, your Meow Wireless service will automatically activate and you‚Äôll see our network appear on your phone.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm activation completion in ConnectX (status: ‚ÄúActive‚Äù).

- Tag the ticket accordingly.

If the customer hasn‚Äôt received their eSIM activation email:

Check whether it was sent or delayed.

Example Response:
‚ÄúI see that your eSIM activation email hasn‚Äôt arrived yet ‚Äî no worries! Sometimes it takes up to 30 minutes to appear in your inbox or spam folder. If you still don‚Äôt see it, I‚Äôll request a resend for you.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm email address on file.

- **Request resend via ConnectX ‚Üí ****Actions > Resend Activation Email****.**

- Advise the customer to check all folders (Inbox, Spam, Promotions).

- Tag ticket accordingly.

If the customer reports that activation failed:

Verify device compatibility and escalate if needed.

Example Response:
‚ÄúThanks for letting us know. If your device showed an error during eSIM setup, it could be due to compatibility or connection issues. Let‚Äôs try reinstalling:

- Remove the previous eSIM attempt from your phone‚Äôs settings.

- Restart your device.

- Re-scan the QR code or click the activation link again.
If it still doesn‚Äôt activate, we‚Äôll escalate this to our Technical Team for manual provisioning.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- **Check device compatibility in ConnectX (supported device list).**

- **If reinstallation fails, escalate to **L1 ‚Üí eSIM Activation Issue**.**

- **Advise the customer of a **24‚Äì48 hour turnaround time** for resolution.**

- Tag ticket accordingly.

### Result:
- The customer successfully activates their Meow Wireless eSIM or receives clear next steps.

- Delayed or failed activations are escalated properly through ConnectX.

- The customer gains immediate access to network service and Meow Wireless benefits.

### Additional Notes:
- Never resend QR codes manually outside ConnectX.

- Always verify device compatibility before troubleshooting further.

- Escalate only if activation remains unposted after 48 hours or repeated failure occurs.

- Confirm email and device information carefully before proceeding.

FAQs
[How do I activate my new Meow Mobile eSIM?](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/knowledge/editor/01K7GQNF7BFN0D7CA7QC5HPEKV/en-us?brand_id=37767586877467)

### eSIM Management

#### Number Suspension
*Article ID: 43019888509851 | Updated: 2025-12-03*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/43019888509851-Number-Suspension*

**Subscriber suspension is primarily reserved for two scenarios:**

- 
**Automatic Suspension:**¬†Due to failed payments.
- 
**Manual Suspension:**¬†In the event of device loss (e.g., lost/stolen phone).
Suspension to termination (deactivation) will occur after¬†**90 days**.

¬†

**A. Suspending a Subscriber**

To suspend a subscriber (e.g., in case of a lost device), follow these steps:

¬†

**Step 1: Access the Actions Menu**

- Navigate to the subscriber's main product plan details screen.
- 
Locate and click the three dots (...), which open the menu of actions.

¬†

[Screenshot 2025-11-06 at 1.06.05‚ÄØPM.png]¬†

**Step 2: Initiate Suspension**

- From the menu, select¬†'**Suspend'**

- Click** 'Confirm'**

[Screenshot 2025-11-06 at 1.17.15‚ÄØPM.png]¬†

**Step 3: Enter Reason and Notes**

- 
On the suspension screen, select the reason for suspending the account.

[Screenshot 2025-11-06 at 1.18.33‚ÄØPM.png]

- 
**Add Notes:**¬†Agents must add a small summary (one to two lines) in the notes section to provide context for any future agent viewing the account.
- 
**Always** mention the¬†**ticket number**¬†for reference.
¬†

**Step 4: Confirm Suspension**

- Click 'Submit' to confirm suspension. Once submitted, suspension will take effect immediately. **Please ensure to suspend the services from end of billing cycle only.****¬†**
[EndofCycle.png]¬†

**B. Reactivating a Suspended Subscriber**

Once a subscriber is suspended, the original "**Suspend**" action is replaced with "**Resume**."

¬†

**Step 1: Access the Actions Menu on Suspended Account**

- 
Navigate to the subscriber's account. The status will show as¬†**Suspended**.¬†*(24:25)*

- 
Locate and click the three dots (**...**) to open the menu.

- Select¬†'**Resume' **to reactivate the subscriber.
¬†

**Step 2: Enter Reason and Notes for Resumption**

- 
Enter a¬†**reason**¬†for reactivating the account.

- Add¬†**notes**, including the ticket number, as required.
**Step 3: Confirm Reactivation**

- 
Click **'Submit'** to confirm reactivation. Once submitted, reactivation will take effect immediately (status will change from **'In Progress'** to **'Completed'**

**C. Automatic Suspension and Manual Payment (Post-Failure)**

In case of a failed auto-payment:

- The suspension is delayed (e.g., set to happen after 6 hours).
- If the customer pays manually¬†*before*¬†the scheduled suspension time:
The manual payment is processed.
- The suspension will be prevented, and the customer will never be suspended.

- If payment fails, the customer can be sent a¬†**payment link**¬†via email or chat to manually pay. The customer must then pay manually.

---

#### eSIM Replacement
*Article ID: 43019589278875 | Updated: 2025-11-07*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/43019589278875-eSIM-Replacement*

**IMPT:**

- **A subscriber can download the eSIM only once. If they delete it by mistake, they need a new one.**
- **The plan remains active, but a new eSIM must be issued.**
¬†

In cases of subscribers reaching out to request for eSIM replacement, below are the steps for L0:

- Click on the three dots **(...)** next to the SIM details.
- 
Select **'Replace eSIM'**.

- 
On the screen that opens, select 'Continue'. ¬†Note that 'SIM offering' is selected by default.

- 
On the next screen **'eSIM' **is by default selected, click **'Continue'**.

- 
Confirm charge (if there's any, currently free of charge).

¬†

- The order is submitted, and the **user must be told it will take a few minutes for the new eSIM email to arrive.**

- 
The subscriber will receive a QR code to scan, install, and activate.

### eSIM issues

#### eSIM Stuck in "Activating"
*Article ID: 44455404526747 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455404526747-eSIM-Stuck-in-Activating*

**eSIM Stuck in "Activating" status**

¬†

### **Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**
- **Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance**
- 
**Confirm:**

**Duration:** How long has it been stuck?.
- 
**Internet Connection:** Is the device connected to stable Wi-Fi?
- 
**Device Lock:** Is the device Carrier Unlocked?

- **Take an alternate contact number.**
- **Add all relevant notes in ConnectX.**
### **Step 3 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Check eSIM Status, if it's active or inactive. - ConnectX

[e-SIM Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600946917019-e-SIM-Status-e-SIM-Replacement-ConnectX)

2
Check for similar outage tickets - Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

¬†

**Step 4 - Troubleshooting Steps to be done (L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)

- 
**Check complete ticket history and past conversations**Determine if this is a new installation or if the customer deleted and tried to reinstall an old eSIM.

- 
**Check internal notes on the account in ConnectX**

**Verify Plan Status:** Ensure the plan is "Active" on the backend, even if the phone is stuck.
- 
**Device Swap Check:** Did the customer recently change devices? (This often causes IMEI mismatches).

- 
**Verify IMEI & EID are correct**
Ask the customer to go to **Settings > General > About** (iOS) or **Settings > About Phone > Status** (Android).
- Read back the last 4 digits of the **IMEI** and **EID**. Match these against the details in ConnectX to ensure the eSIM was generated for the correct hardware.

- 
**Delete OLD or DUPLICATE profiles**
Ask the customer to check their SIM manager list.
- If there are expired travel eSIMs or failed previous attempts (often labeled "Secondary", "Personal", or "Travel"), they must be **Deleted/Removed**.

- 
**Ensure the eSIM is set as Primary for Data / Voice**
Go to **Settings > Cellular / Mobile Data**.
- Select the **Mobile Data** option and ensure the **Meow Mobile** eSIM is selected (even if it says Activating)..

- 
**Update Carrier Settings**

**iOS:** Go to **Settings > General > About**. Wait on this screen for 15-30 seconds. If a pop-up appears saying "Carrier Settings Update," tap **Update**.
- 
**Android:** Settings > Network > Internet > Top right menu > Carrier settings version.

- 
**Force Network Settings Reset**

*Warning:* Inform the customer this forgets Wi-Fi passwords.
- 
**iOS:** Settings > General > Transfer or Reset > Reset > **Reset Network Settings**.
- 
**Android:** Settings > System > Reset Options > **Reset Wi-Fi, mobile & Bluetooth**.

- 
**Re-provision eSIM (Agent Action)**In ConnectX, re-issue a new eSIM to the customer.

### **Step 5 - Providing the ETR to customer**
- **Inform the customer that backend verification may be required**
- 
**Provide a standard ETR ****(Needs to be checked with L1)**

- **Assure proactive update once the provisioning clears.**
### **Step 6 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk -**
- Ensure all mandatory fields are filled and tagged before escalating.
- Set correct Ticket Priority based on impact (High).
- Add complete internal escalation notes
*Note:* Explicitly state "IMEI/EID Verified" and "Network Settings Reset performed."

- Attach all screenshots (Showing the "Activating" status and Device Settings).
- Transfer the chat to L1 queue and not a particular agent.¬†
- Change ticket status to **On-hold**, i.e., **Escalated to L1**

**Details to be provided to L1: (Confirmed Mandatory)**

- Validated IMEI & EID
- Confirmation of Network Settings Reset (Yes/No)
- List of other eSIMs currently on device (if any)
- Screenshot of Error/Status
- Time of Re-provisioning attempt

#### eSIM Device Compatibility Check
*Article ID: 44455336528667 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455336528667-eSIM-Device-Compatibility-Check*

## **SOP - eSIM Device Compatibility Check**This SOP outlines the steps an L0 agent should take to confirm if a customer's device supports eSIM technology and is ready for activation.

- **Probing and Empathy -¬†**
- Acknowledge the importance of device compatibility: "That's a great question; let's confirm your device is ready for eSIM."
- 
Ask the customer for the **exact device name and model number** (e.g., iPhone 13 Pro, Samsung Galaxy S23 Ultra, Google Pixel 7).

¬†

- ### **External Compatibility Check -¬†**
- Use the internal **Device Compatibility Database (eSIM compatibility Sheet - **[**Device List**](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1aQprKiTQjvw90TwCjrybco-D8uRrYG4AbikX0cZuVec/edit?gid=0#gid=0)**)** to search for the specific model provided by the customer.
- You can also refer to Google to determine device eSIM compatibility.
- 
**Confirm two key criteria:**
The model is listed as **eSIM compatible**.
- 
The device is **unlocked** (or locked to *this* carrier).

¬†

- ### **Internal Device Verification (Guided Customer Check) -¬†**
- Guide the customer to check the device settings themselves, as this verifies the physical eSIM component is functional and ready.
- 
**For iPhone (iOS):**
Go to **Settings** ‚Äî **General** ‚Äî **About**.
- Look for the **"EID"** (Embedded Identity Document) number.
- 
**If EID is present:** The device is eSIM-compatible.
- 
**If EID is missing or says "Unavailable":** The device may not support eSIM or the feature is disabled (often the case for some region-specific models, e.g., dual-physical SIM models).

- 
**For Android (Varies by Manufacturer):**

**Method 1 (Samsung/Pixel):** Go to **Settings** ‚Äî **Connections/Network & Internet** ‚Äì **SIM Card Manager/Mobile Network**.
- Look for an option like **"Add mobile plan"** or **"Add eSIM."**

- 
**Method 2 (General):** Dial ***#06#** on the phone app.
- Look for the **"EID"** number displayed on the screen.
- 
**If the option/EID is present:** The device is eSIM-compatible.

¬†

- **Conclusion and Next Steps -¬†**
- 
**Case A: Device is Compatible:**
**Action:** Confirm the device supports eSIM and proceed directly to the eSIM QR code delivery or activation process.

- 
**Case B: Device is NOT Compatible (No EID/Not on List):**

**Action:** Politely inform the customer that based on the model or the check results, the device does not appear to support eSIM functionality.
- 
**Suggestion:** Advise the customer to confirm with the device manufacturer or use a different, known-compatible device.

---

#### QR Code Re-Issuance
*Article ID: 44455117766299 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455117766299-QR-Code-Re-Issuance*

**QR Code Re-Issuance: eSIM ‚Äì Not Downloadable / QR Expired / QR Already Used / Device Changed**

**L0 Action -**

### **Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**
- Acknowledge the concern and reassure assistance
- Confirm:
Why QR re-issuance is required
- Whether the QR was ever scanned successfully
- Exact error message received while scanning (if any)

- Confirm:
New device model (if device changed)
- OS version (Android / iOS)

- Take an **alternate contact number**

- Confirm registered **email address for sending new QR (needs to be same as the registered email ID)**

- Add all relevant notes in **ConnectX**

### **Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Verify IMEI & ICCID Mapping - ConnectX

[e-SIM Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600946917019-e-SIM-Status-e-SIM-Replacement-ConnectX) - **Step 5**

2
Check Failed Payment Status - ConnectX

[Check Payment Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44605895175451-Check-Payment-Status-ConnectX)

3
Check for any bulk QR / activation incidents (Multiple requests done by the customer on Zendesk)

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

### **Step 4 - Troubleshooting / Validation Steps (Before Re-Issuance) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)
- Review complete ticket history and any prior eSIM/activation interactions on **Zendesk.**

- Check all **internal notes in ConnectX**

- Verify current eSIM status:
QR Issued ‚Äì Yes/No
- QR Scanned ‚Äì Yes/No
- Activation Completed ‚Äì Yes/No

- Identify reason for re-issuance:
QR expired
- QR already used
- QR not downloading
- Customer changed device
- Accidental eSIM deletion

- Confirm plan status (Active / Pending Activation / Suspended)
- Check if any **previous QR re-issuance was already done on ConnectX.**

****

- **Note: **Check if there are more than one QR Code issuance emails sent to the customer other than the one sent while Onboarding for the first time.
- Confirm customer is using a **supported eSIM device (**[**Device List**](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1aQprKiTQjvw90TwCjrybco-D8uRrYG4AbikX0cZuVec/edit?gid=0#gid=0)**)**

- Ensure customer:
Has stable Wi-Fi connection
- Is not using a VPN
- Has not already installed another active eSIM profile

- Ask customer to:
Delete any **partially installed eSIM profile**

- Restart the device

- If QR failed earlier:Ask for a **screenshot of the error**

- Confirm storage is available on the device
- Reconfirm that the customer is ready to install the eSIM immediately after QR re-issue
### **Step 5 - QR Code Re-Issuance from ConnectX *****(Only if L0 access is enabled)***
- Open customer profile in **ConnectX**

- Select **Products ‚Üí eSIM Details ‚Üí Click on 3-dots ‚Üí Send eSIM QR Code**

- Verify:
Correct MSISDN / Order ID
- Correct registered email ID

- Trigger **New QR Code Generation**

- Send QR to:Registered Email

- Add internal note:‚ÄúNew QR re-issued on [date/time] via ConnectX‚Äù

*(If L0 is not authorized ‚Üí Proceed directly to L1 escalation.)*

### **Step 6 - Installation Guidance to Customer**
- Guide customer to:
Settings ‚Üí Mobile Network ‚Üí Add eSIM
- Scan the newly issued QR
- Complete installation

- Ask customer to:Restart the device post-installation

- Confirm:
Network appears
- Signal bars are visible

- If activation is delayed:Inform standard activation TAT (TBD)

### **Step 7 - Providing the TAT to Customer**
- For QR only: **Immediate to XX minutes**

- For activation post QR: **XX hours (As per activation SLA)**

- Inform customer that the old QR will become **invalid automatically**

### **Step 8 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk -**(Escalate only if QR regeneration is blocked or activation fails after re-issue)

- Ensure all mandatory fields are completed
- Apply correct **eSIM / QR / Activation Tags**

- Set correct **Ticket Priority**

- Add detailed **internal escalation notes**

- Attach all **error screenshots**

- Change ticket status to **On-Hold if Escalated to L1**

## **Details to be provided to L1: (Confirmed Mandatory)**
- **Registered Email Address**
- **Registered Mobile Number / Order ID**
- **Reason for QR Re-Issuance**
- **Device Model + OS Version**
- 
**Old QR Status** (Unused / Partially Used / Expired)
- **Date & Time of Original QR Issuance**
- **IMEI & ICCID (If Available)**
- **Error Message While Scanning (If Any)**
- **Screenshots of Error / Failure**

#### QR Code Expired
*Article ID: 44455038259355 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455038259355-QR-Code-Expired*

**QR Code Expired / Invalid - Unable to Install eSIM**

**L0 Action -**

### **Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**
- **Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance**
- 
**Confirm:**

**Has this code been scanned before?** Even once? (e.g., "Did you try scanning it yesterday and it failed, or is this the very first try?")
- 
**Are they trying to move the eSIM to a new phone?** (Standard QR codes are one-time use and cannot be transferred by re-scanning).

- **Take an alternate contact number and email if available.**
**Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
ICCID Status Check: Look at the specific ICCID (SIM number). - ConnectX

[e-SIM Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600946917019-e-SIM-Status-e-SIM-Replacement-ConnectX)

2
Check for Similar Ongoing Tickets - Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

¬†

**Step 3 - Troubleshooting Steps to be done (L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)

- 
**Check internal notes on the account in **[**ConnectX**](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1-rfMRbeoi3NYOiNDXZewcLf3w9Ii5KQv4N7ZCcuhdvg/edit?tab=t.0)

**Verify Order Date:** Check when the eSIM was purchased.¬†

(QR can be scanned only once, even if the activation was not successful)

- 
**Verify Activation Status : eSIM status on **[**ConnectX**](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1k7ihp0sC5sig2ex0ZQjXg8bywu8CUpNyTzHiPzS_qUc/edit?tab=t.0#heading=h.r621ahwcme2v)

- 
**Check Device Model in History : **Did the customer recently mention switching phones or upgrading their device?
- 
**The "Already Installed" Check**

*iPhone:* Settings > Cellular. Look under "SIMs". Is there a line with no number, or labeled "Secondary"? Tap it and check if the ICCID matches the order.
- 
*Android:* Settings > Network & Internet > SIMs. Look for "Downloaded SIM" or a generic carrier name.
- 
*If found:* The error is correct. The user just needs to **Turn On** that line and enable Roaming. They do *not* need to scan again.

- 
**Check Internet Connection**Ensure the user is on strong Wi-Fi. A dropped packet during the first handshake can sometimes "burn" the code without finishing the install on the phone.

- 
**Device Compatibility Check**Verify the device is **Carrier Unlocked** (Settings > General > About > Carrier Lock: "No SIM restrictions"). Locked phones often throw generic "Invalid Plan" or "Expired" errors.

- 
**Restart Device**Restarting clears a temporary cache that might be blocking the camera from recognizing the code format.

### **Step 4 - Re-issuing a new e-SIM to the customer from ConnectX. - Refer to **[**eSIM QR Code Generation**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454985470747)- As the QR has expired or is not working, we can go ahead and re-issue a new QR code.¬†### 
¬†

### **Step 5 - Escalate to L1:**
If the issue still persists after re-issuing a new e-SIM, this issue must be escalated to L1 to further check all the details.
- Ensure all mandatory fields are completed
- Set correct **Ticket Priority based on impact***** (High)***

- Add detailed **internal notes (Zendesk)**

- Attach all screenshots and customer confirmations
- Change ticket status to **On-hold if escalated to L1**

- Activation **Attempt Statu**s (Success/Failure/Error)
- 
**Date & time the QR code **was sent
- Are they trying to move the** eSIM** to a new phone? Yes/No

---

#### eSIM QR Code Generation
*Article ID: 44454985470747 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454985470747-eSIM-QR-Code-Generation*

**eSIM QR Code Generation**

This SOP details the process for provisioning the eSIM for the customer by the support agent via the internal tool (ConnectX).

### **Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer (Before Request)**Acknowledge the request and confirm the details for a smooth transition.

- 
**Confirm:**

**The device is currently connected to Wi-Fi** (Crucial for successful eSIM download/installation).
- Inform them about the **steps to scan/install** the eSIM on their device. Also, ensure that customers do not interrupt the phone while the installation progresses.

- 
**Educate the Customer:**Explain that a new **QR code **will be sent to their registered email address.

### **Step 2 - Initiating the eSIM Request (Action Steps)**The action taken depends on the customer's preference or if the agent needs to initiate it directly.

**Request Method**
**L0 Action in ConnectX/Customer Navigation on App**
**Next Expected Outcome**

**Customer Via App**

**Guide the Customer:** Instruct the customer to navigate the App: **Settings >> SIM/Service Management >> Request eSIM. (****Tentative****) ****(****Avoid referring to this step until further confirmation from the team****)**

System processes request; QR code sent to the customer's registered email.

**Agent Via ConnectX**

**Use the Internal eSIM Provisioning Tool:**¬†

Product >> Sim details >> Send eSim QR Code
System processes request and the same can be checked in ConnectX( Interactions)

¬†

### **Step 3 - Tools to analyze and handle (Post-Request)**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Verify that QR code has been sent - ConnectX

[Check Interactions](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600611412123-Check-Interactions-ConnectX)

¬†

### **Step 4 - Troubleshooting and Escalation Check - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)If the eSIM is **Not Installed** after the request, proceed to troubleshoot :

- **Check complete ticket history and past conversations (if any).**
- 
**Verify Customer Eligibility:**
Confirm the customer's **Device Model** is officially supported for eSIM ***(Dail*#06#)***.
- Ensure the customer's **Account Status is Active** and in good standing.

- 
**Review Current Provisioning Status in ConnectX:**
Check if an active eSIM profile already exists. **(Products >> Sim Details)**

- Check for any **recent or pending eSIM requests** (Interactions >> Communication log).

- 
**Installation Failure:** Record and document any specific **Error Codes** the customer reports during installation, such as "Invalid Code" or "Cannot Add Data Plan."
- 
**Device Lock:** If the customer is porting or migrating, verify that their device is **unlocked** and not linked to a different carrier.
- 
**Data Connectivity:** Before the customer begins the eSIM installation, please ensure the following:
The customer's **Wi-Fi connection is stable** and has sufficient strength for the download.
- Remind the customer not to interrupt the installation process once the QR code has initiated the eSIM download.

### **Step 5 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk**If the request fails to process in ConnectX and installation fails with an error code:

- **Ensure all mandatory fields are filled.**
- Set correct **Ticket Priority** (high priority, as service is not activated).
- Add complete internal escalation notes, clearly stating:
- **Failure summary( QR code shared, error message/code)**
- 
**Attach all relevant screenshots** (e.g., ConnectX status screen showing "Failed to Provision").
- Change ticket status to **On-hold (L1 support team).**

#### **Details to be provided to L1/Technical Team: (Confirmed Mandatory)**
- **Device Model + OS Version.**
- **Customer Account Number/ID.**
- **Time & Date of the eSIM Request Attempt.**
- **ConnectX Provisioning Status at time of escalation.**
- 
**Error Codes or System Messages** (If any).

#### QR code not received
*Article ID: 44454944958107 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454944958107-QR-code-not-received*

### **QR code not received after account onboarding**### **Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance. This is a common issue when setting up new services.

- 
**Confirm:**
When the eSIM was ordered/requested/account was created.
- Whether the customer checked the spam/junk folder.
- If the customer sees any record of the email delivery.

- Take an **alternate contact number **from the customer.
### **Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
eSIM order/request submission status - ConnectX

[Check Recent Orders & Activities](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600701856155-Check-Recent-Orders-Activities-ConnectX)

2
Contact information (email address, mobile number) is correct in the system for QR code delivery - ConnectX

[View Customer Details & Address](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44601143075995-View-Personal-Details-Address-ConnectX)

3
Check for similar outage tickets - Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

¬†

### **Step 3 - Troubleshooting Steps to be done (L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)The focus is on resolving the delivery/provisioning of the eSIM profile.

- Check complete ticket history and past conversations.
- Review all previous troubleshooting already performed (If any).
- Check internal notes on the account in ConnectX.
- Confirm system status: Verify that eSIM status shows Not Active, Installation status - shows Not Installed, and the QR Code status shows Not Received in the system.
- 
**Check Device Compatibility (Probing):**
Confirm the customer is using an **eSIM-compatible device (*#06#).**

- Ask the customer for their **Device Model + OS Version.**

- 
**Re-send QR Code/Activation Details:**

Attempt to **re-trigger the delivery of the QR code or activation link/details** to the confirmed, correct email address/mobile number on file through ConnectX.¬†

(Go to Product - Click on Product Detail - Click 3 dots Icon in SIM detail section - send eSIM QR code)

- 
**Instruct the customer to check their spam/junk folder** and confirm receipt.

- 
**Guided Installation Check (If QR is received):**
If the QR code is successfully received, **guide the customer through the installation process step-by-step:**

- Note down any **error codes or system messages** during the installation.

### **Step 4 - Providing the ETR to customer**
- If the re-sending of the QR code/activation details resolves the issue, confirm successful activation and connection.
- If the QR code fails to generate or deliver, or if the installation fails with an error:
Inform the customer that **backend verification and possible manual provisioning may be required.**

- Provide a standard ETR of: **0-1 hour**

- Assure **proactive update** once L1 investigation is completed.

### **Step 5 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk**
- **Ensure all mandatory fields are filled.**
- Apply correct **Primary & Secondary Tags** (e.g., eSIM, Activation, QR Not Received).
- Set correct **Ticket Priority** based on the impact (e.g., total service outage).
- Add complete **internal escalation notes**, detailing all steps taken (especially the re-trigger attempt) and the confirmed delivery channel.
- Attach all **screenshots** (e.g., customer showing they checked spam, or system error from failed re-trigger).
- Change ticket status to **On-Hold if escalated to L1.**

#### **Details to be provided to L1: (Confirmed Mandatory)**
- 
**Device Model + OS Version** (Confirming compatibility)
- **Customer Location (Pincode/Area)**
- **Time & Date of Initial eSIM Request/Order.**
- 
**Results of QR Code Re-send Attempt** (Success/Failure/Customer did not receive).
- 
**Error Codes or System Messages** (If any during re-send or manual installation attempt).

## Payments and Refunds 

### Payment related issues

#### eSIM installed but not activated and requests refund
*Article ID: 44457844920219 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44457844920219-eSIM-installed-but-not-activated-and-requests-refund*

## **eSIM installed but not activated and requests refund**### **L0 Action ‚Äì **Verify activation failure, confirm refund eligibility, initiate refund correctly from the system, and provide accurate refund confirmation & TAT to the customer.## **Step 1 ‚Äì Probing & Empathizing with the Customer**
- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance.
- Confirm with the customer:
When the eSIM was installed.
- What exact issue is seen during activation.
- Whether any **error code** appears.
- Device model & OS version.
- Whether the device is carrier unlocked.

- Confirm clearly that the customer:
**Wants to proceed with a refund instead of further troubleshooting**.

- Reconfirm:
That the service has **never been successfully activated**.
- That **no calls, data, or SMS have worked** on this eSIM.

## **Step 2 ‚Äì Tools to Analyze & Handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Verify eSIM Status, Activation failure, Plan attached to MSISDN, That the plan is unused and inactive - ConnectX

[e-SIM Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600946917019-e-SIM-Status-e-SIM-Replacement-ConnectX)

2
Check Payment Status - ConnectX

[Check Payment Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44605895175451-Check-Payment-Status-ConnectX)

3
Similar open tickets on activation failure refunds - Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

## **Step 3 ‚Äì Troubleshooting Confirmation (Before Refund ‚Äì Mandatory L0 Check) **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)
- Check complete ticket history and past conversations on** Zendesk**.
- Review all previous activation troubleshooting steps performed.
- Check internal notes on the account in **ConnectX**

- Confirm system status:
eSIM status - **Installed**

- Activation status - **Not Active**

- Network status - **Not Working**

- Verify:
Plan purchase date & time.
- Payment status - **Successful**

- Any prior L1 provisioning attempts.

- Confirm there is **no active suspension, abuse flag, or KYC block**.
- Confirm that:
QR installation was successful but **activation never completed**.
- Network never registered on the device.
- Activation retry (if any) did **not succeed**.

- If customer is **firm on refund** and does not want further activation attempts:Proceed with refund initiation.

- If activation is still technically possible and customer agrees:
Follow standard ‚Äú[eSIM Installed but Not Activated](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454558535067)‚Äù SOP.
- Only proceed to refund if the customer declines further troubleshooting.

## **Step 4 ‚Äì Refund Initiation Procedure - Escalate to Supervisor/Viru**### **System Steps (Refund Process):**
- 
**Search for the customer‚Äôs profile** in the system.
- Navigate to the **Payments tab**.
- 
**Select the payment** for which refund is to be initiated.
- Click on the **3 dots (‚ãÆ)**.
- Select **Refund**.
- 
**Enter the refund amount**.
- 
**Mention the reason for refund (Mandatory)**
Reason to use: *‚ÄúeSIM Installed but Not Activated ‚Äì Service Unusable‚Äù*

- 
**Cross-check and confirm to the customer**:
Refunds will be initiated to the **same card used for payment**.
- Confirm the **last four digits of the card** with the customer.

- Click **Refund Customer**.

- Confirm in the system that **refund status shows Initiated**.## **Step 5 ‚Äì Providing the TAT to the Customer**
- Inform the customer that:
The refund has been **successfully initiated**.
- The amount will be credited back to the **original payment card**.

- Provide standard refund TAT:
**5‚Äì7 business days**.

- Advise the customer to:
Monitor their bank statements.
- Contact support again only if the amount is not received after TAT

## **Step 6 ‚Äì Ticket Closure & Documentation (Zendesk ‚Äì L0)**
- Add complete internal notes including:
Installation confirmed but activation failed.
- The customer opted for a refund.
- Refund transaction ID / reference number.
- Refund amount.
- Last four digits of the customer‚Äôs card (masked).
- Date & time of refund initiation.

- Update ticket status to:
**Solved** (if refund initiated successfully).

#### Payment Issues-Payment Status (Customer‚Äôs End)- Double Debit, Payment Status (ConnectX)- Received Both
*Article ID: 44457698753051 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44457698753051-Payment-Issues-Payment-Status-Customer-s-End-Double-Debit-Payment-Status-ConnectX-Received-Both*

**Double Debit, Received Both on ConnectX**

This SOP addresses the issue where the customer's bank statement shows two debits for the same transaction/billing cycle, and ConnectX confirms that both payments have been successfully received and credited to the account.

### **Step 1- Probing, Empathizing with the customer**Acknowledge the concern regarding the double debit and assure the customer that since both payments are confirmed as received, a refund will be processed promptly.

- 
**Confirm:**
**The exact amount of the double payment.**
- 
**The date and time of the debits** from their end (if known).
- 
**The payment method used** (e.g., Credit Card, Debit Card, UPI, Bank Transfer).

- 
**Request Documentation (screenshot):**Politely request the customer to provide a **screenshot or official document (bank statement)** clearly showing the **two separate debits** for the same amount/transaction reference.

**Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Verify the excess credit balance on the customer's account.(Payments>>payment history) - ConnectX

[Check Payment Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44605895175451-Check-Payment-Status-ConnectX)

### **Step 3 - Escalating to Supervisor/Viru - Steps to be completed on Zendesk**
- **Ensure all mandatory fields are filled.**
- Set correct **Ticket Priority** (usually high priority due to financial implications).
- Add complete **internal escalation notes**, clearly stating:
**Amount to be Refunded**
- Refund to Source.
- 
**ConnectX Confirmation:** Both payments received (List Transaction IDs/References).

- 
**Attach the customer's provided documentation** (bank statement/screenshot showing the double debit).
- Change ticket status to **On-Hold if Escalated to Supervisor/Viru.**

#### **Details to be provided to L1/Finance: (Confirmed Mandatory)**
- **Customer Account Number/ID.**
- **Amount to be Refunded.**
- **Date and Time of both successful payments as per ConnectX.**
- **Transaction IDs/Reference Numbers for Both Payments.**
- 
**Payment Method Used** (Original Source of Payment).
- **Customer's Documentation attached (Proof of Double Debit).**

#### Payment Unsuccessful: Autopay ‚Äì Enabled, Funds ‚Äì Available
*Article ID: 44457693627931 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44457693627931-Payment-Unsuccessful-Autopay-Enabled-Funds-Available*

**Payment Unsuccessful: Autopay ‚Äì Enabled, Funds ‚Äì Available, Payment ‚Äì Failed, Status ‚Äì Not Received in ConnectX**

¬†

**Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**

- Acknowledge the concern and reassure assistance
- Check complete ticket history and any previous billing-related interactions on ***Zendesk***.
- Verify:

- *Autopay status is Enabled (**As autopay is mandatory.**)*
- *Correct payment method is saved*

- Confirm:
Date & time when the payment was ***attempted/successful/failed*** (If any screenshot).
- Whether the customer received any **bank/SMS/app alert **(If any screenshot).

- Reconfirm with the customer that:
Sufficient balance was available at the time of debit
- The same payment method usually works

- Take an **alternate contact number or email** for follow-up
**Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Check payment transaction logs

[Check Payment Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44605895175451-Check-Payment-Status-ConnectX)

2
Verify subscription billing cycle and next retry date

3
Check for any active billing/payment outage tickets

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

¬†

**Step 3 - Troubleshooting / Validation Steps to be done (Standard L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)

- Ask customer to:Reconfirm that the **same bank/card is active and not blocked**

- Verify if a customer received a new card with the same card numbers.
- Ensure autopay consent is still **active and not revoked**

- Advise customer **not to attempt multiple payments** until backend validation is completed (to avoid duplicate debits)
- If everything seems to be okay then send **‚ÄúAdd another card link‚Äù **to the Customer from **ConnectX. **This will help customers to add another card or payment method for making the payment.
**Go to Payments > Select the failed Payment from the payment history tab and Click on the 3 dots > Click on Customer portal link > Send Link via Email.**

****

**Step 4 - Providing the ETR to customer**

- Provide a **standard ETR of: 1-2 hours (TBD as per billing SLA)**
**If Still Unresolved:**

**Step 5 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk -¬†**

- Ensure all mandatory billing fields are completed
- Apply correct **Primary & Secondary Billing Tags**

- Set correct **Ticket Priority based on service impact**

- Add detailed **internal escalation notes with transaction timeline**

- Attach all **payment proof / bank screenshots** provided by the customer
- Change ticket status to **On-Hold if escalated to L1 (High)**

**Details to be provided to L1: (Confirmed Mandatory)**

- **Registered Email Address**
- **Registered Mobile Number**
- 
**Autopay Payment Method Type** (Card / Bank / Wallet ‚Äì if applicable)
- **Date & Time of Failed Payment Attempt**
- **Last Successful Payment Date & Amount**
- **Plan Name & Billing Cycle**
- **Bank / Card Reference Number (If Available)**
- **Customer Bank Screenshot (If Debited / Pending)**
- **Payment Status in ConnectX (Exact Wording)**
- 
**Any Error Message Shown to Customer (If Any)**

#### Payment status on Customer‚Äôs end - Successful, Status on ConnectX - Not received
*Article ID: 44457654016027 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44457654016027-Payment-status-on-Customer-s-end-Successful-Status-on-ConnectX-Not-received*

**Payment status on Customer‚Äôs end - Successful,¬†**

**Status on ConnectX - Not received.¬†**
¬†

### **Step 1 - Visual Audit**
- Check complete ticket history and past conversations on **Zendesk**Review if the customer has reported payment delays previously or if there are multiple tickets open for the same issue.

- Check internal notes on the account in ConnectX
- Verify Account Balance & Plan StatusConfirm if the account balance has updated despite the transaction record missing, or if the plan dates have shifted.

**Step 2 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**

- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance
- Confirm:
Exact time and date the payment was made.
- Payment Method used (Credit Card, Debit Card, PayPal, Apple/Google Pay).
- If they received a confirmation email/SMS from *us* (the carrier) or only from their *bank*.
- If the transaction status in their banking app says "Posted/Successful" or "Pending/Processing."

- Take an **alternate contact number** from the customer.
- Add all relevant notes in **ConnectX**.
### **Step 3 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Check the "Payments" tab for any failed, declined, or pending entries matching the amount.
[Check Payment Status on ConnectX](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44605895175451-Check-Payment-Status-ConnectX)

2
Ensure the account hasn't been suspended due to the delay.
[Check Account Status on ConnectX](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600349458331-Check-Account-Status-ConnectX)

3
Check for similar open tickets
[Similar Ongoing tickets on Zendesk](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

¬†

### **Step 4 - Troubleshooting Steps to be done (L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)
- Refresh Account SessionAsk the customer to log out of the App/Website and log back in (forces a refresh of the dashboard data).

- Verify "Pending" vs "Posted"Ask the customer to confirm if the money has actually left the account or is in a "reserved/pending" state.

- Request Proof of PaymentAsk the customer to locate the Transaction ID / Reference Number, Full request/response payloads are captured along with HTTP status, error code, and payment method used (or screenshot the debit notification).

- Check for Double PaymentEnsure the customer hasn‚Äôt been charged twice for the same amount.

**Step 5 - Providing the ETR to customer**

- Inform the customer that backend verification is required
- Provide a standard ETR -¬† Yet to be decided/confirmed by L1.¬†

- Assure proactive update once the L1 team traces the Transaction ID.
### **Step 6 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk -**
- Ensure all mandatory fields are tagged.
- Set correct Ticket Priority based on impact.
- Add complete internal escalation notes
- Attach all screenshots and proofs
- Change ticket status to On-hold, i.e., Escalated to L1
**Details to be provided to L1: (Confirmed Mandatory)**

- Customer ID / Account Number
- Transaction ID / Reference Number (Mandatory for tracing)
- Date & Exact Time of Transaction
- Amount Paid
- Screenshot of Banking/Payment Confirmation
- Customer‚Äôs Email Address (used for payment notification)

#### How to Check Missed Payments?
*Article ID: 42174101294107 | Updated: 2025-12-18*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42174101294107-How-to-Check-Missed-Payments*

Updated:

### Situation:Customers typically ask this question when they‚Äôve received a payment reminder, see a ‚ÄúPending‚Äù or ‚ÄúSuspended‚Äù status in the Meow Wireless app, or experience restricted service.
In some cases, they might have missed their billing due date or had a failed auto-payment.

Agents may also encounter cases where the customer insists they already paid, but the system doesn‚Äôt show it ‚Äî requiring verification and potential escalation.

### Task:The agent‚Äôs goal is to determine whether the missed payment is due to a delay, a failed transaction, or a genuine non-payment, and guide the customer to resolve it.

Steps for Agents:

- 
Check the customer‚Äôs account in ConnectX:

Go to ConnectX > Customer360 > Search by email or phone number.

- Review the Account Status (Active, Pending, or Suspended).

- 
Open the Billing or Payments tab to check for:

Payment due date

- Outstanding balance

- Last successful payment date

- Failed transaction attempts (if any)

- 
Ask clarifying questions:

‚ÄúHave you received a payment reminder or notification from Meow Wireless?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúWhen did you last make a payment?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúWhich payment method did you use ‚Äî card, wallet, or other?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúDid you receive a confirmation email or in-app message after payment?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you currently seeing a suspended or limited access message in your Meow Wireless app?‚Äù

These questions help confirm whether the issue is due to non-payment, delayed posting, or system error.

### Action:#### If the payment is overdue (no recent transaction found):Explain the consequences of the missed payment and how to resolve it promptly.

Example Response:
‚ÄúIt looks like your last payment hasn‚Äôt been completed yet, which is why your account may be temporarily limited. You can quickly restore full access by paying your outstanding balance through the Meow Wireless app. Once payment is confirmed, your services should reactivate automatically within a few minutes.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Advise the customer to complete payment immediately via the Meow Wireless app.

- Remind them that delays beyond **7 days** may lead to service suspension.

- Tag the ticket accordingly.

#### If the customer claims payment was already made but it‚Äôs not visible in ConnectX:Acknowledge their concern and verify whether the payment is still processing or failed.

Example Response:
‚ÄúThanks for letting us know! I don‚Äôt see the payment reflected yet, but sometimes it can take up to 24‚Äì48 hours depending on your payment provider. Could you please share a screenshot or transaction reference number so we can verify it?‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Request proof of payment (screenshot or receipt).

- Check payment status.

- Escalate if payment remains unposted after 48 hours.

- Advise turnaround time of 24‚Äì48 hours for verification.

#### If the account is already suspended due to multiple missed payments:Explain the status clearly and provide reactivation steps.

Example Response:
‚ÄúIt looks like your account is currently suspended due to missed payments. The good news is, you can easily reactivate your service ‚Äî just settle the outstanding balance in your Meow Wireless app. Once payment is completed, your account will automatically be reactivated within a few minutes.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm the outstanding balance.

- Advise that services will be restored after payment confirmation.

- Add a note to monitor account status change.

- Tag ticket accordingly.

### Result:
- The customer understands the impact of missed payments on their service.

- They know how to resolve the issue quickly via the Meow Wireless app.

- Any unclear or disputed payments are escalated and verified properly.

### Additional Notes:
- Do not manually reactivate or adjust credits ‚Äî all updates must go through billing verification.

- Always verify that payment and account details match before escalating.

- Avoid confirming payment success without proof of transaction.

- 
**Escalate if:**

**Payment remains unposted after 48 hours.**

- **There‚Äôs a system mismatch between ConnectX and the Meow Wireless app.**

- **The customer reports multiple failed transactions.**

FAQs
[What happens if I miss my payment?](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42081961947035-What-happens-if-I-miss-my-payment)

### Refunds

#### Refund Initiation SOP
*Article ID: 44457870635419 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44457870635419-Refund-Initiation-SOP*

[pngtree-refund-concept-repayment-red-vector-png-image_13503324.png]## **Refund Initiation**### **L0 Action ‚Äì **Validate refund eligibility strictly as per policy, gather all mandatory details, and assign the ticket to the authorized refund approver (Supervisor or Viru) on Zendesk for final processing.¬†

**Step 1 ‚Äì Probing & Empathizing with the Customer**

- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance.
- Check complete ticket history and past conversations on **Zendesk.**

- 
**Verify**:
No chargeback already raised.
- No previous refund was already processed for the same transaction.

- 
**Confirm**:
Exact **reason for refund request**.
- **Date and purpose of payment**
- Need to verify whether the customer:
If Installed the eSIM &
- Activated the service.¬† ¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†

**Note:**
No refund is needed. Politely inform the customer why we cannot refund the amount.

**Set expectation clearly:**

- Refund approval is **policy-based** and processed only after **internal verification by the authorized team**.## **Step 2 ‚Äì Tools to Analyze & Handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Payment transaction ID & status.
[Check Payment Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44605895175451-Check-Payment-Status-ConnectX)

2

Product mapped to payment (Waitlist / User Plan).

TBC if the agent will be able to access waitlist info.- ConnectX

3
Account creation & activation date- ConnectX

[e-SIM Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600946917019-e-SIM-Status-e-SIM-Replacement-ConnectX)

4

¬†

eSIM status (Not Installed / Installed / Activated)-ConnectX

¬†

5
Next billing date-ConnectX

6
Similar ongoing or past ticket

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

## ## **Step 3 ‚Äì Refund Eligibility Validation**
**L0 Action: **Proceed to **Zendesk assignment to Supervisor/Viru**.### **‚úÖ Scenario 1 ‚Äì (After Launch) Paid Waitlist Fee & Did Not Convert as a User**
- **Refund Allowed**
- 
**L0 Action:**
Validate payment & non-conversion.
- Proceed to **Zendesk assignment to Supervisor/Viru**.

### **‚úÖ Scenario 2 ‚Äì (After Launch) Paid Waitlist Fee & Converted as a User**
- **Refund Auto-Processed**
- 
**L0 Action:**
Check refund status in the Payments tab.
- Inform customers of auto-refund and expected credit timeline.
- No manual escalation unless auto-refund is missing beyond TAT.

### **‚úÖ Scenario 3 ‚Äì (After Launch) Purchased as a User but Unable to Use / Changed Mind****¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†¬†Refund Allowed Only If ALL Conditions Are Met:**

- Account is **less than 30 days old**

- 
**No second payment** has been made
- **eSIM is NOT installed**
**L0 Action:**

- If all conditions are met ‚Üí Assign to **Supervisor/Viru**.
- If any condition fails ‚Üí Refund **Not Allowed** ‚Üí Explain policy clearly.
### **‚úÖ Scenario 4 ‚Äì Service Not Activated**
- **Refund Allowed**
- 
**L0 Action:**
Verify activation never completed.
- Assign ticket to **Supervisor/Viru** with proof.

### **‚úÖ Scenario 5 ‚Äì Installed & Activated**
- **Refund Not Allowed**
- 
**L0 Action:**Inform customers that post-installation & activation refunds are **not permitted**.

### **‚úÖ Scenario 6 ‚Äì Duplicate Payment**
- **Refund Allowed (Only for the Duplicate Transaction)**
- 
**L0 Action:**
Verify both successful transactions.
- Assign ticket to **Supervisor/Viru**.

**‚úÖ Scenario 7 ‚Äì If no payment record appears in ConnectX:**

**Example Response:**

‚ÄúI wasn‚Äôt able to locate your payment record in ConnectX.

Could you please share a screenshot or payment reference ID from your bank or wallet statement?

Once received, we‚Äôll verify it and process the refund if confirmed.‚Äù

**Next Steps for Agent:**

Request proof of payment (screenshot, transaction ID).

Forward details to Viru for manual lookup.

Follow up every 24 hours until refund status is confirmed.

Tag the ticket accordingly.

¬†

**Step 4 ‚Äì L0 Assignment to Authorized Refund Approver (Mandatory)**

¬†L0 must **NOT initiate refunds**.
L0 must only **assign the ticket for approval & execution**.

### **Zendesk Assignment Steps:**
- Open the ticket.
- Ensure the correct **refund eligibility scenario (1‚Äì6)** is selected.
Add **complete internal notes** with:
Scenario description.
- Refund eligibility result.
- Payment Transaction ID.
- Date & time of payment.
- Amount paid.
- eSIM status.
- Account age.

- 
**Assign the ticket to:**
**Supervisor** OR **Viru** (as per availability).

- Change ticket status to:**On-Hold ‚Äì Pending Refund Approval**

**Step 5 ‚Äì Customer Communication by L0**

- 
**Inform the customer that:**
The refund request has been **successfully submitted for internal approval**.
- An authorized team member will **process the refund after review**.

- 
**Share standard TAT:**
**5‚Äì7 business days after approval** (banking timeline).

## **Step 6 ‚Äì Ticket Closure Rules (L0)**
- 
**DO NOT close the ticket** once assigned to Supervisor/Viru.
- Keep status as:**On-Hold ‚Äì Pending Refund Processing**

- L0 may close the ticket **only after confirmation from Supervisor/Viru** that:
Refunds are processed.
- Refund reference number is updated in internal notes.

## **Escalation to Supervisor/Viru ‚Äì Mandatory Cases**
- All **eligible refund scenarios**.
- Any **system restriction where the refund option is missing**.
- 
**Duplicate payment cases**.
- 
**Auto-refund not received after expected TAT**.
### **‚úÖ Mandatory Details to Be Provided to Supervisor/Viru**
- Account/MSISDN
- Customer Name
- Scenario of refund¬†
- Payment Transaction ID
- Refund Amount
- Product Type (Waitlist/User)
- eSIM Status
- Account Age (Days)
- Screenshot of Payments Tab (if available)

#### SOP for every scenario

**SOPs For ConnectX**

¬†

### **1.SOP: Check Network Coverage Method 1:**** Via Customer 360 Menu**
- ### Step 1: Launch the ConnectX application.
- ### Step 2: Click on Customer 360 on the left side of the page
- ### Step 3: Navigate to the Residential Store.
- ### 
- ### Step 4: Click on the **Check **tab.
- ### 
- ### Step 5: Enter the customer's Zip Code to verify coverage.
- ### 
### **Method 2:**** Via Store Shortcut (Active Account)**
- ### Step 1: Ensure the Customer Account is currently open.
- ### Step 2: Click on the Store option on the right side of the page.
- ### 
- ### Step 3: Click on **Check**.
- ### 
- ### Step 4: Enter the customer's Zip Code to verify coverage.
- ### 
### **SOP: Check Usage**
- ### Step 1: Launch the ConnectX application.
- ### Step 2: Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.
- ### 
- ### Step 3: Click on the Products tab once the account is open.
- ### 
- ### Step 4: Select the Plan tab under the Products menu.
- ### 
- ### Step 5: Scroll down to the Usage section.
- ### Step 6: Use the filter options to view specific details for Data, Texts, or Calls, and select the desired Date Range.
- 
¬†

### **SOP: View Device IMEI Details**
- ### Step 1: Launch the ConnectX application.
- ### Step 2: Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.
- ### 
- ### Step 3: Click on the Products tab once the account is open.
- ### 
- ### Step 4: Select the Plan tab under the Products menu.
- ### 
- ### Step 5: Navigate to the Related Products section.
- ### 
- ### Step 6: Click on the Dropdown arrow to expand the section.
- ### 
- ### Step 7: Locate and view the Device IMEI (Note: The Activation Date of the account is also visible here).
- ### 
### **SOP: e-SIM Status & e-SIM Replacement**
- ### Step 1: Launch the ConnectX application or webpage.
- ### Step 2: Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.
- ### 
- ### Step 3: Click on the Products tab once the account is open.
- ### 
- ### Step 4: Select the Plan tab under the Products menu.

¬†

- ### Step 5: Verify if the e-SIM Status is Active or Inactive (Note: ICCID, IMSI, and PUK details are also visible in this section).
- ### Step 6: Click on the 3 dots (‚ãÆ) menu icon within the SIM Details section.
- ### 
- ### Step 7: Select Send Replacement e-SIM or Generate New e-SIM QR Code.
- ### 
- ### Step 8: Confirm the action (Note: The new QR code will be sent to the customer's registered email by default).

**SOP: Account Suspension**
- ### Step 1: Launch the ConnectX application or webpage.
- ### Step 2: Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.
- ### 
- ### Step 3: Click on the Products tab once the account is open.
- ### 
- ### Step 4: Select the Plan tab under the Products menu.
- ### 
- ### Step 5: Navigate to the Product Details section and click on the 3 dots (‚ãÆ) menu icon.
- ### 
- ### Step 6: Click on Suspension.
- ### 

- ### Step 7: Click on confirm for sure you want to suspend?
- ### 
- ### Step 8: Select the Reason for Suspension and add Notes in the section below it.
- ### 
- ### Step 9: Select the Suspension Date as End of the Cycle (Note: For Lost Device or Scam, select immediate/today's date).
### 

**SOP: Account Termination**
- Step 1: Launch the ConnectX application or webpage.
- Step 2: Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.
- 

- Step 3: Navigate to the Product Details section and click on the 3 dots (‚ãÆ) menu icon.
- 
- Step 4: Click on Terminate.
- 
- Step 5: Click on Confirm to finalize the account termination.

**SOP: Check Renewal Date**

¬†

- 
**Step 1:** Launch the ConnectX application.
- 
**Step 2:** Search for the customer account using their **Email ID**, **Phone Number**, or **Name**.
- 

- 
**Step 3:** Navigate to the **Account** tab and view the **Renewal Date** displayed next to the **Customer name**. We can also see the tenure of the account along with the activation date. 

**SOP: Initiate Refund**

¬†

- 
**Step 1:** Launch the ConnectX application.
- 
**Step 2:** Search for the customer account using their **Email ID**, **Phone Number**, or **Name**.
- 

- 
**Step 3:** Click on the **Payments** tab.
- 
- 
**Step 4:** Navigate to the **Payment History** section and choose the specific payment transaction to be refunded.
- 
- 
**Step 5:** Click on the **3 dots (‚ãÆ)** menu icon next to the transaction and select **Refund**.
-

#### What is ConnectX?
*Article ID: 42175830709531 | Updated: 2025-12-16*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42175830709531-What-is-ConnectX*

ConnectX is our internal admin platform that allows our team to view and manage customer accounts, subscriptions, and eSIM activations. It‚Äôs where we handle everything behind the scenes.

Key Functions

- View customer details and plan info
- Check billing, payment, and refund status
- Manage eSIM activations or replacements
- Track support history and account activity
- What It Doesn‚Äôt Show
- Rewards or referral data
- Vet care chat/session details
- App usage analytics

Why It Matters?

ConnectX helps agents deliver accurate, fast, and secure support by giving a full picture of each customer‚Äôs account and activity.

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Overview**

- Customer‚Äôs Products
- Billing History
- Insights

- Recent Orders Timeline
- Notes
- Open Carts

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Products**

- Number of Products
- Product Types
- Details
- SIM Details
- Related Products
- Product Attributes
- Product Orders Timeline
- Commitment Terms
- Usage (Data, Voice and SMS)
- Usage Details
- Resources
- Product Address
- Product Notes
- Agent Information

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Orders**

- Order Details

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Payment****s**

- Payment History
- Recurring Payment History
- Payment Methods

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Billing**

- Billing Accounts
Name
- State
- Billing Period
- Default Payment Method
- External Reference

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Interactions**

- Communication Log
- Date/Time
- Message Type
- Sent To
- Subject
- Action

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Customer Detail****s**

- Personal Details
- Contact Information
- Addresses
- Segments
- Account Information
- Attachments
- Self-Service Access
- Device Information
- Custom Attributes
- Port-Out PIN

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Associated Users**

- Associated Users
Name
- Email
- Products Number
- Status
- Last Login

- Add User

**C****ustomer 360¬∞ - Notes**

- Adding Notes
