### Zendesk

#### Using Macros & Shortcuts
*Article ID: 44559136955803 | Updated: 2025-12-18*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44559136955803-Using-Macros-Shortcuts*

## **Zendesk SOP ‚Äì Using Macros & Shortcuts**## **Purpose**This SOP explains how Zendesk agents should use **Macros** and **Shortcuts** to respond faster, maintain accuracy, and ensure a consistent Meow Mobile customer experience.

## **What Are Macros?**Macros are **pre-written canned responses** created for common customer questions, greetings, closing or scenarios. They help you reduce typing time, avoid errors, and maintain a consistent brand tone.

**Key points:**

- **Macros can only be used on email tickets.**
- Macros insert full responses instantly
- They may include instructions, troubleshooting steps, or next actions
- Macros are templates and must be reviewed before sending
## **What Are Shortcuts?**Shortcuts are **keyboard-triggered quick replies** (e.g., typing ‚Äú/‚Äù ‚Äúforward slash‚Äù followed by key phrase to pull up a response). They serve the same purpose as Macros but are faster to access during **live chats**.

**Key points:**

- **Shortcuts can only be used on Live Chats.**
- Shortcuts speed up live conversations
- They pull approved canned responses, Opening and Closing.
- Content must still be verified before sending
## **When to Use Macros or Shortcuts**Agents should use macros or shortcuts when:

- Greeting the Customer to reduce **FRT.**

- The customer issue is common or repetitive
- The question has a predefined, approved response
- Accuracy and consistency are important
- Speed is required (especially during live chat)
**Examples of suitable use cases:**

- Network or data troubleshooting
- eSIM installation guidance
- Port-in or port-out explanations
- Billing cycle or plan-related questions
- General account or service FAQs
## **When NOT to Use Macros Alone**Macros should not be sent blindly when:

- The customer issue is unique or complex
- Account-specific investigation is required
- The situation involves escalation or sensitive handling
In such cases, macros may be used as a base, but the response must be customized.

## **How to Use Macros in Zendesk**
- Open the customer ticket or chat
- Enter a forward slash ‚Äú/‚Äù on the chat box, or
- Click the **Macros** option or use the macro search
- Select the relevant macro based on the customer issue
- Insert the macro into the reply
## **How to Use Shortcuts in Zendesk**
- Place your cursor in the reply field
- Type forward slash ‚Äú/‚Äù followed by the shortcut keyword or trigger
- Select the appropriate canned response
- Insert it into the conversation
## **Mandatory Verification Before Sending**Macros and shortcuts are **starting points**, not final answers. Agents must always verify the content.

Before sending, ensure:

- The response matches the customer‚Äôs exact issue
- Any placeholders or variables are correctly filled
- Instructions align with the customer‚Äôs device or situation
- The tone remains warm, friendly, and on-brand
**Never send a macro without reviewing it first.**

## **Editing Macros for Accuracy**Agents are expected to:

- Remove any irrelevant steps
- Add missing context if required
- Adjust wording slightly to fit the conversation flow
- Ensure no incorrect assumptions are made
Macros should improve speed, not replace understanding.

## **Quality & Compliance Guidelines**
- Always read the full macro before sending
- Do not modify the core meaning unless required
- Do not add unapproved promises or timelines
- Ensure first-contact resolution whenever possible
## **Best Practices**
- Use macros to save time, not skip thinking
- Combine empathy with accuracy
- Keep responses clear and easy to understand
- If unsure, escalate rather than guessing
## **Summary**Macros and shortcuts are tools to help you respond faster and more accurately. When used correctly with verification and light customization they improve efficiency, consistency, and customer satisfaction while maintaining the Meow Mobile brand experience.

---

#### Zendesk Ticket Status Flow
*Article ID: 44456017457435 | Updated: 2025-12-16*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44456017457435-Zendesk-Ticket-Status-Flow*

### ***Zendesk Ticket Status Flow***¬†

**Status**
**When to Use**
**L0 Agent Mandatory Actions**
**Do Not Use When**

**New**
Ticket just created and not yet worked upon.

- Open ticket immediately
- Review customer context & history¬†
- Fill mandatory fields (Type, Category, Priority, Tags)

If you have already started working on the ticket

**Open**
Actively working on the ticket

- Acknowledge customer¬†
- Perform L0 troubleshooting¬†
- Add internal notes¬†
- Use KB & ConnectX¬†
- Keep customer updated

If waiting for customer reply or backend action

**Pending**
Waiting for customer response

- Clearly ask for required info/action¬†
- Add note on what is awaited¬†
- If the customer is unresponsive - A follow-up reminder is sent after 24 hours.
- If the customer doesn‚Äôt reply to the reminder email the ticket will be marked as auto-solved.

If waiting for L1/backend/system

**On-Hold**
Waiting for L1 / backend / system dependency

- Add escalation note¬†
- Mention expected ETR
- Inform customer of delay(if any)¬†
- Monitor for updates

If the customer is the one expected to respond

**Solved**
Issue resolved and final response sent

- Confirmed resolution¬†
- Send final update to customer¬†
- Ensure notes are complete

If issue is partially resolved or unconfirmed

**Closed**
System auto-closes the ticket after 5 days once ticket is Solved
- No action required
If further action is required (Closed tickets cannot be edited)

¬†

**CSAT Trigger Condition:** Customer Satisfaction (CSAT) surveys are only dispatched when tickets are manually marked as "solved." They will **not** be triggered for tickets that are automatically solved (in pending cases).

¬†

**Mandatory L0 Rules:**

- A ticket must **never remain in New after work begins**

- 
**Pending **means waiting for **Customer Action¬†**

- 
**On-Hold **means waiting for** Backend/L1 Action**

- **Solved only after resolution + final customer update**
- **Closed tickets cannot be reopened**

---

#### Usage of the integrated tools within Zendesk
*Article ID: 44455966908443 | Updated: 2025-12-16*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455966908443-Usage-of-the-integrated-tools-within-Zendesk*

# **SOP ‚Äì Usage of the integrated tools within Zendesk****Purpose:**
To ensure L0 agents correctly use the Extreme Right Panel in Zendesk to understand full customer context, avoid duplicate actions, provide accurate resolutions, and perform correct escalations.

**Responsibility:**
L0 agents are **mandatorily required** to review and use this panel for **every ticket before responding, resolving, or escalating**.

## **1. Customer Context****Contains:**

- Customer Email ID

¬†
- External Ticket ID

¬†
- Timestamp

¬†
- Language

¬†
- Internal Notes

¬†
- Complete Interaction History

¬†
**L0 Must:**

- Verify the **registered email ID** before taking any action

¬†
- Cross-check the **external ticket ID**

¬†
- Review **timestamp** to understand issue timeline

¬†
- Communicate in the **customer‚Äôs preferred language (English only)**

¬†
- Read **all existing internal notes**

¬†
- Review past history to:

¬†
Avoid repeating the same questions

¬†
- Understand if this is a **repeat issue**

¬†
- Ensure continuity in handling

¬†

**Mandatory Rule:**
No troubleshooting or escalation should begin **without reviewing Customer Context**.

## **2. Knowledge Panel****Function:**

- Shows **suggested Knowledge Bank articles**

¬†
- Allows **manual article search also**

¬†
**L0 Must:**

- First check **auto-suggested articles**

¬†
- Use the **search bar** if:

¬†
The issue is new

¬†
- The suggested article is not relevant

¬†

- Follow **only approved and latest articles**

¬†
- Apply the steps exactly as mentioned in the article

¬†
- Never share **internal-only KB articles** with customers

¬†
- If an article is incorrect/outdated:

¬†
Do not use it, search for the article that is relevant in the [Knowledge Bank](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us) directly.

¬†
- Inform the Supervisor

¬†

**Mandatory Rule:**
If the issue is resolvable at L0, it **must be handled through Knowledge guidance** before any escalation.

## **3. Side Conversations****Function:**

- Displays **other live/open tickets** of the same customer with other teams

¬†**L0 Must:**

- Check if:

¬†
The concern is already being handled

¬†
- Another team has provided an update

¬†

- Avoid:

¬†
Giving contradicting information

¬†
- Repeating backend actions already in progress

¬†

- Do **not** close or change status of another team‚Äôs ticket

¬†
- Add internal notes only in your **assigned ticket**

¬†
**Mandatory Rule:**
Always verify Side Conversations to **avoid duplicate escalations and parallel actions**.

## **4. Related Tickets****Function:**

- Displays **past and duplicate tickets** for the same concern

¬†
- Allows **ticket merging**

¬†
**L0 Must:**

- Check if the same issue was raised earlier

¬†
- Review:

¬†
What action was taken

¬†
- How the issue was resolved

¬†

- If a **duplicate active ticket** is found:

¬†
Merge it with the current ticket (Supervisor action)

¬†
- Add an internal note explaining the merge

¬†

- Only **true duplicates** should be merged

¬†
**Mandatory Rule:**
No new escalation should be created if a **related active ticket already exists**.

## **5. Apps Panel**### **5.1 MAVEN AGI Copilot**
- Provides AI-based response suggestions
- After confirming the copilot's response is correct and accurate, you can insert it directly into the messaging box.

¬†
- L0 Must:

¬†
Carefully read and validate the response

¬†
- Modify it as per customer case

¬†
- Never send AI responses without verification

¬†

¬†

### **5.2 Maven Recent Conversations**
- Shows last **5 tickets of the customer**

¬†
- L0 Must:

¬†
Review to check repetition of issues

¬†
- Avoid reopening already resolved matters unnecessarily

¬†

¬†

**This is how recent conversations in Maven are displayed within the panel.**

¬†

### **5.3 JIRA**
- Used only when:

¬†
A **confirmed technical defect** is identified

¬†
- All L0 troubleshooting is completed

¬†

- L0 Must:

¬†
Add correct issue summary

¬†
- Attach proper evidence

¬†
- Note the JIRA ID in Zendesk internal notes

¬†

### **5.4 Braze Email Viewer**
- Displays **all SMS and email communications** sent to the customer

¬†
- L0 Must:

¬†
Check if the customer:

¬†
Already received an update

¬†
- Already received system communication

¬†

- Avoid sending duplicate information

¬†

### **5.5 Network Outage Checker (AT&T-backed)**
- Shows **live outage status using customer pincode**

¬†
- L0 Must:

¬†
Always check this **before network/data troubleshooting**

¬†
- If outage exists:

¬†
Inform customer

¬†
- Do not escalate unnecessarily

¬†
- Share expected restoration timeline (if available)

¬†

¬†

### **5.6 ConnectX User Data**
- Direct access to the customer‚Äôs profile

¬†
- L0 Must use it to verify:

¬†
Account status

¬†
- Plan validity

¬†
- eSIM status

¬†
- Network status

¬†
- Billing/payment status

¬†

- Manual searching should be avoided when ConnectX access is available

¬†
**Mandatory Rule:**
All validations must be **cross-checked in ConnectX before escalation**.

**Note:** This window provides the direct link necessary to open the Customer's Profile within ConnectX.

## **6. Mandatory L0 Workflow Using the Extreme Right Panel**Before responding or escalating, L0 **must complete all checks below**:

- ‚úÖ Review Customer Context

¬†
- ‚úÖ Check Knowledge Articles

¬†
- ‚úÖ Verify Side Conversations

¬†
- ‚úÖ Review Related Tickets

¬†
- ‚úÖ Validate through relevant Apps

¬†
Only after completing all 5 checks can:

- Troubleshooting begin

¬†
- A resolution be provided

¬†
- An escalation be raised
## **7. Non-Compliance for L0 Agents**Failure to properly use the Extreme Right Panel may result in:

- Incorrect resolutions

¬†
- Duplicate escalations

¬†
- SLA breaches

¬†
- QA audit failures

¬†
- Process deviation observations

¬†
Repeated non-compliance will be escalated through **L0 performance management**.

#### Mandatory Checks & Required Fields (Zendesk)
*Article ID: 44455843878043 | Updated: 2025-12-16*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455843878043-Mandatory-Checks-Required-Fields-Zendesk*

# **Mandatory checks & required fields to be filled before changing the status of a ticket (Zendesk) (General)****Key Responsibility**: Perform all checks, complete all fields before changing the status of the ticket, and escalate correctly if required.

¬†

**Step-1**:** As soon as a ticket lands in the queue, after accepting the ticket.**

- Check if the customer's email address has been automatically updated in the Requester tab **(located on the far-left section** of the Zendesk interface).
- Ensure the customer's email ID is entered; updates regarding their ticket will not be sent otherwise. If the email is missing, it must be entered manually.

¬†

¬†

**Step-2**: **Ensure accurate ticket tagging based on customer‚Äôs concern.**

- 
**Type of Concern:** Question, Incident, Problem, and Task. Make sure you record the exact type of concern the customer contacted **support about**.

¬†

- 
**Inquiry Type: **Next, state the precise reason the customer contacted us. To easily select the correct inquiry reason, simply type relevant keywords into the dropdown box. For instance, if a customer is asking about plan details, type "Meow Offerings" and then select the corresponding inquiry type.
¬†

¬†

- 
**Ticket Process: **Specify the channel the customer used to contact us. Examples include Chat, Email, or, in rare cases, a Slack Escalation.
¬†

¬†

**Step-3:****¬†**

**Mandatory Field: Customer Mobile Number**

Filling in the Customer Mobile Number is mandatory. **This** allows us to easily contact the customer for follow-up communication after the ticket has been solved, provided this is their preferred method.

¬†

**Step-4****: Ticket Priority: **The Ticket Priority field is used to define the urgency and business impact of a customer issue. It helps the system and support teams identify which tickets require immediate attention and ensures that customer concerns are handled within the defined Service Level Agreements (SLAs).

¬†

¬†

**Step-5: ****End Session**

It is mandatory to end a messaging session after the customer has concluded the live chat. Failing to do so will result in future conversations **with** that customer continuing on the same ticket, making tracking difficult for management.

It ensures the interaction is **formally closed, accurately recorded, and correctly handed off** within the system. It also confirms that the agent has **completed all required actions** for the customer and prevents open or idle sessions from impacting service quality and reporting.

- It prevents duplicate or overlapping sessions.
- Allows accurate tracking of handle time and productivity
- Supports correct SLA calculation and reporting
- Confirms that the customer has received a final response or next steps.
Failure to end a session properly may lead to data mismatch, reporting errors, missed follow-ups, and customer dissatisfaction. Therefore, you must always confirm the interaction is complete and formally end the session as per process before moving to the next ticket.

**Mandatory Checks and Required Fields for L1 Ticket Escalation (Zendesk)**

**Key Responsibility: **To ensure that all tickets escalated to L1 Support from Zendesk contain complete, accurate, and verified information, enabling faster resolution and reducing back-and-forth communication between teams.

**Escalation Trigger: Escalate the ticket only after providing the troubleshooting steps mentioned in the Knowledge Bank and the issue remains unresolved.**

- 
**Step-1:** The mandatory fields that must be completed are: Requester, Type, Inquiry Type, Ticket Process, Customer‚Äôs Mobile Number, and Ticket Priority.
- 
**Step-2: **To ensure the L1 team can efficiently investigate and resolve customer issues behind the scenes, you must fill all the below fields accurately and completely at the time of escalation. Incomplete or unclear information may delay resolution and lead to rework.
**Email Address:**
- **Mobile Number:**
- **Issue:**
- **Troubleshooting Steps followed:**
- **Escalated By:**
- **Customer Expectation (If any):**

When including the email address in the template, double-check to ensure there are no spelling errors or incorrect domains. Additionally, remember these points when **detailing the issue**:

- What is not working
- Since when the issue started
- Frequency (intermittent/continuous)
- Any exact error messages
**When outlining customer expectations, consider the following points:**

- Mention any **specific request, deadline, or preference** expressed by the customer
- Example:
Callback request
- Urgent resolution timeline
- Refund request

- If no expectation is stated, clearly mention **‚ÄúNo specific expectation shared‚Äù**

- 
**Step-3: **Assign the ticket to the L1-Group rather than to a specific individual within that team.
- 
**Step-4: **End Session before changing the ticket status.

- 
**Step-5: **Change the status of the ticket from ‚Äú**Open**‚Äù to ‚Äú**On-Hold**‚Äù.

#### How to Check if eSIM is Already Activated?
*Article ID: 44462986203419 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44462986203419-How-to-Check-if-eSIM-is-Already-Activated*

Updated:

### Situation:Customers usually ask this question after signing up for Meow Wireless and receiving their eSIM activation email.
They may be:

- Unsure how to install or scan the QR code.

- Trying to activate on a device that‚Äôs not eSIM-compatible.

- Reporting that they didn‚Äôt receive their activation link or email.

Agents should be familiar with the basic steps of eSIM setup and the resources available in ConnectX for troubleshooting activation issues.

### Task:The agent‚Äôs goal is to guide the customer through eSIM activation, confirm whether their device supports eSIM, and ensure the activation completes successfully. If activation fails or the email hasn‚Äôt arrived, the agent should verify the account status in ConnectX.

### Steps for Agents:#### 1. Verify customer details in the ConnectX panel in Zendesk first. If information is not available, proceed to ConnectX Admin:
- Go to ConnectX > Customer360.

- Search by email or phone number.

- Check the Account Status and ensure that the eSIM has been issued **(status: ‚ÄúActivation Pending‚Äù or ‚ÄúActivated‚Äù)**.

- Confirm that the activation link or QR code was sent to the registered email.

#### 2. Ask clarifying questions:
- ‚ÄúHave you received your eSIM activation email from Meow Wireless?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you using an eSIM-compatible device?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúDid you already scan the QR code or try the activation link?‚Äù

- ‚ÄúAre you seeing any specific error message during setup?‚Äù

These questions help identify if the issue is with email delivery, device compatibility, or activation failure.

### Action:If the customer received the activation email but hasn‚Äôt installed the eSIM yet:

Guide them through the standard activation steps.

Example Response:
‚ÄúThanks for confirming! You can activate your Meow Wireless eSIM by following these steps:

- Open the email from Meow Wireless containing your eSIM QR code.

- On your phone, go to Settings > Cellular/Mobile Network > Add eSIM.

- Scan the QR code or enter the activation details manually.

- Wait for your device to complete setup ‚Äî this usually takes just a few minutes.
Once installed, your Meow Wireless service will automatically activate and you‚Äôll see our network appear on your phone.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm activation completion in ConnectX (status: ‚ÄúActive‚Äù).

- Tag the ticket accordingly.

If the customer hasn‚Äôt received their eSIM activation email:

Check whether it was sent or delayed.

Example Response:
‚ÄúI see that your eSIM activation email hasn‚Äôt arrived yet ‚Äî no worries! Sometimes it takes up to 30 minutes to appear in your inbox or spam folder. If you still don‚Äôt see it, I‚Äôll request a resend for you.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- Confirm email address on file.

- **Request resend via ConnectX ‚Üí ****Actions > Resend Activation Email****.**

- Advise the customer to check all folders (Inbox, Spam, Promotions).

- Tag ticket accordingly.

If the customer reports that activation failed:

Verify device compatibility and escalate if needed.

Example Response:
‚ÄúThanks for letting us know. If your device showed an error during eSIM setup, it could be due to compatibility or connection issues. Let‚Äôs try reinstalling:

- Remove the previous eSIM attempt from your phone‚Äôs settings.

- Restart your device.

- Re-scan the QR code or click the activation link again.
If it still doesn‚Äôt activate, we‚Äôll escalate this to our Technical Team for manual provisioning.‚Äù

Next Steps for Agent:

- **Check device compatibility in ConnectX (supported device list).**

- **If reinstallation fails, escalate to **L1 ‚Üí eSIM Activation Issue**.**

- **Advise the customer of a **24‚Äì48 hour turnaround time** for resolution.**

- Tag ticket accordingly.

### Result:
- The customer successfully activates their Meow Wireless eSIM or receives clear next steps.

- Delayed or failed activations are escalated properly through ConnectX.

- The customer gains immediate access to network service and Meow Wireless benefits.

### Additional Notes:
- Never resend QR codes manually outside ConnectX.

- Always verify device compatibility before troubleshooting further.

- Escalate only if activation remains unposted after 48 hours or repeated failure occurs.

- Confirm email and device information carefully before proceeding.

### Plans

#### Is the data really unlimited?

*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44518260506523-Is-the-data-really-unlimited*

Yes. You have unlimited data usage. However, to ensure fair access for everyone, if you use more than 50GB in a single billing cycle, your speeds may temporarily slow down during times when the network is very busy. Once the network clears up (or your next month starts), you're back to full speed.

#### What happens if I miss my payment?
*Article ID: 42081961947035 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42081961947035-What-happens-if-I-miss-my-payment*

When a payment is missed, we‚Äôll automatically retry processing it up to three times within 72 hours.
If all three attempts fail, your account will be auto-suspended until payment is successfully made.

If no payment is received within 90 days, your account will be terminated and your services will be discontinued.

To avoid interruptions, we recommend keeping your payment method up to date so your subscription stays active.

### Port-in and Port-out

#### Numbers that cannot be ported in
*Article ID: 44557267053723 | Updated: 2025-12-18*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44557267053723-Numbers-that-cannot-be-ported-in*

- **Disconnected Numbers:** If the old line is already cancelled, it is lost.
- **International Numbers:** We can only port US numbers (+1).

---

#### Can I start with a new number and port later?
*Article ID: 44557219003931 | Updated: 2025-12-18*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44557219003931-Can-I-start-with-a-new-number-and-port-later*

**Yes.** The customer can activate with a temporary Meow Mobile number today to get data/service immediately. Later, they can submit a port request in the app to replace the temporary number with their old number.

---

#### If I leave in the middle of the month, do I get a refund for the unused days?
*Article ID: 44516855034907 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516855034907-If-I-leave-in-the-middle-of-the-month-do-I-get-a-refund-for-the-unused-days*

No. We do not offer prorated refunds for partial months. Your service will simply end on the day the transfer is complete.

---

#### What happens to my 24/7 Vet Care if I leave?
*Article ID: 44516798401435 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516798401435-What-happens-to-my-24-7-Vet-Care-if-I-leave*

The vet care benefits are part of your active subscription. The moment your number transfers to a new carrier and your Meow Mobile service ends, you will lose access to the vet chat and wellness perks immediately.

---

#### Will I get charged a fee for taking my number to another carrier?
*Article ID: 44516749740571 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516749740571-Will-I-get-charged-a-fee-for-taking-my-number-to-another-carrier*

No. We don‚Äôt believe in holding your number hostage. There are no termination fees for porting out.

---

#### How do I find my account info if I decide to leave Meow Mobile?
*Article ID: 44516680699803 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516680699803-How-do-I-find-my-account-info-if-I-decide-to-leave-Meow-Mobile*

We‚Äôll be sad to see you go! You can find your transfer details directly in the app:

- Go to **Settings** > **Account Management**.

- Look for **"Number Transfer"** or **"Port Out Info."**

- There, you will see your Account Number and a button to **"Generate Transfer PIN."**

#### Can I bring my landline number over to Meow Mobile?
*Article ID: 44516651985307 | Updated: 2025-12-17*

#### How long will it take for my number to move over?
*Article ID: 44516534122907 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516534122907-How-long-will-it-take-for-my-number-to-move-over*

#### How do I actually start the transfer process?
*Article ID: 44516484647451 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516484647451-How-do-I-actually-start-the-transfer-process*

It‚Äôs all done in the Meow Mobile App!

- When you select **"Activate Service,"** choose the option **"Keep My Number."**

- Enter the Account Number and Transfer PIN you gathered earlier.

- Sit back and relax while we pull your number over to the pride.

---

#### What information do I need to find to transfer my number?
*Article ID: 44516461531675 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516461531675-What-information-do-I-need-to-find-to-transfer-my-number*

You will need to gather four things from your current carrier before you start the Meow Mobile activation:

- **Account Number:** This is usually on your bill or in your online account.

- **Number to be Transferred:** The line number that you will be transferring over from your current carrier.¬†

- **Transfer PIN (Port-Out PIN):** This is a specific security code for transfers, *not* your login password. You usually have to request this from your current carrier's app or support team.

- 
**Billing Zip Code:** The zip code currently associated with your phone bill.

---

#### Do I need to cancel my current phone service before I switch to Meow Mobile?
*Article ID: 44516205599003 | Updated: 2025-12-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44516205599003-Do-I-need-to-cancel-my-current-phone-service-before-I-switch-to-Meow-Mobile*

No! Please do not cancel your current service yet. Your number must be active for us to transfer it. If you cancel your old plan first, you might lose your number forever. Once we successfully activate your number on Meow Mobile, your old service will cancel automatically.

---

#### Can I port my existing number from another carrier?
*Article ID: 42082737998619 | Updated: 2025-12-18*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/42082737998619-Can-I-port-my-existing-number-from-another-carrier*

Yes. Meow Wireless will support number portability, allowing you to transfer your existing number during activation. Detailed steps will be shared at launch.

---

## Network and Technical Troubleshooting

### Suspension & Termination Related Concerns

#### Service resumed from Suspension, Status on ConnectX - Active, Services - Not working
*Article ID: 44455726855067 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455726855067-Service-resumed-from-Suspension-Status-on-ConnectX-Active-Services-Not-working*

**Service resumed from Suspension, Status on ConnectX - Active, Services - Not working.¬†**

¬†

### **Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**
- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance
- Confirm:
Have they restarted the device *after* the payment was made?¬†
- What exactly is displayed on the screen? (e.g., "Emergency Calls Only," "No Service," or Signal bars present but calls failing).
- If they received a "Service Restored" SMS or email confirmation.

- Take an alternate contact number from the customer.
- Capture exact location/pincode.
- Add all relevant notes in ConnectX.
**Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Account status - ConnectX

[Account Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600349458331-Check-Account-Status-ConnectX)

2
Similar open tickets on activation failure refunds - Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

### **Step 3 - Troubleshooting Steps to be done (L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Steps**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)
- Check complete ticket history and past conversationsReview the timeline: When was the suspension applied? When was the payment made/service restored?

- Check internal notes on the account in ConnectX
Confirm the Account Status specifically reads "Active" and not "Suspended" or "Barred."
- Check notes on the account.¬†

- Mandatory Restart (Power Cycle)Ask the customer to power the phone completely off, wait 30 seconds, and turn it back on.¬†

- Toggle Airplane Mode ON/OFFIf a restart is not immediately possible, toggle Airplane mode for 10 seconds.

- Manual Network SelectionGo to Settings > Cellular > Network Selection. Turn off "Auto" and then select Meow Mobile again.

- Reset Network SettingsIf the issue persists, perform a Reset of Network Settings to clear any stuck routing tables.

### **Step 4 - Providing the ETR to customer**
- Inform the customer that backend verification may be required.
- Provide a standard ETR - 1-2 hours.

- Assure proactive update once the Network team refreshes the profile.
### **Step 5 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk -**
- Ensure all mandatory fields are tagged.
- Apply correct Primary & Secondary Tags (e.g., Category: Suspension, Sub-category: Resume Failed / Mismatch)
- Set correct Ticket Priority based on impact (High - Customer is without service despite paying).
- Add complete internal escalation notes
- Attach all screenshots and test results
- Change ticket status to On-hold.
- 
**Details to be provided to L1:**
Device Model + OS Version
- Customer Location (Pin code/Area)
- Time of Payment
- Confirmation that "Restart" was performed (Yes/No)
- Current Signal Status (e.g., "Emergency Calls Only")
- Error Message when attempting a call.

### Troubleshooting Guide

#### SOP: Mandatory Incident Data Collection & Escalation (L0 ‚Üí L1)
*Article ID: 46471334875547 | Updated: 2026-02-10*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46471334875547-SOP-Mandatory-Incident-Data-Collection-Escalation-L0-L1*

## **Purpose**This SOP defines **mandatory data collection and validation steps for L0 agents** before escalating incidents to L1.
Proper data capture ensures:

- Faster L1/L2 triage
- Clean AT&T / OSP escalations
- Reduced back-and-forth
- Audit-safe, compliant handling
‚ö†Ô∏è **If mandatory fields are missing, the escalation must NOT be sent.**

# **L0 Action (Applies to All Incident Types)**### **L0 Action ‚Äì **Identify the incident category, collect all mandatory data exactly as required, validate accuracy, and escalate only after all non-negotiable fields are captured.## **Step 1 ‚Äì Visual Audit**
- Review complete ticket history.
- Check previous escalations or rejections.
- Review internal notes in ConnectX.
- Identify **incident type**:
Subscriber Connectivity
- Port-In
- Port-Out
- API Issue
- Billing
- Voice
- SMS/MMS

- Confirm this is **not a duplicate or already active escalation**.
## **Step 2 ‚Äì Incident Categorization**L0 must clearly classify the issue into **ONE primary category** before proceeding:

- Subscriber Connectivity
- Port-In
- Port-Out
- API Issues
- Subscriber Billing
- Voice Service
- SMS / MMS
‚ö†Ô∏è **Wrong categorization = L1/L2 rejection**

# **1. Subscriber Connectivity Issues (L0 SOP)**### **Use for**No Service, No Data, Drops, Slow Data, Hotspot failure, Coverage complaints.

## **Mandatory Fields ‚Äì L0 Must Collect ALL**
- ICCID
- IMEI
- SIM Type (Physical / eSIM)
- Device Make & Model
- Issue Start Date & Time (with timezone)
- Ongoing or Intermittent
- Location (Full Address)
- Latitude & Longitude (**ZIP only is NOT allowed**)
- Technology Attached (4G / LTE / 5G / NSA / SA)
- Signal Bars (0‚Äì5)
- Worked Before at Same Location (Yes / No)
- Worked in Other Location (Yes / No)
- Issue Scope (Everywhere / Specific Location)
- Other Devices Affected in Same Area (Yes / No)
- Impact (Data / Voice / SMS / Complete Loss)
- **Exact Error Message (copy-paste only)**
## **L1 Validation Rules**
- ICCID + IMEI + Location + Time = **Non-negotiable**

- ZIP code alone ‚â† valid location
- Error messages must be **exact**, not paraphrased
# **2. Port-In Issues**### **Use for**New number port-in failures, rejections, stuck states.

### **Mandatory Fields**
- Exact Error Message
- New SIM ICCID
- IMEI
- Pricing Plan
- Customer Full Name (as per OSP)
- OSP Account Number
- OSP Account Address (exact)
- SSN (Last 4 digits ONLY ‚Äì secure field)
- OSP Port-Out PIN / Password (secure field)
- Additional Notes
### **Security Rules**
- ‚ùå Never paste SSN/PIN in comments, Slack, screenshots
- ‚úÖ Secure fields only
### **Common Rejection Causes (For L0 Awareness)**
- PIN mismatch
- Name/address mismatch
- Inactive donor account
# **3. Port-Out Issues**### **Use for**Customer leaving network, donor release failures.

### **Mandatory Fields**
- Exact Error Message
- Active SIM ICCID
- IMEI
- Current Pricing Plan
- Customer Full Name (OSP)
- OSP Account Number
- OSP Account Address
- SSN (Last 4 digits ‚Äì secure)
- Port-Out PIN / Password (secure)
- Additional Notes
### **L0 Notes**
- Port-out uses **active SIM**, not new SIM
- PIN expiry is the #1 failure reason
# **4. API Issues**### **Use for**CSI, BSS, provisioning API failures.

### **Mandatory Fields**
- CSI Service Name
- Environment (PROD / UAT / SIT)
- Conversation ID(s)
- Transaction / Correlation ID
- Request Timestamp (timezone)
- Response Timestamp (timezone)
- XML Request (raw, unedited)
- XML Response (raw, unedited)
- Masked Subscriber Identifiers:
MSISDN
- IMSI
- ICCID

### **L1 Rules (L0 Must Enforce)**
- ‚ùå No screenshots of XML
- ‚ùå No partial payloads
- ‚úÖ Mask identifiers
- ‚úÖ Include all retries & conversation IDs
# **5. Subscriber Billing Issues**### **Mandatory Fields**
- MSISDN
- Account / Customer ID
- ICCID (if applicable)
- Billing Issue Type
- Impacted Amount & Currency
- Billing Period
- Invoice Number
- Transaction / Payment ID
- Current Plan
- Active Add-ons
- Last Plan Change Date
- Issue First Noticed (Date/Time/Time zone)
- Customer Expected Resolution (Refund / Credit / Explanation)
# **6. Voice Service Issues**### **Mandatory Fields**
- ICCID
- IMEI
- SIM Type
- Device Make / Model
- Issue Start Date & Time
- Ongoing or Intermittent
- Location (Full Address + Lat/Long)
- Technology (4G/LTE/5G/VoLTE)
- Signal Bars
- Worked Before (Same / Other Location)
- Issue Scope
- Other Devices Affected
- Impact (Voice-specific)
- Exact Error Message
# **7. SMS / MMS Issues**### **Use when**SMS/MMS not working while Data & Voice are working.

### **Mandatory Fields**(Same structure as Voice, with SMS/MMS impact)

¬†

## **Escalation Guardrails**L1/L2 will **reject tickets** if:

- Mandatory fields are missing
- Error messages are paraphrased
- Sensitive data is exposed
- No timestamps or IDs exist

---

#### Troubleshooting guide
*Article ID: 44455761075099 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099-Troubleshooting-guide*

# **üìò Mobile Device Troubleshooting Guide (iOS, Samsung, Pixel, OnePlus)**¬†

# **1. Check IMEI or EID**### **iOS**### ****
- Go to **Settings ‚Üí General ‚Üí About**

- Scroll to **IMEI** and **EID**

- (EID is mandatory for eSIM activation)

¬†
### **Samsung / Pixel / OnePlus**### ****
- Go to **Settings ‚Üí About Phone ‚Üí Status ‚Üí IMEI information**

- EID appears under **SIM status / eSIM information**

- Or dial ***#06#**

¬†
¬†

# **2. Restart the Device****Purpose:** Clears temporary network conflicts and reloads carrier services.

### **iOS**
- Hold **Volume Up + Side button** ‚Üí slide to power off

¬†
- Turn back on after 10 seconds

¬†
### **Samsung / Pixel / OnePlus**- Hold **Power button** ‚Üí **Restart** (or Power Off then turn on)

¬†¬†

# **3. Toggle Airplane Mode****Purpose:** Forces the device to detach and reconnect to the nearest cell towers.

### **All Devices**
- Pull down the quick settings panel

¬†
- Toggle **Airplane Mode ON** ‚Üí wait 10 seconds ‚Üí **OFF**

¬†
¬†

# **4. Reset Network Settings****Purpose:** Clears old carrier profiles, corrupt settings, APNs, Wi-Fi, Bluetooth, and reconnects devices to the network fresh.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí General ‚Üí Transfer or Reset iPhone ‚Üí Reset ‚Üí **Reset Network Settings**

### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí General Management ‚Üí Reset ‚Üí **Reset Network Settings**

### **Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí System ‚Üí Reset Options ‚Üí **Reset Wi-Fi, Mobile & Bluetooth**

¬†

# **5. Check APN Settings (‚Äúereseller‚Äù)****Purpose:** Ensures the device is using the correct APN values for data and eSIM provisioning.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Mobile Data Options ‚Üí Mobile Data Network

- Confirm APN shows **ereseller**

¬†### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí Mobile Networks ‚Üí **Access Point Names**

- Check APN shows **ereseller**

¬†### **Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí **Access Point Names**

- Confirm APN is **ereseller**

¬†¬†

# **6. Manual Network Selection****Purpose:** Helps reconnect to the correct network when auto-connect fails.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Network Selection ‚Üí disable **Automatic** ‚Üí choose network manually.

### **Samsung / Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí Connections / Network & Internet ‚Üí Mobile Networks ‚Üí **Network Operators** ‚Üí disable auto and select manually.

¬†

# **7. Toggle Between 4G and 5G****Purpose:** Fixes issues where 5G signal is weak or registration hasn‚Äôt occurred.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Voice & Data ‚Üí switch between **5G Auto / LTE**

### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí Mobile Networks ‚Üí **Network Mode** ‚Üí choose 5G/LTE/Auto or LTE only.

### **Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí **Preferred Network Type** ‚Üí switch between 5G/LTE.

¬†

# **8. Manual eSIM Setup****Purpose:** Required when automatic eSIM activation fails or QR code needs to be added manually.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Add eSIM ‚Üí

- Choose **Use QR Code** or **Enter Details Manually**

¬†
- Enter SM-DP+ and activation code if required

¬†
### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí SIM Manager ‚Üí Add eSIM ‚Üí

- Scan QR code or choose **Enter activation code**

¬†### **Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí **Add SIM** ‚Üí

- Scan QR or **Enter activation code manually**

¬†¬†

# **9. Toggle eSIM Setting****Purpose:** Refreshes eSIM registration and forces network re-attach.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí tap your eSIM ‚Üí turn **Line On / Off**

### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí SIM Manager ‚Üí toggle eSIM **ON/OFF**

### **Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí toggle **SIM ON/OFF**

¬†

# **10. Set eSIM as Primary****Purpose:** Ensures the correct eSIM is used for mobile data, voice, and SMS.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Default Line / Mobile Data ‚Üí select the eSIM as **Primary**

### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí SIM Manager ‚Üí

- Choose **Preferred SIM** for Calls, SMS, and Mobile Data**Pixel / OnePlus**

¬†

- Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí- Set **Preferred SIM for calls, SMS, and data**

¬†¬†

# **11. Delete Old / Unused SIM Profiles****Purpose:** Clears outdated or conflicting eSIM profiles that may block activation.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí tap unused plan ‚Üí **Delete eSIM**

### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí SIM Manager ‚Üí select SIM ‚Üí **Remove**

### **Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí select SIM ‚Üí **Erase / Delete SIM**

¬†

# **12. Check Roaming Status****Purpose:** Ensures roaming is enabled when customers travel and prevents data block.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Mobile Data Options ‚Üí

- Check **Data Roaming** = ON (if required)

¬†### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí Mobile Networks ‚Üí

- Check **Data Roaming** = ON

¬†### **Pixel / OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí

- Toggle **Roaming** ON/OFF

¬†¬†

# **13. Check OS Version****Purpose:** Confirms the device is updated, since outdated OS can break eSIM or APN functions.

### **iOS**Settings ‚Üí General ‚Üí **Software Update**

- Shows the current version and available updates

¬†### **Samsung**Settings ‚Üí Software Update ‚Üí **Download and Install**

### **Pixel**Settings ‚Üí System ‚Üí System Update

### **OnePlus**Settings ‚Üí System ‚Üí **System Updates**

¬†

**14. ****Paths to check VPN settings:**

### **iOS (iPhone)****Settings**** > ****General**** > ****VPN & Device Management**** > ****VPN**

### **Google Pixel****Settings**** > ****Network & internet**** > ****VPN**

### **Samsung****Settings**** > ****Connections**** > ****More connection settings**** > ****VPN**

¬†

**15. eSIM profile is Enabled (Turned On):**

### **iOS (iPhone)**Settings > Cellular > Select the eSIM > Toggle Turn On This Line to **ON**

### **Google Pixel**Settings > Network & internet > SIMs > Select the eSIM > Toggle Use SIM to **ON**

### **Samsung**Settings > Connections > SIM manager > Toggle the switch next to the eSIM to **ON**

### App related scenarios

#### Customer cannot login to the app
*Article ID: 44455662017307 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455662017307-Customer-cannot-login-to-the-app*

## **App Login Status ‚Äì Failed**## **L0 Action ‚Äì***** **Identify the exact login failure reason, validate customer account details, perform standard app-level troubleshooting, and escalate only if backend or system-level errors are confirmed.*## **Step 1 ‚Äì Probing & Empathizing with the Customer**
- **Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance.**
- 
**Confirm the following with the customer:**
Exact **error message shown on the app** (if any Screenshot).¬†
- Whether login is attempted via:
Apple ID
- Email ID (Gmail)

- Whether the issue started **suddenly or after an update**.
- The app is updated to the **latest version** from the Play Store/App Store.
- Ask alternative email and contact number

- 
**Confirm whether:**The customer is connected to **Wi-Fi or mobile data**.

## **Step 2 ‚Äì Tools to Analyze & Handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Check Account Status-ConnectX

[Account Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600349458331-Check-Account-Status-ConnectX)

2
Verify Customer details (Email, Mobile Number) are correct-ConnectX

3
Check Failed Payment Status-ConnectX

4
Similar Ongoing Tickets-Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

¬†

## **Step 3 ‚Äì Troubleshooting Steps to be Done**
- Check complete ticket history and past conversations on **Zendesk**.
- Review any previous login or app-access issues.
- Verify:
Account status (Active / Suspended / Terminated).
Registered mobile number & email ID.
- Last successful login timestamp (if available).

### **1. Network & Device Check**Ask the customer to do:

- Switch between **Wi-Fi and mobile data**.
- Turn on **Airplane Mode for 30 seconds**, then turn it off.
- Restart the device.
- Disable any **VPN**.
### **2. App Health Check**Guide the customer to:

- **Force close the Meow Wireless App.**
- 
**Clear**:
App Cache
- App Data (if applicable)

- 
**Retry login after logout**

¬†

## **Step 4: Mark if App Login Failure ‚Äì Backend Check Required.****Escalation to L1 ‚Äì Steps to be Completed on Zendesk**

Before escalating:

- Ensure all mandatory fields are filled.
- Set correct priority based on impact ***(should be high).***

- Add complete internal notes with:
Error message shown.
- Account/MSISDN
- Device model & OS version.
- App version.
- Network type used (Wi-Fi/Mobile Data).
- Time & date of failed attempts.

- Attach screenshots (if provided).
- Change ticket status to **On-Hold ‚Äì Pending L1 Review**.
## **Step 5 ‚Äì Providing the TAT to the Customer**
- Inform that a backend investigation is required.
- Provide standard TAT: **1-2 business hours**.
- Assure proactive updates once reviewed by the backend team.

#### Usage mis-display / data integrity issues/ App display incorrect information (e.g. negative data, impossible dates, wrong plan details)
*Article ID: 44455636926875 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455636926875-Usage-mis-display-data-integrity-issues-App-display-incorrect-information-e-g-negative-data-impossible-dates-wrong-plan-details*

**Data Usage Mis-Display / Integrity Issues**

**Scenario:** App displays incorrect information such as negative data, impossible dates, wrong plan details, or mismatched usage.
¬†

**Step 1 ‚Äì Probing & Empathizing with the Customer**

-Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance.

- Need to verify the email or contact number
- Review any past troubleshooting already performed, as well as internal notes and account details on **Zendesk/ConnectX** ***(if any)***.
- Identify the exact mis-display issue:-

- Since when has it been showing a mismatch?
- If any mismatch is found between backend data and app display
- Need to confirm which usage entries are duplicated or missing.
- Need to ask for a screenshot of the error.
- Need to ask for alternative contact number
**Step 2 - Standard L0 Troubleshooting**

**Ask the customer to perform**

- *Logout and login again*
- *Clear cache of the app*
- *Update the app to the latest version*
- *Check on another device (if available)*
**Step 3 ‚Äì Tools to Analyze & Handle (ConnectX)**

- *Click on Customer 360 on the left side of the page*
- 
*Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.*

- *Click on the **Product tab.***
- ***Scroll down and check on Usage Detail accordingly like SMS, Call, Voice.***
**Step 4: Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk **[**Mandatory Checks & Required Fields (Zendesk)**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455843878043)

- Ensure all mandatory fields are filled
- Set correct Ticket Priority based on impact
- Add complete internal escalation notes
- Attach all screenshots and test results
- Change ticket status to **On - hold**, i.e, Escalated to L1.
**Step 5 - Providing the TAT to customer**

- Inform the customer that backend verification may be required
- Provide a standard TAT of: 1-2 hours (TBD as per policy)
- Assure proactive update once L1 investigation is completed¬†
***Details to be provided to L1: (Confirmed Mandatory)***

- Need to attach the screenshot of the error.
- Add complete internal escalation notes
- Mention the detailed troubleshooting you have guided the customer through in the internal notes.
- Exact Time & Date when Issue Started
- Mention the Alternative number

#### App crash
*Article ID: 44455595851675 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455595851675-App-crash*

## **Meow Wireless Application Crash**This SOP guides an L0 agent through troubleshooting steps when a customer reports that the mobile application (app) is crashing, freezing, or closing unexpectedly.

### **Step 1. Probing and Empathy**
- *Acknowledge the inconvenience: "I apologize that the app is crashing. I know that's frustrating. We'll try a few steps to get it running smoothly again."*
- Gather crash details:
Review any past troubleshooting already performed, as well as internal notes and account details on Zendesk/ConnectX (if any).
- When did the crash occur?¬†
- 
**Device details:** **Device Model** and **Operating System (OS)** version.
- Ask for alternative email and contact number(For further communication).
- 
**App version:** *(If known, or guide them to check it in the device app settings - Settings > General > iPhone Storage, finding the app in the list, and tapping it to see the version number).*

### **Step 2.¬† L0 Device Troubleshooting Steps¬†**
- **¬†Basic Refresh (Restart/Toggle):**
- 
**Action:** Ask the customer to **completely close the app** (swipe it away from the recent apps list) and then **reopen it**.
- 
***If that fails***, ask the customer to **fully restart their device** (power off, then on).

- 
**¬†Check Connectivity:**
**Action:** Ensure the customer has a **stable internet connection** (Wi-Fi or Mobile Data). Sometimes, poor connectivity causes app processes to hang and crash.

- 
**¬†Clear App Cache (Android Only):**

**Action:** Guide Android users to go to **Settings **‚Äì **Apps** ‚Äì Find the specific app ‚Äì **Storage** ‚Äì **Clear Cache**.
- *Note: Do not instruct them to clear Data unless the following steps fail, as this forces a re-login.*

- 
**¬†Check for App Updates:**
**Action:** Guide the customer to the **App Store (iOS) or Play Store (Android)**. Search for the app and ensure there are **no pending updates**. Crashes are often fixed in the latest release.

- 
**¬†Reinstallation (Final L0 Attempt):**

**Action:** **Warn the customer:** This will require them to log in again.
- Guide the customer to **Uninstall** the application, restart the device, and then **Reinstall** the latest version from the respective App Store.

### **3. Escalation to L1*****Escalate only if the issue happens again and is not resolved.***

- 
**Prioritize the Escalation:** This is often a bug. The information gathered must be precise for the technical team.
- 
**Details for L1:**

**Device Model/OS Version:** (Crucial for replication).
- 
**App Version:** (Must be the latest version.
- 
**Specific Replication Steps:** (e.g., "The app crashes every time I tap the 'View Usage' button after logging in.")
- 
**Screenshots/Video:** Ask the customer if they can provide a screenshot of the error message (if any) or a screen recording of the crash.
- Confirmation that **all L0 troubleshooting steps were performed** (especially reinstallation).
- Change ticket status to On - hold, ie, Escalated to L1.
- Set correct priority based on impact ***(should be high).***

**Step 4 - Providing the TAT to customer**

- Inform the customer that backend verification may be required
- Provide a standard TAT of: 1-2 hours (TBD as per policy)
- Assure proactive update once L1 investigation is completed

---

### Network related issues:

#### SMS / MMS messages Issues Playbook for L1/L2 [DRAFT]
*Article ID: 46732322495899 | Updated: 2026-02-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46732322495899-SMS-MMS-messages-Issues-Playbook-for-L1-L2*

- If the customer is able to make voice calls, but has messaging issues, check that SMS/ MMS SOCs are provisioned through TMF 637. If the customer cannot make voice calls, please refer to voice troubleshooting.
- If SOCs are present, check IMSHSS details on AT&T Self Service webpage.¬†Ensure Id: sip:+13035706414@one.att.net
Unregistered Service Ind: true
Barring Ind: **<should not be true>**
Default Id Ind:

- If above information is fine, open a ticket for AT&T with following information
Messaging | (Case Type)
CTN
ICCID
IMEI
Optional: Billing Market
- Issue Description / Impact, Roaming, Was number ported, Issue Start Date / Time, Physical Address of Issue, Technology, Signal Bars, Has it worked before at this location, Has it worked in another area, Other Devices/ ¬†Services, Provide Error Messages

#### Data Not working playbook for L1/L2 [DRAFT]
*Article ID: 46731372972443 | Updated: 2026-02-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46731372972443-Data-Not-working-playbook-for-L1-L2*

- Confirm that the customer is in an active status ('A') on AT&T portal.
- Confirm that customer is latched to EPCHSS by checking **MME Registration Attach Status**:¬†** 2. **Value 2 means the device is registered for **full services** ‚Äî data, voice, and SMS. If not latched, eSIM or device issue.¬†
- Check TMF 637 (TLG) for ¬†SOCs existing on account which would block/prevent service (no data soc, no international roaming, etc) in TLG. If yes, then enable/disable the SOCs as required.
- If the issue is about data not working in domestic/national roaming, then check TLG for SOCs existing on account which would enable data/domestic roaming.
- If all seems ok, open ticket for AT&T with following information
CTN
ICCID
IMEI
Optional: Billing Market
- Issue Description / Impact, Roaming, Was number ported, Issue Start Date / Time, Physical Address of Issue, Technology, Signal Bars, Has it worked before at this location, Has it worked in another area, Other Devices/ ¬†Services, Provide Error Messages, whether the issue is with a specific URL or if it is a more widespread issue.

#### eSIM Not Working Troubleshooting Playbook for L1/L2 [DRAFT]
*Article ID: 46727438572187 | Updated: 2026-02-17*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46727438572187-eSIM-Not-Working-Troubleshooting-Playbook-for-L1-L2*

- Check the eSIM status from SMDP+ platform. If it is not in INSTALLED status then eSIM is not installed on device. If the status is 'READY TO INSTALL', then eSIM is yet to be installed. If the status is unavailable then eSIM has been deleted.
- If the eSIM status is installed then check on AT&T Self Service portal whether device is latched on network or not. If device is latched then escalate to AT&T.¬†Check **MME Registration Attach Status** on EPCHSS information page. If the value is 0 then OTA is not success. If value is 1, 2 then device is latched to network.

#### Voicemail Box Full
*Article ID: 46569014727323 | Updated: 2026-02-12*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46569014727323-Voicemail-Box-Full*

### **What this means:**When the voicemail box is full, **new callers cannot leave messages** until existing voicemails are deleted. This is a **storage issue on the voicemail platform**, not a network issue.

## **‚úÖ L0 Confirmation Checklist**
- Old voicemails deleted
- Deleted messages folder cleared (iPhone)
- Test voicemail successful
- Customer confirms resolution
## **üì± iPhone ‚Äì Clear Voicemail Box**### **Step 1: Delete Voicemails from Visual Voicemail**
- Open the **Phone** app
- Tap **Voicemail** (bottom-right)
- Review the list of voicemails
- Swipe **left** on old or unwanted voicemails
- Tap **Delete**

### **Step 2: Empty Deleted Messages (Important)**Deleted voicemails may still take up space.

- In **Voicemail**, scroll down
- Tap **Deleted Messages**

- Tap **Clear All**

- Confirm deletion
### **Step 3: Test Voicemail**
- Call the customer‚Äôs number from another phone
- Let it ring to voicemail
- Confirm a new voicemail can be left
If successful ‚Üí close case.

## **ü§ñ Android ‚Äì Clear Voicemail Box**Steps may vary slightly by manufacturer (Samsung, Pixel, etc.)

### **Option A: Visual Voicemail App**
- Open the **Phone** app
- Tap **Voicemail** or **Visual Voicemail**

- Long-press old voicemails
- Tap **Delete**

- Confirm deletion
### **Option B: Dial-In Voicemail (Most Reliable)**
- Open **Phone** app
- 
**Press and hold 1** (or dial *86)
- Enter voicemail PIN (if prompted)
- Follow voice prompts to:
Listen to messages
- Delete messages one by one

- Confirm messages are permanently deleted
### **Step 3: Restart & Test**
- Restart the device
- Call the customer‚Äôs number from another line
- Confirm voicemail accepts new messages
## **üîî L0 Notes & Guardrails**
- Visual Voicemail deletion alone may **not** clear the box on Android ‚Äî always recommend dial-in if unsure
- Restart helps sync mailbox status with the network
- If mailbox still shows full after deletion ‚Üí escalate (possible backend sync issue)
¬†

- 
**How to Set / change / retrieve Voicemail PIN ? (Universal Method)**
Open the **Phone** app
- **Press and hold 1** *(or dial *86)*
- When prompted, enter the **current PIN**
- 
Follow the voice menu to:
Change PIN
- Set a new PIN

- 
Choose a PIN that:
Is **4‚Äì7 digits**
- Is not a simple sequence (e.g., 1234)

- Confirm PIN change completed successfully¬†

- 
### **Attempt PIN Reset via Device**

iPhone:**Settings ‚Üí Phone ‚Üí Change Voicemail Password**

- 
Android:**Phone app ‚Üí Settings ‚Üí Voicemail ‚Üí Change PIN** (if available)

---

#### SOP ‚Äì Voicemail Issues
*Article ID: 46520293633819 | Updated: 2026-02-11*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46520293633819-SOP-Voicemail-Issues*

## **Scope**This SOP applies **only to L0 support** handling customer-reported voicemail issues across Android and iPhone devices.

## **Voicemail Issue Types Covered:**
- Voicemail not set up or not working
- Caller unable to leave a voicemail
- Customer not receiving voicemails
- No voicemail notifications
- Unable to access voicemail
- Visual voicemail not loading or syncing
## **Mandatory Data Collection**Collect **all** details before troubleshooting:

### **Customer & Account Details**
- Phone number (MSISDN)
- Account status (Active / Suspended)
- Device make & model
- OS version
- eSIM or physical SIM
### **Issue Details**
- Exact issue description in customer‚Äôs words
- When the issue started
- Is the issue constant or intermittent
- Any error messages shown
### **Voicemail Context**
- Was voicemail previously working? (Yes / No / Unsure)
- Type of voicemail: Carrier voicemail or Visual voicemail
- Date & time of last successful voicemail (if known)
## **L0 Troubleshooting Steps:**Follow steps in order. Do **not** skip steps.

### **Step 1: Account & Signal Validation**
- Confirm line is **Active**

- Confirm device has cellular signal
- Ask customer to toggle Airplane Mode for 30 seconds
- Restart the device
### **Step 2: Basic Voicemail Access Test**
- Ask customer to **press and hold 1** on the dial pad
- OR dial their own phone number
- Confirm whether voicemail system answers
**Outcomes:**

- Voicemail answers ‚Üí proceed to Step 3
- Voicemail does not answer ‚Üí document and proceed to Step 6
### **Step 3: Check Voicemail Settings ‚Äì iPhone**Guide the customer step-by-step:

- Open **Phone** app
- Tap **Voicemail** (bottom-right)
- Confirm voicemail inbox loads
- Check:
Voicemail greeting is set
- Voicemail box is not full

- Tap **Greeting** ‚Üí confirm custom or default greeting plays
- Go to **Settings ‚Üí Phone ‚Üí Notifications**Ensure notifications are enabled

**If Visual Voicemail does not load:**

- Ask customer to pull down to refresh
- Confirm iOS is up to date
### **Step 4: Check Voicemail Settings ‚Äì Android**(Exact steps may vary slightly by manufacturer)

- Open **Phone** app
- Tap **Three dots / Menu**

- Go to **Settings ‚Üí Voicemail**

- Check:
Voicemail number is populated
- Voicemail service is enabled

- Tap **Advanced Settings** (if available)Confirm notifications are enabled

- Open **Visual Voicemail** tab (if present)Confirm inbox loads

- 
**If, Voicemail Number is not populated****,¬†**
**Open ****Phone app**
- **Tap ****Three dots ‚Üí Settings**
- **Go to ****Voicemail**
- **Tap ****Advanced Settings**
- **Tap ****Voicemail number**
- **Enter: *****86**
- **Save and exit**

### **Step 5: Notification & App Checks (Both Devices)**
- Confirm Do Not Disturb / Focus mode is off
- Confirm voicemail notifications are allowed at OS level
- Clear Phone app cache (Android only)
- Ensure Phone / Voicemail app is updated
### **Step 6: Live Test Call**
- Call customer‚Äôs number from another line
- Let the call ring until voicemail
- Confirm:
Caller can leave voicemail
- Customer can retrieve voicemail

**Outcomes:**

- Test successful ‚Üí confirm resolution with customer and close case
- Test fails ‚Üí proceed to Step 7
### **Step 7: Escalation Criteria (L0 ‚Üí L1)**Escalate only after **all steps above** are completed:

- Voicemail cannot be accessed
- Caller cannot leave voicemail
- Visual voicemail fails after all checks
### **Mandatory Escalation Notes**
- All data collected above
- Results of test call
- Device type & OS version
- Exact failure point
## **Documentation & Closure**
- Document all steps taken
- Confirm customer experience verbally
- Close ticket only after customer confirmation
## **Notes**
- Keep explanations simple and calm
- Avoid technical jargon
- Always aim to complete resolution in L0

---

#### SOP: SMS Not Delivered, Stuck, or Not Received
*Article ID: 46520199049755 | Updated: 2026-02-11*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46520199049755-SOP-SMS-Not-Delivered-Stuck-or-Not-Received*

## **Step 1 ‚Äì Probing & Empathizing with the Customer**
- Acknowledge the customer‚Äôs concern and assure them of assistance.

- Ask when the SMS issue started.

- Confirm whether the issue occurs with all SMS or only specific numbers.

- Request an alternate contact number from the customer.

- Need to check when the port-in was completed, as services may take up to 1 hour to stabilize.

## **Step 2 ‚Äì Tools to Analyze and Handle**

Sl. No.
What to check
Where to check

1
Check for SMS limit is over
[Check Voice, SMS & Data Usage](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/45474788406299)

2
Check for similar outage tickets - Zendesk
[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

**Additional Internal Checks:**

- Review complete ticket history and past conversations.

- Check previous troubleshooting steps already performed (if any).

- Review internal notes in ConnectX (if available).

- Check if similar issues were recently reported in the same area.

- Toggle Airplane Mode ON/OFF.

- Restart the device.

## **Step 3 ‚Äì Troubleshooting Steps to Ask the Customer**
- ¬†Restart the phone to allow a fresh network registration.
- iPhone: Settings ‚Üí Messages ‚Üí Ensure ‚ÄúSend as SMS‚Äù is ON.
([iPhone: Settings ‚Üí App‚ÄìMessages ‚Üí Ensure ‚ÄúSend as SMS‚Äù is ON](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1hGVVCSy_oTuftMWESf5bxt91n3QS9u121HuQLfDdaFc/edit?tab=t.0))

- Android: Settings ‚Üí Apps ‚Üí Messages ‚Üí Ensure ‚ÄúSMS Allow‚Äù.[Android: Settings ‚Üí Apps ‚Üí Permission‚Üí SMS‚ÄìEnsure ‚ÄúSMS Allow‚Äù](https://docs.google.com/document/d/18ctVo4Uph5rP2_2YrokkvVMbNZ0ZvSluqoc89QG6X1Y/edit?tab=t.0)

- Toggle Airplane Mode for 30‚Äì60 seconds.
- Reset Network Settings (this will not erase personal data).
- Allow 30‚Äì120 minutes after activation for full provisioning.
## **Step 4 ‚Äì Providing ETR to the Customer**
- Inform the customer that backend verification may be required.
- Provide an estimated turnaround time (ETR) of 0‚Äì1 hour.
- Assure proactive updates once L1 completes the investigation.
## **Step 5 ‚Äì Escalation to L1 (Zendesk)**
- Ensure all mandatory fields are completed.
- Apply correct primary and secondary tags.
- Set correct ticket priority based on issue impact.
- Add detailed internal escalation notes.
- Attach screenshots and all test results.
- Change ticket status to On-Hold ‚Üí Escalated to L1.
- Transfer the chat to the L1 group, not to a specific L1 agent.
## **Mandatory Details to Provide to L1**
- ICCID / SIM Number ‚Äì*** (From ConnectX)***

- IMEI ‚Äì ***(From ConnectX)***

- Device detail ***(Need to ask from the customer)***

- Device Present Location ***(Need to confirm from the customer)***

- Need to ask the customer for the ZIP code and the live location where the device is currently located.
- Number of signal bars displayed on the device ***(Need to confirm from customer)***

- Screenshot of the error*** (From the Customer)***

- Since when this issue is facing*** (Need to confirm from the customer)***

- If in case other services are fine like data, call etc. ***(Need to confirm from the customer)***

#### Calls keep dropping
*Article ID: 44454839305883 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454839305883-Calls-keep-dropping*

# **Calls Keep Dropping**# **L0 Action ‚ûï**## **Step 1 ‚Äì Probing, Empathizing with the Customer**
- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance
- Ask when the call drops started
- Check if the issue occurs on all calls or specific numbers
- Confirm if the issue is intermittent or continuous
- Confirm whether issue occurs in one location or everywhere
- Check if both outgoing and incoming calls drop
- Ask if the customer travelled or updated the device recently
- Request an alternate contact number
- Capture exact location/pincode and movement history
- Add all customer inputs and findings in ConnectX
## **Step 2 ‚Äì Tools to Analyze and Handle**

Sl. No.
What to check
Where to check

1
Check for barring, suspension, or partial provisioning flags - ConnectX

[Account Suspension](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600508659867-Account-Suspension-ConnectX)

2
Check for similar outage tickets - Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243-Check-Similar-Ongoing-Past-Tickets-Zendesk)

3
Verify real-time network/tower alerts in customer area - Zendesk

[Network Outage Checker - Zendesk](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600050078363-Network-Outage-Checker-Zendesk)

## **Step 3 ‚Äì Troubleshooting Steps (L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099-Troubleshooting-guide)
- Check complete ticket history and past conversations
- Review previous troubleshooting already performed (If any)
- Check internal notes in ConnectX
- Check if similar issues were recently reported in the same area
- Toggle Airplane Mode ON/OFF
- Restart the device
- Confirm VoLTE is enabled:

**iOS (iPhone)**: Go to Settings > Cellular > Cellular Data Options > Voice & Data and ensure VoLTE is ON (or LTE/5G is selected).
- 
**Samsung**: Go to Settings > Connections > Mobile Networks and toggle VoLTE calls to ON.
- 
**Google Pixel**: Go to Settings > Network & internet > SIMs > [Select SIM] and toggle VoLTE to ON.
- 
**OnePlus**: Go to Settings > Mobile Network > [Select SIM] and toggle VoLTE to ON.

- Switch between 5G and 4G manually and retest¬†

**iOS : **Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Voice & Data ‚Üí switch between 5G Auto / LTE
- 
**Samsung : **Settings ‚Üí Connections ‚Üí Mobile Networks ‚Üí Network Mode ‚Üí choose 5G/LTE/Auto or LTE only.
- 
**Pixel / OnePlus : **Settings ‚Üí Network & Internet ‚Üí SIMs ‚Üí Preferred Network Type ‚Üí switch between 5G/LTE.

- Perform manual network selection

**iOS :**Settings ‚Üí Mobile Data ‚Üí Network Selection ‚Üí disable Automatic ‚Üí choose network manually.
- 
**Samsung / Pixel / OnePlus : **Settings ‚Üí Connections / Network & Internet ‚Üí Mobile Networks ‚Üí Network Operators ‚Üí disable auto and select manually.

- Disable any third-party dialer or call recording apps
- Perform outgoing and incoming call tests.
## **Step 4 ‚Äì Providing ETR to Customer**
- Inform the customer that backend verification may be needed
- Provide the ETR of 0-1 hour.
- Assure proactive updates once L1 completes investigation
## **Step 5 ‚Äì Escalating to L1 (Zendesk)**
- Ensure all mandatory fields are filled
- Apply correct primary and secondary tags
- Set correct ticket priority based on issue impact
- Add complete internal escalation notes
- Attach screenshots and all test results
- Change ticket status to On-Hold ‚Üí Escalated to L1
- Ensure we transfer the chat to the L1 group and not to a particular L1 agent.
- Please ensure that session has been ended so that we can ensure that there isn't any confusion later.
## **Mandatory Details to Provide to L1**
- Device model + OS version
- Customer location ( pin code /area)
- Exact time and date issue started
- Call drop pattern (immediate / mid-call / fixed duration)
- Screenshots of signal strength, Volte enabled¬†
- Any error messages shown

#### Network throttling & Fair Usage Policy
*Article ID: 44454798595739 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454798595739-Network-throttling-Fair-Usage-Policy*

# **SOP: Network Throttling & Fair Usage Policy (FUP)**### **L0 Action ‚Äì** Identify whether reduced speed is due to Fair Usage Policy (FUP) or Network throttling and clearly communicate policy impact, reset timeline, and next steps to the customer.## **Step 1 ‚Äì Probing & Empathizing with the Customer**
- Acknowledge the concern and assure support.
- Explain that speed reduction can happen after high usage as part of fair usage policy.
- Confirm with the customer:
Since when the speed has become slow.
- Whether slow speed is on **mobile data, hotspot, or both**.
- Approximate recent data usage (streaming, downloads, gaming, etc.).
- Whether they recently used hotspots extensively.
- Current location and whether the issue is happening everywhere.

- Confirm that calls and SMS are working normally.
## **Step 2 ‚Äì Tools to Analyze & Handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Total Data Consumption - ConnectX

[Check Voice, SMS & Data Usage](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600830296219-Check-Data-Voice-and-SMS-Usage-ConnectX)

2
Total Hotspot Consumption - ConnectX(Confirmation pending from L1)

3
Any abuse or compliance flags on notes - ConnectX

[View Account Notes](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44601230033691-View-Add-Account-Notes-ConnectX)

## **Step 3 ‚Äì Troubleshooting Steps to be Done - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)
- Check complete ticket history and past conversations on **Zendesk (Customer Context)**

- Need to verify the ZIP code
- Check for any Network outages in the area using the Zipcode provided by them. ([***Network Outage in Zendesk***](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1XpWLfgPKLxB3o7IwWoFEevM66CjLgCIi9GNi_5WTyIM/edit?tab=t.0)***)***.
- Check internal notes on the account in [***ConnectX***](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1-rfMRbeoi3NYOiNDXZewcLf3w9Ii5KQv4N7ZCcuhdvg/edit?tab=t.0)

- Verify current plan status is [***Active on ConnectX***](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1JBNN9OYzvlTSYZkwm0uCs1AJR6tw0vQ7yyLYmKG7v_8/edit?tab=t.0)

- Check:
Total monthly data usage.*** Product >> Data/Usage details section (ConnectX).***

- Hotspot usage **(Above/Below 10GB**). (Need to get an update from L1 on how we check this on ConnectX).

- Any active **FUP/Throttle flag** on the account** above/below 50GB**. ***Product >> Data/Usage details section (ConnectX)***

- 
### **Confirm FUP Applicability**

If total data usage **exceeds 50GB** ‚Üí Data speed reduction is valid.
- If hotspot usage **exceeds 10GB** ‚Üí Hotspot speed reduction is valid.

***If usage is below limits but throttle exists ‚Üí Mark for escalation to L1.***

- 
### **Basic Network Refresh**
Guide the customer to:
Turn on Airplane Mode for 30 seconds and turn it off.
- Ensure network mode is set to **4G/5G Auto**.
- Turn off any active VPN.
- Run a speed test on one trusted app.

- 
### **Policy Explanation to Customer**
Clearly explain:
Unlimited data is meant for **personal use only**.
- After crossing **50GB**, speeds may be reduced for the rest of the billing cycle.
- Hotspot usage above **10GB** can also lead to reduced speeds.
- Full speeds will automatically restore at the **start of the next billing cycle**.
- No additional charges apply for high usage.

- ### **Abuse Check**
**If system shows spamming, bulk messaging, or abnormal traffic:**

- Inform the customer that the line is under policy review.
- Do **NOT** promise speed restoration
## **Step 4 ‚Äì Providing the ETR to the Customer**
- If FUP throttling is correctly applied:
Inform that speed will automatically reset at the **next billing cycle**.
- No manual removal is possible at L0.

- If throttle appears incorrect:
Inform backend verification is required.
- Provide standard TAT: **1-2 hours**.
- Assure a proactive update post-investigation

## **Step 5 ‚Äì Escalation to L1 ‚Äì Steps to be Completed on Zendesk**
- Escalate only if:
Usage is **below FUP limit but throttle is active**.
- Throttle **did not reset after the billing cycle**.
- Wrong hotspot usage is recorded.
- Customer disputes abuse flag.

- Before escalating:
Ensure all mandatory fields are filled.
- Set ticket priority based on impact.
- Add complete internal notes along with other mandatory information required:
- Total data usage.
- Hotspot usage.
- Billing cycle dates.
- Throttle flag status.
- Speed test results (if shared).

- Attach screenshots if provided.
- Change ticket status to **On-Hold** if escalated.
### **Details to be Provided to L1 (Confirmed Mandatory):**
- Account/MSISDN
- Current billing cycle dates
- Total data usage (GB)
- Total hotspot usage (GB)
- Throttle flag status (System Applied / Manual / Abuse)
- Date & time speed issue started
- Customer location (Area/Pincode)
- Speed test screenshots (if available)

#### eSIM installed, not activated.
*Article ID: 44454558535067 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454558535067-eSIM-installed-not-activated*

**eSIM Installed, Unable to Activate**

**L0 Action -**

**Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**

- Acknowledge the concern and reassure assistance
- Confirm:
When the eSIM was installed
- Whether activation was ever attempted
- Any error message received during installation/activation (Screenshot).
- If there was any internet interruption during the activation

- Confirm device type:Android / iOS (Make and Model)

- Take an **alternate contact number** from the customer.
**Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Similar Ongoing Tickets

[To Check Similar Ongoing Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

2
eSIM Status

[SOP: e-SIM Status](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600946917019-e-SIM-Status-e-SIM-Replacement-ConnectX)

¬†

**Step 3 - Troubleshooting Steps to be done - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099-Troubleshooting-guide)

- Check complete ticket history and any previous communication in **Zendesk (Customer Context).**

- **Check the Plan is active/pending**
*(Go to Products Tab >check on the SIM details section).*

- Check for **activation backlogs ***(Need to check from L1/L2)¬†*

- Toggle **Airplane Mode ON/OFF**

- **Check APN settings - ‚Äúereseller‚Äù or not¬†**

- 
**IOS **- Go to Settings > Cellular (or Mobile) > Cellular Data Options > Mobile Data Network
- 
**Android **- Go to Settings > Network & internet > SIMs & mobile network > Access Point Names
- Device Specific Checks:
- Check if any **VPN or device management profile** is blocking the network
- 
**Delete and reinstall the eSIM profile** after **sending a new QR code** to them via email from **ConnectX**.

**Step 4 - Providing the ETR to the customer if the issue is still not resolved.**

- Inform the customer that **backend activation verification is required (If New QR is being generated)**

- Provide a **standard ETR of: 0-1 hours.**

- Assure proactive update once activation review is completed.
**Step 5 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be completed on Zendesk -**** (This case should not be escalated, the issue must be resolved after sending a new QR code)**

- Ensure all mandatory fields are completed
- Set correct **Ticket Priority based on impact**

- Add detailed **internal notes (Zendesk)**

- Attach all screenshots and customer confirmations
- Change ticket status to **On-hold if escalated to L1**

¬†
- **Details to be provided to L1: (Confirmed Mandatory)**
- **Device Model + OS Version**
- **Date & Time of eSIM Installation**
- **Activation Attempt Status (Success/Failure/Error)**
- **IMEI, ICCID & Order ID (If Available)**
- 
**Screenshots**
eSIM status page
- Network selection screen
- Error message (if any)

- 
**Exact Error Codes (If Displayed)**

#### Data fluctuating, calls working and network available
*Article ID: 44454513061531 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454513061531-Data-fluctuating-calls-working-and-network-available*

**Data - Fluctuating/ Intermittent**

**L0 Action -**

**Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**

- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance.
- Confirm:
When exactly the issue started
- If they have tried restarting the device. If the threshold is not reached.

- Take an **alternate contact number** from the customer.
- Capture exact **location/pincode and movement history (if travel involved)**

- Add all relevant notes in **Zendesk.** (If required)

**Where to check**

- 
**Access Point Names**

- Switch between 5G/4G manually and re-test
-

- **Toggle Airplane Mode ON/OFF**

-

If data works after performing the troubleshooting steps.
- Ask the customer to perform a **Speed Test** (if data partially connects)
