#### Calls & Data not working
*Article ID: 44454272223643 | Updated: 2026-02-13*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44454272223643-Calls-Data-not-working*

**L0 Action -**

**Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the customer**

- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance
- Confirm if NW signal bars are visible on the device.
- Confirm the following for **Data not working**:
When exactly the issue started - Any particular time in the day¬†
- Whether the issue is continuous or intermittent - experiencing the issuing some room/ place in the house/basement/ any other particular location
- Confirm the ZIP code to ensure that the customer is not facing the issue at any other location than the registered address (like office etc.)

- Confirm the following for **calls not working**:
Is the issues in I/C calls or O/G calls or both
- Whether the issue is continuous or intermittent - experiencing the issuing some room/ place in the house/basement/ any other particular location
- Any particular number(s) the issue is being faced or its across numbers
- Confirm the ZIP code and take any particular location to ensure that the customer is not facing the issue at any other location than the registered address (like office etc.)

- Confirm the following for **SMS not working**:
Is the issues in I/C SMS or O/G SMS or both
- Confirm if any Bank‚Äôs/institution OTP issue - Take Bank‚Äôs/institution details
- SMS IC or OG issues on any particular number.

- Take an **alternate contact number** from the customer
- Add all relevant notes in **Zendesk &** **ConnectX****(Yet to get approval from L1)**

**Step 2 - Tools to analyze and handle**

**What to check**
**Where to check**

1

- 
**Android - **Settings ‚Üí System/General Management ‚Üí Reset ‚Üí Reset Network Settings

Outgoing calls
- Incoming calls
- Mobile data

#### IMEI Blacklisted Check
*Article ID: 46469428612763 | Updated: 2026-02-10*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46469428612763-IMEI-Blacklisted-Check*

**Step 1: Acknowledge & Probe**

- Apologize for the inconvenience and reassure assistance.
- We need to ask the customer for the IMEI number to verify the device¬†
***Step 2: Required Details from customer¬†***

- IMEI number verified
- Email id or Apple¬†
- Error message details
***STEP 3 To Check in ConnectX-***[***How to Check ‚ÄúIMEI Not Qualified‚Äù in ConnectX***](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/46383788927131)

- *Go to Residential Store*
- *Click on Select in Swap IMEI Offer*
- *Enter the IMEI number, and it will show the status as ‚ÄòUnqualified‚Äô along with the reason.*
**Step 4 :Explain clearly to the customer**

- I'm sorry to inform you that after checking the details, I can confirm that your device IMEI is blacklisted. This usually means the device has been reported as lost, stolen, involved in fraud, or blocked due to financial or compliance issues. Because of this, mobile services cannot be activated on the device.I kindly request you to use a different device that is not locked or blacklisted so¬† we can proceed further without any issues.

- **¬†IMEI number verified**
- **Contact Number**
- **Email id or Apple**
- **¬†Error message details**

- *Go to Residential Store*
- *Click on Select in Swap IMEI Offer*
- *Enter the IMEI number, and it will show the status as ‚ÄòUnqualified‚Äô along with the reason.*

#### SOP: Checking Voice, Text & Data Usage on ConnectX
*Article ID: 45474788406299 | Updated: 2026-01-15*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/45474788406299-SOP-Checking-Voice-Text-Data-Usage-on-ConnectX*

## **Purpose**To accurately verify a customer‚Äôs **voice, text (SMS), data, and hotspot usage** using [ConnectX ](https://gather.console.amdocs-dbs.com/customer/696594fa14d9d44a46f0034c/product?sid=696595728829b6717d9bcf0e)before troubleshooting or escalation.

## **When to Use:**
- Customer reports **data not working / slow**

- Usage or limit-related queries
- Hotspot not working concerns
- Before escalating usage-related issues to L1
## **Step-by-Step Process**### **Step 1: Search the Customer**
- Log in to [**ConnectX**](https://gather.console.amdocs-dbs.com/customer/696594fa14d9d44a46f0034c/product?sid=696595728829b6717d9bcf0e)

- Search the customer using:
Registered Name, or
- Email ID / External ID

### **Step 2: Open Product Details**
- Navigate to the **Products** tab
- Select the **Active Plan** linked to the customer‚Äôs line
### **Step 3: Access Usage Details**
- Scroll down to **Usage Details**

- Locate the usage section under the active plan

### **Step 4: Apply Usage Filters**- Use the **checkbox filters** to view required data:

**Usage Type**:
Voice
- Text (SMS)
- Data

- 
**Time Frame**:
Today
- Last 24 hours
- Current billing cycle (as applicable)

### **Step 5: Check Hotspot Usage (If Applicable)**
- Review **Hotspot Usage** from the same Usage Details section
- Confirm whether hotspot data is:
Consumed
- Available
- Restricted

## **Post-Check Actions**
- Document findings in **internal notes on Zendesk.**

- Inform the customer clearly:
Current usage status
- Any visible consumption or limits

- Proceed with troubleshooting or escalation if required
## **Important Notes for L0**
- Usage visibility may lag slightly, inform customers accordingly
- Do **not** assume suspension without confirming usage
- Always add usage screenshots or notes when escalating to L1
## **Do Not**
- Share backend system screenshots with customers
- Modify any plan or usage settings

---

#### Account Suspension - ConnectX

*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600508659867-Account-Suspension-ConnectX*

### **SOP: Account Suspension**
- ### Step 1: Launch the ConnectX application or webpage.
- ### Step 2: Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.
- ### Step 3: Click on the Products tab once the account is open.
### 
- ### Step 4: Select the Plan tab under the Products menu.
- ### Step 5: Navigate to the Product Details section and click on the 3 dots (‚ãÆ) menu icon.
- ### Step 6: Click on Suspension.
- ### Step 7: Click on confirm for sure you want to suspend?
- ### Step 8: Select the Reason for Suspension and add Notes in the section below it.
- ### Step 9: Select the Suspension Date as End of the Cycle (Note: For Lost Device or Scam, select immediate/today's date).

#### Check Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets - Zendesk
*Article ID: 44600232393243 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243-Check-Similar-Ongoing-Past-Tickets-Zendesk*

**To Check Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets**

## **Customer Context****Contains:**

- Customer Email ID
- External Ticket ID
- Timestamp
- Language
- Internal Notes
- Complete Interaction History
**L0 Must:**

- Verify the **registered email ID** before taking any action
- Cross-check the **external ticket ID**

- Review **timestamp** to understand issue timeline
- Communicate in the **customer‚Äôs preferred language (English only)**

- Read **all existing internal notes**

- Review past history to:
Avoid repeating the same questions
- Understand if this is a **repeat issue**

- Ensure continuity in handling

**Mandatory Rule:**
No troubleshooting or escalation should begin **without reviewing Customer Context**.

#### Lost/Stolen Device
*Article ID: 44455497814555 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455497814555-Lost-Stolen-Device*

**SOP: Lost/Stolen Device**

**Scenario**:

Customers report that their device is lost or stolen and needs the line to be suspended to prevent unauthorized use.

**Step 1:** **Probing, Empathizing with the customer**

- Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance
- 
Inform the customer about the consequences of suspension:¬†
Suspending the plan will immediately block calls, SMS, and data usage.¬†
- This helps prevent any unauthorized usage or charges.

- Verify the email ID by sending an OTP
- We will ask if they have an alternative device to re-activate the eSIM. If not, we will suggest suspending the line until they get a new device, as this is a high-risk transaction.
**Step 2: Tools to analyze and handle - ConnectX**

- Launch the ConnectX application or webpage.
- 
Search for the customer account using their Email ID, Phone Number, or Name.

- 
Click on the **Products tab** once the account is open.

- 
Select the Plan tab under the Products menu.

- 
Navigate to the Product Details section and click on the 3 dots (‚ãÆ) menu icon.

- ### ¬†Click on **Suspension**.
- 
### Click on confirm for sure you want to suspend?
### 

- 
Select the Reason for Suspension.

- ¬†Add notes after selecting the reason for suspension.

- ### Select the Suspension Date as End of the Cycle (Note: For Lost Device or Scam, select immediate/today's date).## **Step 3 ‚Äì Communication & Customer Guidance**Inform the customer:

- The plan has been **successfully suspended**.
- No further usage will occur while suspended.
- Billing behavior during suspension (as per policy, if applicable).
- 
Advise the customer to:
Report the theft to local authorities if the device is stolen.
- Secure personal accounts (email, banking, social apps) linked to the device.

- 
Explain next steps:
Plan can be **reactivated** once the customer has a new device.
- A **new eSIM** can be issued if required.
- MSISDN can usually be retained unless otherwise restricted.

---

#### Carrier-Restricted Device
*Article ID: 44455469897243 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455469897243-Carrier-Restricted-Device*

## **SOP: Device Compatibility and Status / Carrier-Restricted Device****Scenario:** Customer cannot activate service because their device is either **not compatible with the network technology (e.g., specific bands)** or is **locked/restricted by a previous carrier**.

### **Step 1 - Probing, Empathizing with the Customer**
- 
**Acknowledge the concern and assure assistance.** (e.g., "I understand this is frustrating. Since your account looks active on our side, let's check your device setup, as that is the most common reason for these messages. I'll guide you through it.")
- 
**Confirm Key Details:**

**Device Model and exact OS Version.** (Crucial for compatibility check).
- 
**Where the device was purchased** (e.g., specific carrier, retailer, unlocked).
- 
**Previous Carrier** (if applicable).
- 
**If the device has ever been used successfully** with another carrier's SIM/eSIM since purchasing it.
- The **exact error message** displayed on the screen (e.g., "SIM Not Supported," "Invalid SIM," "Enter Unlock Code").
- 
**If the customer has confirmed the device is unlocked** with the previous carrier.

- 
**Take an alternate contact number **from the customer.
### **Step 2 - Tools to Analyze and Handle**

**Sl. No.**
**What to check**
**Where to check**

1
Check if the IMEI is blacklisted or flagged for any reason. (Internal Notes on ConnecX)
[View/Add Account Notes](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44601230033691-View-Add-Account-Notes-ConnectX)

2
Check for Similar Issues - Zendesk

[Similar Ongoing/Past Tickets](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)

### **Step 3 - Troubleshooting Steps to be done (Standard L0) - Refer to **[**Troubleshooting Guide**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455761075099)The focus is on isolating the issue to network compatibility or carrier lock.

- **Check complete ticket history and past conversations on Zendesk.**
- 
**Review all previous troubleshooting** already performed.
- **Check internal notes on the account in ConnectX.**
- 
**Confirm system status:** Verify that the service provisioning is **Active** and the eSIM is registered in the system (i.e., the problem is device-specific, not a provisioning failure).*If the eSIM is not registered, the provisioning SOP should be followed first.*

- 
**Verify Device Lock Status (Primary Fix):**

**If the error message is "eSIM Not Supported" or "Carrier Lock":** This is the strongest indicator of a carrier restriction.

**Instruct the customer** that the device appears to be locked to their previous carrier.
- 
**Provide guidance** on the process to contact their previous carrier to request an unlock.

- 
**If the customer *****claims***** it is unlocked:**Ask the customer to **insert a known-working SIM card from a different carrier** (if available) to independently test the unlock status.

- 
**Verify APN Settings (Standard Check):**
If the error is **"No Signal"** and *not* a lock error, guide the customer to check and update the **APN (Access Point Name)** settings to the correct carrier standard.
- Instruct them to manually enter the correct APN - ‚Äú**ereseller**‚Äù.

- 
**Basic Device Checks:**
**Power Cycle:** Instruct the customer to turn the device off, remove/re-insert the physical SIM (if applicable), wait 30 seconds, and turn it back on.

- 
**Device Compatibility Confirmation:**Based on the check in Step 3, clearly inform the customer of the compatibility status:
"Your **[Device Model]** is compatible with our network." (Proceed to Step 5 if lock is still suspected).
- "We have confirmed that your **[Device Model]** **does not support the required [Technology/Band]** needed for service in your area." (Proceed to Step 5).

### **Step 4 - Providing the TAT to Customer & Next Steps**
- 
**If the Device is Identified as Carrier-Locked:**
Inform the customer that **the issue is resolved by the previous carrier**, not our internal team.
- Provide the **exact contact information/process** for the previous carrier's unlocking team.
- 
**Action for the customer:** Obtain the unlock code/confirmation.
- 
**Next step for you:** Mark the ticket as "Resolved - Device Lock," or "Pending Customer Action."

- 
**If the Device is Identified as Incompatible:**
Inform the customer clearly that their device cannot be used on the network.
- 
**Action for the customer:** Obtain a compatible device.
- 
**Offer assistance:** Provide details on purchasing compatible devices (e.g., link to company store).

- 
**If the Device is Compatible, but Lock/Issue Persists (Uncommon):**
Inform the customer that backend verification of the device registration may be required.
- Provide a standard TAT of: **2 - 4 hours** (or as per policy) for L1 to verify the IMEI provisioning status against the network register.
- Assure proactive update once the L1 investigation is completed.

### **Step 5 - Escalating to L1 - Steps to be Completed on Zendesk (If Issue is NOT a Clear Lock/Incompatibility)**
- **Ensure all mandatory fields are filled.**
- **Set correct Ticket Priority**
- 
**Add complete internal escalation notes,** detailing:
The **Confirmed Device Model, OS Version, and Compatibility Status**.
- The **Exact Error Message** seen on the device.
- Results of **APN Check** and **Network Reset**.
- If a **test SIM** from another carrier was used and the result.

- 
**Attach all screenshots** (e.g., system showing active provisioning, or the device error message provided by the customer).
- **Change ticket status to On-Hold if escalated to L1.**
- 
**Details to be provided to L1 (Confirmed Mandatory):**
**Device Model + OS Version.**
- **IMEI Number.**
- 
**Previous Carrier** (if known).
- 
**Result of Compatibility Check** (Internal Tool Confirmation).
- **Exact Error Message.**
- 
**Screenshot of ConnectX** showing **Active Service Provisioning**.

---

#### Locked Device
*Article ID: 44455447219099 | Updated: 2025-12-19*
*URL: https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44455447219099-Locked-Device*

**SOP for Locked Device¬†**

¬†

**Step 1 - Visual Audit (Review & Pre-Requisites)**

**Check complete ticket history and past conversations. (**[**Zendesk**](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600232393243)**)**

- Verify Customer Eligibility:
Confirm the customer's Device Model is officially supported for eSIM.( Check in Compatible List device list)
- 
Ensure the customer's Account Status is Active and in good standing.

¬†

- Crucial Device Lock Confirmation:
If the customer is porting or migrating, ask directly: "Is your device currently locked to your previous carrier, or has the device unlock process been completed?"

¬†

## **Step 2 - Probing & Managing Expectations (Pre-Provisioning)****Acknowledge the request but immediately pivot to addressing the device lock. Do NOT proceed to the next step until the lock is resolved.**

- Educate the Customer:
Explain clearly that the device must be fully unlocked by the previous carrier before our eSIM can be successfully downloaded and installed.
- Use empathic language: "I understand you are eager to switch, but to ensure your new service works without issues, we must first confirm your phone is fully unlocked."

- Provide Clear Next Steps for the Customer:
Instruct the customer on how to check their device's lock status (e.g., using a SIM card from a different carrier).
- Advise them to contact their previous carrier (Name them, if possible) to request or confirm the unlock has been processed through their helpline, chat or email support.
- Crucial Action: Inform the customer to contact us again only after they receive confirmation from their previous carrier that the device is unlocked.
¬†

## **Step 3 - Initiating the eSIM Request :**

**Condition**
**L0 Action in ConnectX/App**
**Next Expected Outcome**

**If Device Status is PENDING UNLOCK**
DO NOT Initiate Provisioning. (No action in ConnectX needed).
The customer contacts the previous carrier and returns to us when the unlock is confirmed.

**If Device Status is CONFIRMED UNLOCKED**
Proceed with standard provisioning¬†
System processes request; QR/link sent to the customer's registered email/phone.

¬†

## **Step 4 - Troubleshooting Specific to Locked Devices**- If the customer reports an installation error code, specifically look for messages related to "SIM Not Supported," "Carrier Lock," or "Cannot Add Data Plan (Carrier Restriction)."
Action: If these errors appear, reiterate Step 2. Provisioning will always fail until the external carrier unlocks the device.
- ConnectX Check: If an eSIM request was mistakenly initiated (Step 3B), check Interactions >> Communication log. ¬†- Refer to How to [Check interactions on ConnectX](https://rockstarautomations.zendesk.com/hc/en-us/articles/44600611412123-Check-Interactions-ConnectX).

**Step 5 - Documentation and Resolution**

- Ticket Documentation:Document the date and time the customer was informed that the device must be unlocked.

- Resolution:Do not escalate to L1. The issue is external (the locking carrier), not internal.

## **Step 6 - Escalation Check****Escalate ONLY if: **The customer confirms the previous carrier completed the unlock, and a new provisioning attempt fails with an internal system error NOT related to carrier restrictions.

**Details to be provided upon Re-Engaging and Successful Provisioning Failure:**

- Customer Account Number/ID.
- Clear Confirmation: "The customer has confirmed with [Previous Carrier Name] that the device is unlocked."
- Time & Date of the failed eSIM Request Attempt *after* unlock confirmation.
- ConnectX Provisioning Status (showing "Failed to Provision").
- Error Codes or System Messages (If any).

Incident Type
Severity
Description

Emergency Incident
Severity 1 (S1)
Used when either a business capability is completely unavailable or severely restricted and the effects are directly observable by subscribers due to an unplanned event.
Maintained program elements performing real time processing or if a defect can result in unrecoverable loss of revenue.
Business critical functionality affects more than 5% of subscribers.

Critical Incident
Severity 2 (S2)
Used when either a business capability is completely unavailable or severely restricted and the effects are directly observable by subscribers due to an unplanned event.
Business critical functionality affects up to 5% of subscribers.

Major Incident
Severity 3 (S3)
Used when a business capability is impaired, but the effects are not business impacting as they affect fewer than 10 Customer employees.
For Customer employee impacting events, it is limited to events that impact more than 10 Customer employees but less than 25% of CSRs from being impacted by a degradation of network, system or application that is not required to directly support subscribers.

Minor Incident
Severity 4 (S4)
Incidents that impact a single individual and do not require immediate resolution.
